 PB  oṃ mahan me voco bhargo me voco yaśo me vocaḥ stomaṃ me voco bhuktiṃ me vocaḥ sarvaṃ me vocas tan māvatu tan māviśatu tena bhukṣiṣīya 
PB  devo devam etu somaḥ somam etv ṛtasya pathā
PB  vihāya dauṣkṛtyam
PB  badvā nāmasi sṛtiḥ somasaraṇī somaṃ gameyam
PB  pitaro bhūḥ pitaro bhūḥ pitaro bhūḥ
PB  nṛmaṇa ūrdhvabharasaṃ tvordhvabharā dṛśeyam
PB  mṛdā śithirā devānāṃ tīrthaṃ vedir asi mā mā hiṃsīḥ
PB  viṣṇoḥ śiro 'si yaśodhā yaśo mayi dhehi
PB  iṣa ūrja āyuṣe varcase ca
PB  yunajmi te pṛthivīm agninā saha yunajmi vācaṃ saha sūryeṇa yukto vāto 'ntarikṣeṇa te saha yuktās tisro vimṛjaḥ sūryasya
PB  ṛtasya sadane sīdāmi
PB  ṛtapātram asi
 PB  vānaspatyo 'si bārhaspatyo 'si prājāpatyo 'si prajāpater mūrdhāsy atyāyupātram asīdam ahaṃ māṃ prāñcaṃ prohāmi tejase brahmavarcasāya 
PB  maruto napāto 'pāṅkṣayāḥ parvatānāṅkakubhaḥ śyenā ajirā endraṃ vagnunā vahata ghoṣeṇāmīvāṃ cātayadhvaṃ yuktāstha vahata
PB  idam aham amuṃ yajamānaṃ paśuṣv adhy ūhāmi paśuṣu ca māṃ brahmavarcase ca
 PB  vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa chandasā saṃ mṛjantu rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena chandasā saṃ mṛjantv ādityās tvā jāgatena chandasā saṃ mṛjantu 
 PB  pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspate prabhur gātrāṇi pary eṣi viśvato 'taptatanūr na tad āmo aśnute śṛtāsa id vahantaḥ saṃ tad āśataḥ 
PB  praśukraitu devīmanīṣāsmad rathaḥ sutaṣṭo na vājy āyuṣe me pacasva varcase
me pavasva viduḥ pṛthivyā divo janitrāc chṛṇvantv āpo 'dhaḥ kṣarantīḥ somehodgāya
mām āyuṣe mama brahmavarcasāya yajamānasyarddhyā amuṣya rājyāya
PB  vekurānāmāsi juṣṭā devebhyo namo vāce namo vācas pataye devi vāg yat te vāco madhumat tasmin mā dhāḥ sarasvatyai svāhā
PB  sūryo mā divyābhyo nāṣṭrābhyaḥ pātu vāyur antarikṣābhyo 'gniḥ pārthivābhyaḥ svāhā
PB  yo 'dya saumyo vadho 'ghāyūnām udīrate viṣūkuhasya dhanvanāpa tān varuṇo 'pa dhamatu
PB  yo ma ātmā yā me prajā ye me paśavas tair ahaṃ mano vācaṃ pra sīdāmi
PB  agnes tejasendrasyendriyeṇa sūryasya varcasā bṛhaspatis tvā yunaktu devebhyaḥ
prāṇāyāgnir yunaktu tapasā somaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu
PB  annaṃ kariṣyāmy annaṃ praviṣyāmy annaṃ janayiṣyāmi
PB  annam akaram annam abhūd annam ajījanam
 PB  śyeno 'si gāyatracchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃ pārayā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam 
PB  saṃ varcasā payasā saṃ tapobhir aganmahi manasā saṃ śivena saṃ vijñānena
manasaś ca satyair yathā vo 'haṃ cārutamaṃ vadānīndro vo dṛśe bhūyāsaṃ sūryaś cakṣuṣe
vātaḥ prāṇāya somo gandhāya brahma kṣatrāya
PB  namo gandharvāya viṣvag vādine varcodhā asi varco mayi dhehi
PB  adhvanām adhvapate svasti me 'dyāsmin devayāne pathi bhūyāt
PB  samrāḍ asi kṛśānuḥ
PB  tutho 'si janadhāyo nabho 'si pratakvāsaṃmṛṣṭo 'si havyasūdanaḥ
PB  vibur asi pravāhaṇaḥ
PB  vahnir asi havyavāhanaḥ
PB  śvātro 'si pracetāḥ
PB  tutho 'si viśvavedā uśig asi kavir aṅghārir asi bambhārir avasyur asi duvasvān
PB  śundhyur asi mārjālīyaḥ
PB  ṛtadhāmāsi svarjyotiḥ
PB  samudro 'si viśvavyacāḥ
PB  ahir asi budhnyaḥ
PB  ajo 'sy ekapāt
PB  sagarā asi budhnyaḥ
PB  kavyo 'si kavyavāhanaḥ
PB  pāta māgnayo raudreṇānīkena piṣṭata mā namo vo 'stu mā mā hiṃsiṣṭa
PB  ṛtasya dvārau stho mā mā saṃ tāptam
PB  namaḥ sakhibhyaḥ pūrvasadbhyo namo parasadbhyaḥ
PB  śyeno nṛcakṣā agneṣ ṭvā cakṣuṣāva paśyāmi
PB  indav indrapītasya ta indriyāvato gāyatracchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
PB  ūrdhvaḥ sapta ṛṣīn upa tiṣṭhasvendrapīto vācas pate saptartvijo 'bhyuc chrayasva juṣasva lokam mārvāg ava gāḥ
PB  soma rārandhi no hṛdi pitā no 'si mama tan mā mā hiṃsīḥ
PB  soma gīrbhiṣ ṭvā vayaṃ vardhayāmo vācovidaḥ sumṛḍīko na ā viśa
PB  ā pyāyasva sam etu te viśvataḥ soma vṛṣṇyam 
bhavā vājasya saṃgathe
 PB  avamais ta ūrdhvais te kāvyais te pitṛbhir bhakṣitasya madhumato nārāśaṃsasya sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi 
PB  dīkṣāyai varṇena tapaso rūpeṇa manaso mahimnā vāco vibhūtyā prajāpatis tvā yunaktu prajābhyo 'pānāya
PB  vāyur yunaktu manasā stomaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu
 PB  vṛṣako 'si triṣṭupchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃ pārayā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam 
PB  indav indrapītasya ta indriyāvato triṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
PB  sūryo yunaktu vācā stomaṃ yajñāya voḍhave dadhātv indra indriyaṃ satyāḥ kāmā yajamānasya santu
 PB  svaro 'si gayo 'si jagacchandā anu tvā rabhe svasti mā saṃ pārayā mā stotrasya stotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām 
PB  indav indrapītasya ta indriyāvato triṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
PB  āyur me prāṇo mano 'si me prāṇa āyupatnyām ṛci yan me mano yamaṃ gataṃ yad vā me aparāgataṃ rājñā somena tad vayaṃ punar asmāsu
PB  yan me yamaṃ vaivasvataṃ mano jagāma dūragās tan ma āvartayā punar jīvātave na martave 'tho ariṣṭatātaye
PB  yenāhy ājim ajayad vicakṣya yena śyenaṃ śakunaṃ suparṇaṃ yad āhuś cakṣur aditāv anantaṃ somo nṛcakṣā mayi tad dadhātu
 PB  aindraṃ saho 'sarji tasya ta indav indrapītasyendriyāvato 'nuṣṭupchandaso harivataḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi 
PB  indav indrapītasya ta indriyāvato 'nuṣṭupchandasaḥ sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
PB  stutasya stutam asy ūrjasvat payasvad ā mā stotrasya strotraṃ gamyād indravanto vanemahi bhakṣīmahi prajām iṣam
PB  iṣṭayajuṣas te deva soma stutastomasya śastokthasya tirohnyasya yo 'śvasanir gosanir bhakṣas tasyopahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
PB  ṛtasya tvā deva stomapade viṣṇor dhāmāni vi muñcāmy etat tvaṃ deva stomān avakaram agann aśīmahi vayaṃ pratiṣṭhām
PB  somehānu mehi soma saha sadasa indriyeṇa
PB  subhūr asi śreṣṭho raśmir devānāṃ saṃsad devānāṃ yātur yayā tanvā brahma jinvasi tayā mā jinva tayā mā janaya prakāśaṃ mā kuru
PB  apāṃ puṣpam asy oṣadhīnāṃ rasa indrasya priyatamaṃ haviḥ svāhā
PB  hāriyojanasya te deva someṣṭayajuṣaḥ stutastomasya śastokthasya yo 'śvasanir gosanir bhakṣas tasyopahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
PB  devakṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi pitṛkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi manuṣyakṛtasyainaso
'vayajanam asy asmatkṛtasyainaso 'vayajanam asi yad divā ca naktaṃ cainaś cakṛma
tasyāvayajanam asi yat svapantaś ca jāgrataś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asi yad
vidvāṃsaś cāvidvāṃsaś cainaś cakṛma tasyāvayajanam asy enasaenasāvayajanam asi
PB  apsu ghautasya te deva soma nṛbhiḥ sutasya
PB  madhumantaṃ bhakṣaṃ karomi
PB  sam adbhya oṣadhībhyaḥ
PB  kāmakāmaṃ ma ā vartaya
PB  ūrg asy ūrjam mayi dhehi
PB  prāṇa somapīthe me jāgṛhi
PB  dadhikrāvṇo akāriṣaṃ jiṣṇor aśvasya vājinaḥ 
surabhi no mukhā karat pra na āyūṃṣi tāriṣat
PB  aśvo 'sy atyo 'si mayo 'si hayo 'si vājy asi saptir arvāg si vṛṣāsi
PB  ādityānāṃ patmānv ihi namas te 'stu mā mā hiṃsīḥ
PB  vāyoṣ ṭvā tejasā prati gṛhṇāmi nakṣatrāṇāṃ tvāṃ rūpeṇa prati gṛhṇāmi sūryasya tvā varcasā prati gṛhṇāmi
PB  rathantaram asi vāmadevyam asi bṛhad asi
PB  aṅkānyaṅkū abhito rathaṃ yau dhvāntaṃ vātāgram abhisaṃcaratau dūre hetir indriyavān patatrī te no 'gnayaḥ paprayaḥ pārayantu
PB  vaiśvānaraḥ pratnathā nākam ā ruha divaḥ pṛṣṭhe mandamānaḥ sumanmabhiḥ sapūrvavaj jantave dhanāḥ samānam ayman pary eti jāgṛviḥ
PB  gidaiṣa te ratha eṣa vām aśvinā ratho 'riṣṭo viśvabheṣajaḥ
PB  kṛśāno savyān ā yaccha
PB  dāsāno dakṣiṇān ava gṛhāṇa
PB  devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ prati gṛhṇāmi
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe varuṇāyāśvaṃ tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe rudrāya gāṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe 'gnaye 'jam
PB  agnaye hiraṇyam
PB  agnīṣomābhyām ajān mayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  annasyānnapatiḥ prādād anamīvasya śuṣmiṇo namo viśvajanasya kṣāmāya bhuñjati mā mā hiṃsīḥ
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe tvaṣṭre 'viṃ tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  gnās tvā 'kṛntann apaso 'tanvata vayitryo 'vayan
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe bṛhaspataye vāsas tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigṛhītre
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe uttānāyāṅgirasāyāprāṇat tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe pūṣṇa uṣṭram
PB  vāyave mṛgaṃ tenāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  jāpataye hastinaṃ prajāpataye varāhaṃ prajāpataye vrīhiyavāṃs tair amṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe kṣetrapataye tilamāṣās tair amṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  varuṇas tvā nayatu devi dakṣiṇe savitre 'śvataraṃ vāśvatarīṃ vā tayāmṛtatvam aśīya vayo dātre bhūyān mayo mahyaṃ pratigrahītre
PB  ka idaṃ kasmā adāt kāmaḥ kāmāyādāt kāmo dātā kāmaḥ pratigrahītā kāmaḥ samudram āviśat kāmena tvā prati gṛhṇāmi kāmaitat te
PB  raśmir asi kṣayāya tvā kṣayaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  pretir asi dharmaṇe tvā dharmaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  anvitir asi dive tvā divaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  saṃdhir asy antarikṣāya tvāntarikṣaṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  pratidhir asi pṛthivyai tvā pṛthivīṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  viṣṭambho 'si vṛṣṭyai tvā vṛṣṭiṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  prāco 'sy ahne tvāhar jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  anvāsi rātryai rātriṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  uśig asi vasubhyas tvā vasūn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  praketo 'si rudrebhyas tvā rudrān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  sudītir asy ādityebhyas tvādityān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  ojo 'si pitṛbhyas tvā pitṝn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  tantur asi prajābhyas tvā prajā jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  rodasy asy oṣadhībhyas tvauṣadhīr jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  pṛtanāṣāḍ asi paśubhyas tvā paśūn jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  abhijid asi yuktagrāvendrāya tvendraṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  adhipatir asi prāṇāya tvā prāṇān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  dharuṇo 'sy apānāya tvāpānān jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  saṃsarpo 'si cakṣuṣe tvā cakṣur jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  vayodhā asi kṣetrāya tvā kṣetraṃ jinva savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
PB  trivṛd asi trivṛte tvā savṛd asi savṛte tvā pravṛd asi pravṛte tvānuvṛd asy anuvṛte tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
 PB  niroho 'si nirohāya tvā saṃroho 'si saṃrohāya tvā praroho 'si prarohāya tvānuroho 'sy anurohāya tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye 
PB  vasuko 'si vasyaṣṭir asi veṣaśrīr asi savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye stuta
 PB  ākramo 'sy ākramāya tvā saṃkramo 'si saṃkramāya tvotkramo 'sy utkramāya tvotkrāntir asy utkrāntyai tvā savitṛprasūtā bṛhaspataye 
PB  tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa prathamayā tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa madhyamayā tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa uttamayodyatī trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ
PB  jyeṣṭho jyaiṣṭhineya stuvīta
PB  agrād agraṃ rohaty abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
PB  pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtir vipāpmanā vartate ya etayā stute nāvagato 'pa rudhyate nāparuddho 'va gacchati 
na śreyāṃsaṃ pāpīyān abhyā rohati na janatā janatām abhy eti nānyo 'nyasya prajā ā dadate yathākṣetraṃ kalpante 
avarṣukas tu parjanyo bhavatīme hi lokās tṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa vy eti
PB  eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ prati tiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
PB  tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhiḥ parivartinī triviṣṭutiḥ
PB  praparīvartam āpnoti ya etayā stute saṃtatā viṣṭutiḥ prāṇo 'pāno vyānas ta ṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa saṃ tanoti 
sarvam āyur eti na purāyuṣaḥ pra mīyate ya etayā stute varṣukaḥ parjanyo bhavatīme hi lokās tṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa saṃ dadhāti
PB  ślakṣṇeva tu vā īśvarā paśūn nirmṛjaḥ saiṣā ca parācota śreyān bhavaty uta yādṛṅ eva tādṛṅ net tu pāpīyān
PB  tām etāṃ bhāllavaya upāsate tasmāt te pratigṛṇantaḥ parīvartān na cyavante
PB  tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhis tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti yā madhyamā sā prathamā
yottamā sā madhyamā yā prathamā sottamā tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti yottamā sā prathamā yā
prathamā sā madhyamā yā madhyamā sottamā kulāyinī trivṛto viṣṭutiḥ
PB  prajākāmo vā paśukāmo vā stuvīta vai kulānāyapaśavaḥ kulāyaṃkulāyam eva bhavati
PB  etām evānujāvarāya kuryād etāsām evāgraṃ pariyatīnāṃ prajānām agraṃ pary eti
PB  etām eva bahubhyo yajamānebhyaḥ kuryāt yat sarvā agriyā bhavanti sarvā
madhye sarvā uttamāḥ sarvān evainān samāvadbhājaḥ karoti nānyo 'nyam apa ghnate sarve
samāvadindriyā bhavanti
PB  varṣukaḥ parjanyo bhavatīme hi lokās tṛcas tān hiṅkāreṇa vyati ṣajati
PB  pāpavasīyasaṃ tu bhavati
 PB  adharottaram apāvagato rudhyateva gacchaty aparuddhaḥ pāpīyān śreyāṃsam abhyā rohati janatā janatām abhy ety anyo 'nyasya prajā  
ā dadate na yathākṣetraṃ kalpante 
PB  pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
pañcapañcinī pañcapañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ
PB  pāṅktaḥ puruṣaḥ pāṅktāt paśavas tayā puruṣaṃ ca paśūṃś cāpnoti vajro vai
pancapaśo yat pañcapañca vyūhati vajram eva tad vy ūhati śāntyā eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā
pañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ prati tiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
 PB  pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhiḥ saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhis 
PB  trīn stomān prativihitā brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta
PB  pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ tisṛbhis trivṛtaṃ saptabhiḥ saptadaśam
PB  vīryaṃ vai stomā vīryam eva tad ekadhā samūhate brahmavarcasyāvaruddhyai tejasvī brahmavarcasī bhavati ya etayā stute
 PB  tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhiḥ pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa  
tisṛbhir udyatī pañcadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ 
PB  etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃl lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
PB  pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir
daśasaptā saptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ
PB  etayā vai devā asurān aty akrāmann ati pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ krāmati ya etayā stute
PB  abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāmantyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
PB  garbhiṇī viṣṭutiḥ pa prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya etayā stute
PB  viḍ vai saptadaśas tasyā rājā garbho viśa eva tad rājānaṃ garbhaṃ karoti
PB  nāvagato 'pa rudhyate nāparuddho 'va gacchati
 PB  annaṃ vai saptadaśo yat sapta madhye bhavanti pañcapañcābhito 'nnam eva tan madhyato dhīyate 'naśanāyuko yajamāno bhavaty anaśanāyukāḥ 
PB  vairājo vai puruṣaḥ sapta grāmyāḥ paśavo yad daśapūrvā bhavanti saptottamā yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu prati ṣṭhāpayati
PB  eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā saptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ prati tiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
PB  eṣa eva vyūhaḥ saptaikamadhyā
PB  brahmaṇo vā āyatanaṃ prathamā kṣatrasya madhyamā viśa uttamā yat prathamā
bhūyiṣṭhā bhājayati brahmaṇy eva tad ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti brahmaṇa eva tat kṣatraṃ
ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti kṣatrasyāsya prakāśo bhavati ya etayā stute
PB  tām etāṃ trikharvā upāsate tasmāt te spardhamānā na vlīyante
 PB  saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti parācībhiḥ saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa  
tisṛbhiḥ saptāsthitā 
PB  bhrātṛvyaṃ stuvīta yathā saptāsthitena matyena samī karoty evaṃ pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ pra rujati
PB  etām eva bahubhyo yajamānebhyaḥ kuryād yaḥ prathamo hiṅkāraḥ sa prathamāyā
yattāṃ saptabhyo hiṅ karoti tena sā sapta bhajate yat saptaiva madhye sapadyante
tena sā sapta bhajate ya uttamo hiṅkāraḥ sa uttamayā yattāṃ saptabhyo hiṅ karoti
tena sā sapta bhajate sarvān evainān samāvadbhājaḥ karoti nānyo 'nyam apa ghnate
samāvadindriyā bhavanti
PB  tām etām abhipratāriṇa upāsate tasmāt ta ojiṣṭhāsvānām
PB  eṣa eva vyūha ubhayaḥ saptaikamadhyā nirmadhyā
 PB  ānujāvara stuvītāloko vā eṣa yad ānujāvaro yat saptaprathamāḥ saptottamās tisro madhye tryakṣaraḥ puruṣo lokam evāsmai tan madhyataḥ  
karoti tasmiṃl loke prati tiṣṭhati 
 PB  etām eva prajākāmāya kuryān madhyato vā eṣa saṃrūḍho yaḥ prajāṃ na vindate lokam evāsmai taṃ madhyataḥ karoti taṃ lokaṃ prajayā  
ca paśubhiś cānu pra jāyate 
 PB  etām evāparuddharājanyāya kuryād viḍ vai saptadaśas tasyā rājā garbho viśa eva tad rājānaṃ nir hanty apāvagato 'pa rudhyate 'va  
gacchaty aparuddhaḥ 
PB  etām evābhicaryamāṇāya kuryāt prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim eva madhyattaḥ pra viśanty astṛtyai
 PB  pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhir navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ  
sa tisṛbhiḥ 
PB  caturastomān prativihitā brahmavarcasakāmāḥ stuvīta pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ
tisṛbhis trivṛtaṃ navabhis triṇavaṃ svayaṃ saptadaśaḥ sampanno vīryaṃ vai stomā vīryam
eva tad ekadhā samūhate brahmavarcasyāvaruddhyai tejasvī brahmavarcasī bhavati ya etayā stute
 PB  tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhiḥ pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ  
sa tisṛbhir udyatīsaptadaśasya viṣṭutiḥ 
PB  etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya
samaṣṭyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'bhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena
hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
PB  saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa ekayā sa tisṛbhir bhastrāvācīnabilā
PB  yaṃ dviṣyāt tasya kuryād yathāvācīnabilayā bhastrayā pradhūnuyād evaṃ
yajamānasya paśūn pradhūnoty apakrāmantī viṣṭutis tayā yajamānasya paśavo 'pakrāmanti
pāpīyān bhavati ya etayā stute
PB  saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṅ karoti
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
saptasaptiny ekaviṃśasya viṣsṭutiḥ
PB  sapta grāmyāḥ paśavas tān etayā spṛṇoti sapta śirasi prāṇāḥ prāṇā indriyāṇīndriyāṇy evaitayāpnoti
PB  eṣā vai pratiṣthitaikaviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
PB  pañcabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṅ karoti
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir
udyaty ekaviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ
PB  etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya
samaṣṭyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'bhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena
hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
PB  saiṣā trivṛt prāyaṇā trivṛd udayanā yat trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati
navaitā ekaviṃśasyottamā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān eva tad ubhayato dadhāti
tasmād ayam ardhabhāgavāk 
prāṇa uttareṣāṃ prāṇānāṃ sarvam āyur eti na purāyuṣaḥ pramīyate ya etayā stute
PB  tām etāṃ kradviṣa upāsate tasmāt te sarvam āyur yanti
PB  navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ pañcabhyo hiṅ
karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa
tisṛbhiḥ pratiṣṭutiḥ
PB  navabhis trivṛtaṃ pratiṣṭauti pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcadaśaṃ saptabhiḥ saptadaśaṃ svayam ekaviṃśaḥ saṃpannaḥ
PB  sa eva stomā yajñaṃ vahanti tān uttame stotre saṃtarpayati yathānaḍuho
vāśvān vāśvatarān vohuṣaḥ saṃtarpayed evam etad uttame stotre stomān saṃtarpayati
tṛpyati prajayā paśubhir ya etayā stute
PB  etām eva purodhākāmāya kuryād brahma vai trivṛt kṣatram ekaviṃśo yat
trivṛtaikaviṃśaṃ pratipadyate brahma tat kṣatrasya purastān nidadhāti gacchati purodhāṃ
na purodhāyāś cyavate ya etayā stute
PB  tām etāṃ prāvāhaṇya upāsate tasmāt te purodhāyā na cyavanta
 PB  navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhis tisṛbhyo hiṅ karoti sa parācībhir navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ  
sa tisṛbhiḥ sūrmy ubhayata ādīptā 
PB  brahmavarcasakāmaḥ stuvīta tejo vai trivṛt tryakṣaraḥ puruṣo yat trivṛtāv
abhito bhavatas tisro madhye yathā hi hiraṇyaṃ niṣṭaped evam enaṃ trivṛtau niṣṭapatas
tejase brahmavarcasāya
PB  apaśavy eva tu vā īśvarā paśūn nirdahaḥ kilāsattvān nūbhayamati hi niṣṭapataḥ
PB  etām evābhiśasyamānāya kuryāc chamalaṃ vā etam ṛcchati yam aślīlā vāg
ṛcchati yaivainam asāv aślīlaṃ vāg vadati tām asya trivṛtau niṣṭapatas tejasvī bhavati ya etayā stute
 PB  navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa ekayā navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir navabhyo hiṅ karoti  
sa pañcabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ 
PB  vajro vai triṇavo vajram eva tad vyūhati śāntyai
PB  pañcabhir vihitaikā paricarā pāṅktāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yat pañcabhir
vidadhāty ekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā
triṇavasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
PB  saptabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā
sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir
udyatī triṇavasya viṣṭutiḥ
PB  etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya
samaṣṭyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'bhikrāmantī viṣṭutir abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena
hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
 PB  ekādaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa saptabhiḥ sa ekayaikādaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa saptabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṅ  
karoti sa saptabhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ 
PB  anto vai trayastriṃśaḥ paramo vai trayastriṃśa stomānāṃ saptabhir vihitaikā
paricarā sapta grāmyāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yat saptabhir vidadhāty ekā paricarā
bhavati yajamānam eva tad antataḥ paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā trayastriṃśasya
viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
PB  ekādaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhir ekādaśabhyo
hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa pañcabhiḥ
sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir nedīyaḥsaṃkramā
 PB  anto vai trayastriṃśo yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmaty evam etan nedīyaḥsaṃkramayā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmati 
PB  pañcabhir vihitās tisraḥ paricarāḥ pāṅktāḥ paśava etāvān puruṣo yadātmā
prajā jāyā yat pañcabhir vidadhāti tisraḥ paricarā bhavanti yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu
pratiṣṭhāpayati paśumān bhavati ya etayā stute
PB  navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa ekayaikādaśabhyo hiṅ karoti
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa saptabhis trayodaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa saptabhiḥ sa tisṛbhir
udyatī trayastriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ
PB  etayā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargakāmaḥ stuvīta svargasya lokasya
samaṣṭyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvāno 'grād agraṃ rohaty abhikrāmantī viṣṭutir
abhikrāntyā evābhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti tasmād etayā stotavyam ṛddhyā eva
PB  trayodaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo
hiṅ karoti sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir navabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa
tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ pratyavarohiṇītrayastriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ
PB  yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā śākhāyāḥ śākhām ālambham upāvarohed evam etayemaṃ lokam upāvarohati pratiṣṭhityai
 PB  trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti sarvam āyur eti na purāyuṣaḥ pramīyate ya etayā stute 
PB  tām etāṃ karadviṣa upāsate tasmāt te sarvam āyur yanti
 PB  pañcadaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa pañcabhir ekādaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa pañcabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ saptabhyo hiṅ karoti  
sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ 
PB  yo vai trayastriṃśam ekaviṃśe pratiṣṭhitaṃ veda pratitiṣṭhati pratiṣṭhā
vā ekaviṃśaḥ stomānāṃ yad etāḥ sapta trayastriṃśasyottamā bhavanti saptavidhaikaviṃśasya
viṣṭutir ekaviṃśa eva tat trayastriṃśaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
 PB  aṣṭābhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa catasṛbhiḥ sa ekayāṣṭābhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa catasṛbhir aṣṭābhyo hiṅ karoti  
sa catasṛbhiḥ sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ 
PB  paśavo vai chandogā yad aṣṭābhyo'ṣṭābhyo hiṅ karoti aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti
PB  catasṛbhir vihitaikā paricarā catuṣpādāḥ paśavo yajamānaḥ paricarā yac
catasṛbhir vidadhāty ekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tat paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā caturviṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
PB  pañcadaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā caturdaśabhyo
hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ pañcadaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekādaśabhiḥ
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
PB  brahmaṇo vā āyatanaṃ prathamā kṣatrasya madhyamā viśa uttamā yat pañcadaśinyau
pūrve bhavataś caturdaśottamā brahmaṇi caiva tat kṣatre caujo vīryaṃ dadhāti brahmaṇe
caiva tat kṣatrāya ca viśam anugāṃ karoti kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati ya etayā stute
PB  astomā vā ete yac chandogā ayujo hi stomā yugmanti chandāṃsi yad eṣā yujinī catuścatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutis tenāstomāḥ
PB  eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā catuścatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhait ya etayā stute
PB  caturdaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ sa ekayā pañcadaśabhyo
hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ pañcadaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa ekādaśabhiḥ
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhir nirmadhyā
 PB  astīva vā ayaṃ loko 'stīvāsau chidram ivedam antarikṣaṃ yad eṣā nirmadhyā bhavatīmān eva lokān anu prajāyate pra prajayā pra paśubhir  
jāyate ya etayā stute 
PB  pañcadaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ sa ekayā pañcadaśabhyo
hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa ekādaśabhiḥ caturdaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa daśabhiḥ
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
PB  ājyānāṃ prathamā pṛṣṭhānāṃ dvitīyokthānāṃ tṛtīyā
PB  yājyānāṃ sā hotur yā pṛṣṭhānāṃ sā maitrāvaruṇasya yokthānāṃ sā brāhmaṇācchaṃsino
yaiva hotuḥ sācchāvākasya yā pṛṣṭhānāṃ sahotur yokthānāṃ sā maitrāvaruṇasya yājyānāṃ
sā brāhmaṇācchaṃsino yaiva hotuḥ sācchāvākasya yokthānāṃ sā hotur yājyānāṃ sā maitrāvaruṇasya
yā pṛṣṭhānāṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsino yaiva hotuḥ sācchāvākasya sarvā ājyeṣu sarvāḥ pṛṣtheṣu sarvā uktheṣu
 PB  paśavo vai samīṣantī yad eṣā sarvāṇi savanāny anusaṃcaraty anusavanam evainaṃ paśubhiḥ samardhayati paśuman bhavati ya etayā stute 
PB  ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa dvadaśabhiḥ sa ekayā ṣoḍaśabhyo
hiṅ karoti sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ sa dvādaśabhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa dvādaśabhiḥ
sa ekayā sa tisṛbhiḥ
PB  anto vā aṣṭācatvāriṃśaḥ paśavaś chandogā yat ṣoḍaśabhyaḥṣoḍaśabhyo hiṅ karoti ṣoḍaśakalāḥ paśavaḥ kalāśas tat paśūn āpnoti
PB  dvādaśabhir vihitaikā paricarā dvādaśamāsās saṃvvatsaro yajamānaḥ paricarā
yad dvādaśabhir vidadhāty ekā paricarā bhavati yajamānam eva tad antatas saṃvvatsare
paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayaty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitāṣṭācatvāriṃśasya viṣṭutiḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya etayā stute
PB  ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo
hiṅ karoti sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhiḥ sa daśabhiḥ ṣoḍaśabhyo hiṅ karoti sa daśabhiḥ
sa tisṛbhiḥ sa tisṛbhir nedīyaḥsaṃkramā
 PB  anto vā aṣṭācatvāriṃśo yathā mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ sṛptvā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmaty evam etan nedīyaḥsaṃkramayā nedīyaḥsaṃkramāt saṃkrāmati 
PB  daśabhir vihitā tisraḥ paricarā daśākṣarā virāḍ etāvān puruṣo yad ātmā
prajā jāyā yad daśabhir vidadhātt tisraḥ paricarā bhavanti yajamānam eva tad virājy
annādye 'ntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayaty annādo bhavati ya etayā stute
PB  gāvo vā etat sattram āsata tāsāṃ daśasu māssu śṛṅgaṇy ajāyanta tā abruvannarāḥ smottiṣṭhāmopaśā no 'jñateti tā udatiṣṭhan
PB  tāsāṃ tv evābruvann āsāmahā evemau dvādaśau māsau saṃsaṃvvatsaram āpayāmeti
tāsāṃ dvādaśasu māḥsu śṛṅgāṇi prāvartanta tāḥ sarvam annādyam āpnuvaṃs tā etās tūparās
tasmāt tāḥ sarvān dvādaśamāsaḥ prerate sarvaṃ hi tā annādyam āpnuvan
PB  sarvam annādyam āpnoti ya evaṃv veda
PB  prajāpatir vā idam eka āsīt so 'kāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa etam atirātram apaśyat tam āharat tenāhorātre prājanayat
 PB  yad eṣo 'tirātro bhavaty ahorātre eva prajanayanty ahorātrayoḥ pratitiṣṭhanty etāvān vāva saṃvvatsaro yad ahas ca rātriś cāhorātrābhyām  
eva tat saṃvvatsaram āpnuvanti 
PB  yaj jyotiṣṭomo bhavati yajñamukhaṃ tad ṛdhnuvanti yad uktho yajñakrator anantarayāya yad rātriḥ sarvasyāptyai
PB  sa etān stomān apaśyat jyotir gaur aur itīme vai lokā ete stomā ayam eva jyotir ayaṃ madhyamo gaur asāv uttama āyuḥ
PB  yad ete stomā bhavantīmān eva lokān prajanayanty eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  sa etaṃ tryahaṃ punaḥ prāyauṅkta tena ṣaḍahena ṣaṭkratūn prājanayat
PB  yad eṣa ṣaḍaho bhavati ṛtūn eva prajanayanti ṛtuṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  sa etaṃ ṣaḍahaṃ punaḥ prāyuṅkta tābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ ṣaḍahābhyāṃ dvādaśamasaḥ prājanayat
PB  yad etau ṣaḍahau bhavato māsān eva prajanayanti māseṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  sa etau dvau ṣaḍahau punaḥ prayuṅkta taiś caturbhiḥ ṣaḍahaiś caturviṃśatim ardhamāsān prājanayat
PB  yad ete catvāraḥ ṣaḍahā bhavanty ardhamāsān eva prajanayanty ardhamāseṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  sa idaṃ bhuvanaṃ prajanayitva pṛṣṭhyena ṣaḍahena vīryam ātmany adhatta
PB  yad eṣaḥ pṛṣṭhyaḥ ṣaḍaho bhavati vīrya evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  tena māsān saṃvvatsaraṃ prājanayad yad eṣa māso bhavati saṃvvatsaram eva prajanayanti saṃvvatsare pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  prāyaṇīyam etad ahar bhavati
PB  prāyaṇīyena vā ahnā devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyan yat prāyaṃs tat prāyaṇīyasya prāyaṇīyatvam
PB  tasmāt prāyaṇīyasyāhna ṛtvijā bhavitavyam etad dhi svargasya lokasya nediṣṭhaṃ ya etasyartviṅ na bhavati hīyate svargāl lokāt
PB  caturviṃśaṃ bhavati
PB  caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam ārabhya prayanti
PB  caturviṃśaṃ bhavati caturviṃśo vai saṃvvatsaraḥ sākṣād eva saṃvvatsaram ārabhante
PB  yāvatyaś caturviṃśasyokthasya stotrīyās tāvatyaḥ saṃvvatsarasya rātrayaḥ stotrīyābhir eva tat saṃvvatsaram āpnuvanti
PB  pañcadaśastotrāṇi bhavanti pañcadaśārdhamāsasya rātrayo 'rdhamāsaśa eva tat saṃvvatsaram āpnuvanti
PB  pañcadaśa stotrāṇi pañcadaśaśastrāṇi samāso māsaśa eva tat saṃvvatsaram āpnuvanti
PB  tad āhur īrma iva vā eṣā hotrā yad acchāvākyā yad acchāvākam anusaṃtiṣṭhata
īśvarermā bhavitor iti yady ukthaṃ smātraikakubhañcodvaṃśīyañcāntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpye
vīryaṃ vā ete samanī vīrya evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  atho khalv āhur agniṣṭomam eva kāryam eṣa vai yajñaḥ svargyo yad agniṣṭoma ūrdhvo hi hotāram anusaṃtiṣṭhate
PB  dvādaśastotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvvatsaras tena saṃvvatsarasaṃmito
dvādaśa stotraṇi dvādaśa śastrāṇi tac caturviṃśatiś caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvvatsaras
tena saṃvvatsarasaṃmitaḥ
PB  atho khalv āhur uktham eva kāryam ahnaḥ samṛddhyai
PB  sarvāṇi rūpāṇi kriyante sarvaṃ hy etāhnāpyate
PB  pavante vājasātaye somāḥ sahasrapājasa iti sahasravatī pratipat kāryā
PB  saṃvvatsarasya rūpaṃ sarvan evainān etayā punāti sarvān abhivadati
 PB  atho khalv āhuḥ pavasva vāco agriya ity eva kāryā mukhaṃ vā etat saṃvvatsarasya yad vāco 'graṃ mukhata eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhante 
 PB  mithunam iva vā eṣā vyāhṛtiḥ pavasveti puṃso rūpaṃ vāca iti striyāḥ someti puṃso rūpaṃ citrābhir iti striyā mithunam evaibhyo yajñamukhe  
dadhāti prajananāya 
 PB  agne yuṅkṣvā hi ye taveti jarābodhīyam agniṣṭoma sāma kāryaṃ yuktenaiva saṃvvatsareṇa prayanti caturviṃśatyakṣarāsu bhavati caturviṃśasya 
PB  atho khalv āhur yajñāyajñīyam eva kāryam
PB  panthā vai yajñāyajñīyaṃ patha eva tan na yanti
PB  abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavati
PB  abhīvartena vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam abhyavartanta yad abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavati svargasya lokasyābhivṛttyai
PB  ekākṣaraṇidhano bhavaty ekākṣarā vai vāg vācaiva tad ārabhya svargaṃ lokaṃ yanti
PB  sāmneto yanty ṛcā punar āyanti
PB  sāma vai asau loka ṛg ayaṃ yad itaḥ sāmnā yanti svargaṃ lokam ārabhya yanti yad ṛcā punar āyanty asmin loke pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  yat sāmāvasṛjeyur ava svargāl lokāt padyeran yad ṛcam anusṛjeyur naśyeyur asmāl lokāt
PB  samānaṃ sāma bhavaty anyo'nyaḥ pragātho 'nyadanyad dhi citram adhvānam avagacchann eti
PB  vṛṣā vā eṣa retodhā yad abhīvartaḥ pragātheṣu reto dadhad eti yad itaḥ
samānaṃ sāma bhavaty anyo'nyaḥ pragātho reta eva tad dadhati yat parastāt samānaḥ
pragātho bhavaty anyadanyat sāma reta eva tad dhitaṃ prajanayanti
PB  sāmnetaḥ pragāthāṃ dugdhe pragāthena parastāt sāmāni dugdhe salomatvāya
PB  yo vā adhvānaṃ punar nivartayanti nainaṃ te gacchanti ye 'punar nivartaṃ yanti te gacchati
PB  ya āstutaṃ kurvate yathā dugdhām upasīded evaṃ tat
PB  ye nāstutaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayante tam abhyaśnuvate
 PB  brahmavādino vadanti yātayāmāḥ saṃvvatsarā ayātayāmā iti te nāyātayāmeti vaktavyaṃ punar anyāni stotrāṇi nivartanta ūrdhvam eva 
PB  pañcasu māḥsu bārhatāḥ pragāthā āpyante
PB  teṣv āpteṣu chandasī saṃyujyaitavyam
PB  tisra uṣṇihaḥ syur ekā gāyatrī tās tisro bṛhatyo bhavanti
PB  tad āhuḥ saṃśara iva vā eṣa cchandasāṃ yad dve chandasī saṃyuñjantīti
PB  catur uttarair eva cchandobhir etavyam
PB  paśavo vai caturuttarāṇi cchandasāṃsi paśubhir eva tat svargaṃ lokam ākramam ānayanti
PB  ekaṃ gāyatrīm ekāham upeyur ekāmuṣṇiham ekāham ekām anuṣṭubham ekāhaṃ
bṛhatyā pañcamāsa iyuḥ paṅktim ekāham upeyus triṣṭubhā ṣaṣṭhaṃ māsam īyuḥ śvo viṣuvān
bhaviteti jagatīm upeyuḥ
PB  tad āhur anavakḷptāni vā etāni cchandāṃsi madhyandine bṛhatyā caiva triṣṭubhā caitavyam
PB  ete vai chandasī vīryavatī ete pratyakṣaṃ madhyandinasya rūpam
PB  rathantare 'hani bṛhatī kāryaitad vai rathantarasya svam āyatanaṃ yad
bṛhatī sva eva tad āyatane rathantaraṃ pratitiṣṭhati bārhate 'hani triṣṭup kāryaitad
vai bṛhataḥ svam āyatanaṃ yat triṣṭup sva eva tad āyatane bṛhadrathantare pratitiṣṭhantī itaḥ
PB  trayastriṃśatā pragāthair etavyaṃ trayastriṃśad devatā devatāsv eva pratitiṣṭhanto
yanti caturviṃśatyaitavyaṃ caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsara eva
pratitiṣṭhanto yanti dvādaśabhir etavyaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsara eva
pratitiṣṭhanto yanti ṣaḍbhir etavyaṃ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanto yanti caturbhir
etavyaṃ catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanto yanti tribhir etavyaṃ traya
ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanto yanti dvābhyām etavyaṃ dvipād yajamānaḥ svargasya
lokasyākrāntyā anyenānyena hi padā puruṣaḥ pratitiṣṭhann eti
PB  svarasāmāna ete bhavante
PB  svarbhānur vā āsur ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat taṃ devāḥ svarair aspṛṇvan yat svarasāmāno bhavanty ādityasya spṛtyai
PB  parair vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam apārayan yad aparayaṃs tat parāṇāṃ paratvaṃ
PB  pārayanty enaṃ parāṇi ya evaṃv veda
PB  saptadaśā bhavanti
PB  prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evopayanti
PB  anuṣṭup chandaso bhavanty ānuṣṭubho vai prajāpatiḥ sākṣād eva prajāpatim ārabhante
PB  trayaḥ purastāt trayaḥ parastād bhavanti
PB  devā vā ādityasya svargāl lokād avapādād abibhayus tam etaiḥ stomaiḥ saptadaśair adṛṃhan yad ete stomābhavanty ādityasya dhṛtyai
PB  catustriṃśā bhavanti varṣma vai catustriṃśo varṣmaṇaivainaṃ saṃmimate
 PB  tasya parācīnātipādād abibhayus taṃ sarvaiḥ stomaiḥ paryārṣan viśvajidabhijidbhyāṃ vīryaṃ vā etau stomau vīryeṇaiva tad ādityaṃ  
paryuṣanti dhṛtyai 
PB  anavapādāyānatipādāya
PB  tad āhuḥ kartapraskanda iva vā eṣa yat trayastriṃśataḥ saptadaśam upayantīti pṛṣṭhyo 'ntaraḥ kāryaḥ
PB  tasya yat saptadaśam ahas tad uttamaṃ kāryaṃ salomatvāya
PB  tad āhur udaraṃ vā eṣa stomānāṃ yat saptadaśo yat saptadaśaṃ madhyato nirhareyur aśanāyavaḥ prajāḥ syur aśanāyavaḥ sattriṇaḥ
PB  trayastriṃśād eva saptadaśa upetyo varṣma vai trayastriṃśo varṣma saptadaśo varṣmaṇa eva tad varṣmābhisaṃkrāmanti
PB  nānāhur ukthāḥ kāryā iti yady ukthāḥ syuḥ
PB  paśavo vā ukthāni śāntiḥ paśavaḥ śāntenaiva tad viṣuvantam upayanti
PB  tad āhur vivīvadham iva vā etad yad agniṣṭomo viṣuvān agniṣṭomau viśvajidabhijitāv athetara ukthāḥ syur iti
PB  agniṣṭomā eva sarve kāryāḥ
PB  vīryaṃ vā agniṣṭomo vīrya eva madhyataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti nava saṃstutā bhavanti nava prāṇāḥ praṇeṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  viṣuvān eṣa bhavati
PB  devaloko vā eṣa yad viṣuvān devaokam eva tad abhyārohanti
PB  ekaviṃśo bhavaty ekaviṃśo vā asya bhuvanasyāditya ādityalokam eva tad abhyārohanti
PB  dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśaḥ
PB  madhyata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  vāyo śukro ayāmi ta iti śukravatī pratipad bhavaty ādityasya rūpam
PB  vāyur vā etaṃ devatānām ānaśe 'nuṣṭup chandasaṃ yad ato 'nyā pratipat syāt pradahet
PB  yanti vā ete prāṇādityāhur ye gāyatryāḥ pratipado yantīti yad vayavyā bhavanti tena prāṇān na yanti prāṇo hi vāyuḥ
PB  atho śamayanty evainam etayā śantir hi vāyuḥ
PB  ā yāhi somapītaya iti saumī pāvamānī
PB  niyutvatī bhavati paśavo vai niyutaḥ śāntiḥ paśavaḥ śāntenaiva tad ādityam upayanti
PB  divākīrtyasāmā bhavati
PB  svarbhānur vā āsur ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat tasya devā divākīrtyais tamo
'pāghnan yad divākīrtyāni bhavanti tama evāsmād apaghnanti raśmayo vā eta ādityasya
yad divākīrtyāni raśmibhir eva tad ādityaṃ sākṣād ārabhante
PB  bhrājābhrāje pavamānamukhe bhavato mukhata evāsya tābhyāṃ tamo 'paghnanti
 PB  mahādivākīrtyaṃ ca vikarṇaṃ ca madhyato bhavato madhyata evāsya tābhyāṃ tamo 'paghnanti bhāsam antato bhavati patta evāsya tena  
tamo 'paghnanti 
PB  daśastobhaṃ bhavti daśākṣarā virāḍ virājy eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  yat tv ity āhuḥ ṣaḍbhir ito māsair adhvānaṃ yanti ṣaḍbhiḥ punar āyanti kva tarhi svargo loko yasya kāmāya sattram āsata iti
PB  mūrdhānaṃ diva iti svargaṃ lokam ārabhante
PB  aratiṃ pṛthivyā ity asmiṃ loke pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  vaiśvānaram ṛta ājātam agnim iti viṣuvata eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
PB  kaviṃ samrājam atitihiṃ janānām ity annādyam evopayanti
PB  āsan nāpātraṃ janayanta devā iti jāyanta eva
PB  tat triṣṭub jagatīṣu bhavati traiṣṭubhjāgato vā ādityo yad ato 'nyāsu syād ava svargāl lokāt padyeran
PB  samrāḍvatīṣu bhavati sāmrājyaṃ vai svargo lokaḥ svarga eva loke pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  ātmā vā eṣa saṃvvatsarasya yad viṣuvān pakṣāv etāv abhito bhavato yena
ceto 'bhīvartena yanti yaś ca parasmāt pragātho bhavati tāv ubhau viṣuvati kāryau
pakṣāv eva tad yajñasyātman pratidadhati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
PB  indra kratuṃ na ābhareti pragātho bhavati
PB  vasiṣṭho vā etaṃ putrahato 'paśyat sa prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyata yad eṣa pragātho bhavati prajātyai
PB  jīvā jyotir aśīmahīti ye vai svasti saṃvvatsaraṃ saṃtaranti te jīvā jyotir aśnuvate
PB  māno ajñātā vṛjanā durādhyo māśivāso 'vakramur iti ye vai stenā ripavas te durādhyas tān eva tad atikrāmati
PB  tvayā vyayaṃ pravataḥ śaśvatīr apo 'ti śūra tarāma so 'tisaṃvvatsaro vai pravataḥ śaśvatīr apas tam eva tat taranti
 PB  adyādyāśvaḥ śvas tvām idā hyo naro vayam enam idā hya iti saṃtanayaḥ pragāthā bhavanti teṣām ekaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāya śvastanam evābhisaṃtanvanti 
PB  atho khalv āhur indra kratuṃ na ābharety eva kāryaṃ samṛddhyai
PB  pratyavarohiṇo māsā bhavanti
PB  yathā vā ito vṛkṣaṃ rohanty evam enaṃ pratyavarohanti svargam eva lokaṃ rūḍhvāsmiṃl loke pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  gauś cāyuś ca stomau bhavataḥ
PB  dvipād yajamānaḥ pratiṣṭhityai
PB  ūnātiriktau bhavata ūnātiriktaṃ vā anu prajāḥ prajāyante prajātyai
PB  vairājau bhavato 'nnaṃ virāḍ annādya eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  dvādaśāhasya daśāhāni bhavanti
PB  virāḍ vā eṣā samṛddhā yad daśāhāni virājy eva samṛddhāyāṃ pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  pṛṣthāni bhavanti vīryaṃ vai pṛṣṭhāni vīrya eva pratitiṣṭhanti cchandomā
bhavanti paśavo vai cchandomāḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanty athaitad daśamam ahar āptastomam
āptacchanda āptavibhaktikam aniruktaṃ prājāpatyam
PB  yad adhyāhur ati tad recayanti tasmān na vyucyam
PB  parokṣam anuṣṭubham upayanti prajāpatir vā anuṣṭub yat pratyakṣam upeyuḥ prajāpatim ṛccheyuḥ
 PB  yo vai sattrasya sad veda sad bhavati vāmadevyaṃ vai sāmnāṃ sad agnir devatānāṃ virāṭ chandasāṃ trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ tāny eva  
tad ekadhā saṃbhṛtyottiṣṭhanti 
PB  brahmavādino vadanti yataḥ sattrād udasthātāsthitād iti
PB  ye rathantareṇa stutvottiṣṭhanti te yata uttiṣṭhanti tān brūyād apratiṣṭhānā
bhaviṣyantīti ye bṛhatā stutyottiṣṭhanti te sthitād uttiṣṭhanti tān brūyāt sthāyukaiṣāṃ
śrīr bhaviṣyati na vasīyāṃso bhaviṣyantīti
PB  ye vāmadevyena stutvottiṣṭhanti te sataḥ sad abhyuttiṣṭhanti pūrṇāt pūrṇam āyatanād āyatanam antarikṣāyatanā hi prajā
PB  trayastriṃśadakṣarāsu bhavati trayastriṃśaddevatāsv eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti
PB  prājāpatyaṃ vai vāmadevyaṃ prajāpatāv eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśuṣv eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti
PB  patnīḥ saṃyājya prāñca udetyāyaṃ sahasramānava ity aticchandasāhavanīyam upatiṣṭhante
PB  ime vai lokā aticchandā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  gor iti nidhanaṃ bhavati virājo vā etad rūpaṃ yad gaur virājy eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  pratyañcaḥ prapadya sārparājñyā ṛgbhiḥ stuvanti
PB  arbudaḥ sarpa etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata mṛtām evaitābhirs tvacam apaghnate
PB  iyaṃ vai sārparājñy asyām eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  tisṛbhiḥ stuvanti traya ime lokā eṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  manasopāvartayati
PB  manasā hiṅ karoti manasā prastauti manasodgāyati manasā pratiharati manasā nidhanam upayanty asamāptasya samāptyai
PB  yad vai vācā na samāpnuvanti manasā tat samāpnuvanti
PB  pariśrite stuvanti brahmaṇaḥ parigṛhītyai
PB  brahmodyaṃ vadanti brahmavarcasa eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  caturhotāraṃ hotā vyācaṣṭe stutam eva tad anuśaṃsati nahi tat stutaṃ yad ananuśastam
PB  prajāpatiṃ parivadanty āptvevainaṃ tad vyācakṣate tāvad āpāmainam iti
PB  gṛhapatir audumbarīṃ dhārayati gṛhapatir vā ūrjo yantorjam evaibhyo yacchati
PB  vācaṃ yacchanti
PB  dugdhānīva vai tarhi chandasāṃsi yātayāmāny antargatāni tāny eva tad rasenāpyāyayanti
PB  atho śvastanam evābhisaṃtanvanti
PB  ātmadakṣiṇaṃ vā etad yat sattram
PB  yadā vai puruṣa ātmano 'vadyati yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam abhyaśnute
PB  dvābhyāṃ lomāvadyati dvābhyāṃ tvacaṃ dvābhyāṃ māṃsaṃ dvābhyām asthi dvābhyāṃ majjānaṃ dvābhyāṃ pīvaś ca lohitaṃ ca
PB  śikhā anupravapante pāpmānam eva tad apaghnate laghīyāṃsaḥ svargaṃ lokam ayāmeti
PB  atho gavām evānurūpā bhavanti sarvasyānnādyasyāvaruddhyai
PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata so 'ricyata so 'padyata taṃ devā abhisamagacchanta
te 'bruvan mahad asmai vrataṃ saṃbharāma yad imaṃ dhinavad iti tasmai yat saṃvvatsaram
annaṃ pacyate tat samabharaṃs tad asmai prāyacchaṃs tad avrajayat tad enam adhinon
mahan maryā vrataṃ yad imam adhinvīd iti tan mahāvratasya mahāvratatvam
PB  prajāpatir vāva mahāṃs tasyaitad vratam annam eva
PB  tad āhur madhyaḥ saṃvvatsarasyopetyaṃ madhyato vā annaṃ jagdhaṃ dhinoti
 PB  tad v āhur yan madhyata upayanty ardham annādyasyāpnuvanty ardhaṃ sambaṭ kurvantīty upariṣṭād eva saṃvvatsarasyopetyaṃ saṃvvatsare  
vā annaṃ sarvaṃ pacyate 
PB  caturviṃśaṃ bhavati caturviṃśo vai saṃvvatsaro 'nnaṃ pañcaviṃśam
PB  yad vā adaś caturviṃśaṃprāyaṇīyaṃ tad etad udayanīyam
PB  yat saṃvvatsaram annaṃ saṃbharanti saiṣā pañcaviṃśy upajāyate
PB  vāmadevyaṃ mahāvrataṃ kāryam
PB  trivṛc chiro bhavati
PB  trivṛd dhy eva śiro loma tvag asthi
PB  pāṅkta itara ātmā loma tvaṅ māṃsam asthi majjā
PB  sakṛd dhiṅkṛtena śirasā pārācā stuvate
PB  tasmāc chiro 'ṅgāni medyanti nānumedyati na kṛśyanty anukṛśyati
PB  punar abhyāvartam itareṇātmanā stuvate tasmād itara ātmā medyati ca kṛśyati ca
PB  arkavatīṣu gāyatrīṣu śiro bhavati
PB  annaṃ vā arko brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatry annādyaṃ caivaibhyo brahmavarcasaṃ ca mukhato dadhāti
PB  pañcadaśasaptadaśau pakṣau bhavataḥ prakṣābhyāṃ vai yajamāno vayo bhūtvā svargaṃ lokam eti
PB  tāv āhuḥ samau kāryau pañcadaśau vā saptadaśau vā savīvadhatvāya
 PB  tad v āhur yat samau bhavata ekavīryau tarhi bhavata iti pañcadaśasaptadaśāv eva kāryau sācīva vai vayaḥ pakṣau kṛtvāpatīyaḥ patati 
PB  dakṣiṇato bṛhat kāryaṃ dakṣiṇo vā ardha ātmano vīryavattaraḥ
 PB  atho khalv āhur uttarata eva kāryaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsino 'rdhāt traiṣṭubhaṃ vai bṛhat traiṣṭubho vai brāhmaṇācchaṃsī traiṣṭubhaḥ pañcadaśastomaḥ 
PB  dakṣiṇato rathantaraṃ kāryaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyārdhād gāyatraṃ vai rathantaraṃ gāyatro maitrāvaruṇo gāyatraḥ saptadaśastomaḥ
PB  ekaviṃśaṃ pucchaṃ bhavati
PB  ekaviṃśo vai stomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā tasmād vayaḥ pucchena pratiṣṭhāyotpatati pucchena pratiṣṭhāya niṣīdati
PB  yajñāyajñīyaṃ pucchaṃ kāryaṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ hy eva mahāvratasya puccham
PB  atho khalv āhur atiśayaṃ vai dvipadāṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ bhadram kāryaṃ samṛddhyai
PB  vāmadevyaṃ mahāvrataṃ kāryaṃ tasya gāyatraṃ śiro bṛhadrathantare pakṣau yajñāyajñīyaṃ puccham
PB  yo vai mahāvrate sahasraṃ protaṃ veda pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti
PB  tasya prācī dik śiras tac chandobhiḥ sahasram asāv anyataraḥ pakṣaḥ sanakṣattraiḥ
sāhasro 'yam anyataraḥ pakṣaḥ sa oṣadhibhiś ca vanaspatibhiś ca sāhasro 'ntarikṣam
ātmā tad vayobhiḥ sāhasraṃ pratīcī dik pucchaṃ tad agnibhiś ca raśmibhiś ca sāhasraṃ
pra sasasraṃ paśūn āpnoti ya evaṃv veda
PB  tad āhur apṛṣṭhaṃ vai vāmadevyam anidhanaṃ hīti
PB  anāyatanaṃ vā etat sāma yad anidhanam
PB  rājanaṃ mahāvrataṃ kāryam
PB  etad vai sākṣād annaṃ yad rājanaṃ pañcavidhaṃ bhavati pāṅktaṃ hy annam
PB  hiṅkāravad bhavati tena vāmadevyasya rūpam
PB  nidhanavad bhavati tena prṣṭhasya rūpam
PB  aticchandaḥsu pañcanidhanaṃ vāmadevyaṃ brahmasāma kāryam
PB  ati vā eṣānyāni cchandāṃsi yad aticchandā aty etad anyāny ahāny ahar yan mahāvratam
PB  brahmasāmnaiva tad anyāny ahāny atimedayati
PB  pañcanidhanaṃ bhavati pāṅktaṃ hy annam
PB  ilāndam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam
PB  etad vai sākṣād annaṃ yad ilāndam irānnaṃ etad irāyām evānnādye 'ntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  samudro vā etac chandaḥ salilaṃ lomaśaṃ samudra iva khalu vai sa bhavati salila iva lomaśa iva yo bhavati
PB  tasmād etāsu kāryaṃ samṛddhyai
PB  vratam iti nidhanaṃ bhavati mahāvratasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate svar iti
bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai śakuna iti bhavati śakuna iva vai yajamāno vayo
bhūtvā svargaṃl lokam eti
PB  yajñāyajñīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam
PB  yad vā anyā vāṅ nātivadet tad agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ na vai vāg vācam ativadati vāg yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam
PB  agnir vā idaṃ vaiśvānaro 'dahan naitasmād devā abibhayus taṃ varaṇaśākhayāvārayanta yad avārayanta tasmād vāravantīyam
PB  tasmād varaṇo bhiṣajya etena hi devā ātmānam atrāyanta
PB  tasmād brāhmaṇo vāraṇena na pibed vaiśvānaraṃ necchamayā iti
PB  paśavo vai vāravantīyaṃ śāntiḥ paśavaḥ śāntād eva tat saṃvvatsarād uttiṣṭhanti
PB  prāṇena purastād āhavanīyam upatiṣṭhante prāṇam eva taj jayanti
PB  apānena paścāt puccham upatiṣṭhante apānam eva taj jayanti
PB  vratapakṣābhyāṃ pakṣāv upatiṣṭhante diśa eva taj jayanti
PB  prajāpater hṛdayenāpikakṣam upatiṣṭhante jyaiṣṭhyam eva taj jayanti
PB  vasiṣṭhasya nihavena cātvālam upatiṣṭhante svargam eva tal lokam āotvā śriyaṃ vadante
PB  vaiśvadevyām ṛci bhavati viśvarūpaṃ vai paśūnāṃ rūpaṃ paśūn eva taj jayanti
PB  sattrasyarddhyāgnīdhram upatiṣṭhanta ṛddhāv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  caturakṣarāṇidhanaṃ bhavati catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  ātamitor nidhanam upayanty āyur eva sarvam āpnuvanti
PB  ślokānuślokābhyāṃ havirdhāne upatiṣṭhante kīrtim eva taj jayanti
PB  yāmena mārjālīyam upatiṣṭhante pitṛlokam eva taj jayanti
PB  āyurṇavastobhābhyāṃ sada upatiṣṭhante brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca jayanti
PB  ṛśyasya sāmnā gārhapatyam upatiṣṭhante
 PB  indraṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny astuvaṃs tasyarśya ekam aṅgam astutam acāyat tad asyaitenāstaut tenāsya priyaṃ dhāmopāgacchat priyam evāsyaitena 
PB  yat paro'kṣaṃ nidhanam upeyur hrītamukhaṃ pratimuñceran pratyakṣam upayanti hrītamukham evāpajayanti
PB  āsandīm āruhyodgāyati devasākṣya eva tad upariṣadyaṃ jayati
PB  audumbarī bhavaty ūrg udumbara ūrjam evāvarunddhe
PB  prādeśamātrī bhavaty asya lokasyānuddhānāya
PB  chandobhir ārohati svargam eva tal lokam ārohati
PB  chandobhir upāvarohaty asmiṃ loke pratitiṣṭhati
PB  sarveṇātmanā samuddhṛtyodgeyam eṣu lokeṣu ned vyāhito 'sānīti
PB  ekasyāṃ stotrīyāyām astutāyāṃ pādāv upāharati
PB  saha nidhanena pratiṣṭhām upayanty eṣeṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhante
PB  preṅkhām āruhya hotā śaṃsati mahasa eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
PB  yadā vai prajā maha āviśati preṅkhās tarhy ārohanti
PB  phalakam āruhyādhvaryuḥ pratigṛṇāti
PB  kūrcān itare 'dhyāsata ūrdhvā eva tad utkrāmanto yanti
 PB  abhigarāpagarau bhavato nindaty enān anyaḥ prānyaḥ śaṃsati ya enān nindati pāpmānam eṣāṃ so 'pahanti yaḥ praśaṃsati yad evaiṣāṃ  
suṣṭutaṃ suśastaṃ tat so 'bhigṛṇāti 
PB  śūdrāryau carmaṇi vyāyacchete tayor āryaṃ varṇam ujjāpayanti
PB  devāś ca vā asurāś cāditye vyāyacchantas taṃ devā abhyajayaṃs tato devā abhavan 
parāsurā abhavann ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  yadāryaṃ varṇam ujjāpayanty ātmānam eva tad ujjāpayanti
PB  parimaṇḍalaṃ carma bhavaty ādityasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
PB  sarvāsu sraktiṣu dundubhayo vadanti yā vanaspatiṣu vāk tām eva taj jayanti
PB  bhūmidundubhir bhavati yā pṛthivyāṃ vāk tām eva taj jayanti
PB  sarvā vāco vadanti yeṣu lokeṣu vāk tām eva taj jayanti
PB  saṃnaddhāḥ kavacinaḥ pariyantīndriyasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate 'tho mahāvratam eva mahayanti
PB  sarve sahartvijo mahāvratena stuvīran
PB  adhvaryuḥ śirasodgāyan maitrāvaruṇo dakṣiṇena pakṣeṇa brāhmaṇācchaṃsy uttareṇa gṛhapatiḥ pucchenodgātātmanā
PB  tad yady evaṃ kuryur ekaikayā stotrīyayāstutayodgātāram abhisameyuḥ
PB  tisṛbhir udgātātmana udgīyātha yā śirasaḥ stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyād aparābhis
tisṛbhir udgīyātha yā dakṣiṇasya pakṣasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyād aparābhis tisṛbhir
udgīyātha yottarasya pakṣasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyāt tisṛbhir vaikayā vā stutaṃ syād
atha yā pucchasya stotrīyā tāṃ dadhyāt
PB  ātmany eva tad aṅgāni pratidadhati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
PB  atho khalv āhuḥ katham adhvaryur bahvṛcaḥ sāma gāyed ity udgātaiva sarveṇodgāyet tad eva samṛddhaṃ samṛddhāv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  havirdhāne śirasā stutvā saṃrabdhāḥ pratyañca eyus te dakṣiṇena dhiṣṇyān
parītya paścān maitrāvaruṇasya dhiṣṇyasyopaviśya rathantareṇa pañcadaśena stuvīraṃs
ta udañcaḥ saṃsarpeyur jaghanena hotur dhiṣṇyaṃ paścād brāhmaṇācchaṃsino dhiṣṇyasyopaviśya
bṛhatā saptadaśena stuvīraṃs te yenaiva prasarpeyus tena punar niḥsṛpyottareṇāgnīdhraṃ
parītya paścād gārhapatyasyopaviśya pucchenaikaviṃśena stuvīraṃs te yenaiva niḥsarpeyus
tena punaḥ prasṛpya yathāyatanam upaviśyāsandīm āruhyodgātātmanodgāyati
PB  taṃ patnyo 'paghāṭilābhir upagāyanty ārtvijyam eva tat patnyaḥ kurvanti saha svargaṃl lokam ayāmeti
PB  kulekule 'nnaṃ kriyate tad yat pṛccheyuḥ kim idaṃ kurvantītīme yajamānā annam atsyantīti brūyuḥ
PB  yo vai dīkṣitānāṃ pāpaṃ kīrtayati tṛtīyam evāṃśaṃ pāpmano haraty annādas tṛtīyaṃ pipīlikās tṛtīyam
PB  parimādbhiś caranti tvak ca vā etal loma ca mahāvratasya yat parimādas tvacaṃ caiva tal loma ca mahāvratasyāptvāvarundhate
PB  vāṇaṃ vitanvanty anto vai vāṇo 'nto mahāvratam antenaiva tad antam abhivādayanti
PB  śatatantrīko bhavati śatāyur vai puruṣaḥ śatavīryaḥ
PB  tam ullikhet prāṇāya tvāpānāya tvā vyānāya tveti prāṇāpānavyānān eva tad āptvāvarundhate
PB  pari kumbhinyo mārjālīyaṃ yantīdaṃ madhv idaṃ madhv iti saghoṣā eva tad vayo bhūtvā saha svargaṃl lokaṃ yanti
 PB  devā vai vācaṃ vyabhajanta tasyā yo raso 'tyaricyata tad gaurīvitam abhavad anuṣṭubham anu pariplavate vāg anuṣṭub vāco raso gaurīvitam 
PB  yad gaurīvitenānvahaṃs stuvate vācy eva tad vācā rasaṃ dadhati
PB  rasavad vācā vadati ya evaṃv vedeti
PB  dvyudāsaṃ bhavati svargasya vā etau lokasyāvasānadeśau pūrveṇaiva pūrvam ahaḥ saṃsthāpayanty uttareṇottaram ahar abhyativadanti
PB  etad vai yajñasya śvastanaṃ yad gaurīvitaṃ yad gaurīvitam anusṛjeyur aśvastanā aprajasaḥ syuḥ
PB  saṃ vā anyo yajñas tiṣṭhata ity āhur vāg eva na saṃtiṣṭhata iti yad gaurīvitam anvahaṃ bhavati vācam eva tat punaḥ prayuñjate
PB  svarṇidhanam anvahaṃ bhavati
PB  devakṣetraṃ vā ete 'bhyārohanti ye svarṇidhanam upayanti sa u vai sattriṇaḥ
sattram upanayed ity āhur ya enān devakṣetram abhyārohed iti na vai devakṣetra āsīna
ārtim ārchati yat svarṇidhanam anvahaṃ bhavati naiva kāṃ canārtim ārchanti
PB  cyavante vā ete 'smāl lokād ity āhur ye svarṇidhanam upayantīti yad ṛcā
svarūpaṃ yanty asmiṃ loke pratitiṣṭhanti yad ekāro 'tarikṣe yat sāmnāmuṣmint sarveṣu
lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhanti svarṇidhanena tuṣṭuvānāḥ
PB  sujñānaṃ bhavati
 PB  devā vai svargaṃl lokaṃ yanto 'jñātād abibhayus ta etat saṃjñānam apaśyaṃs tena jñātram agacchan yat sujñānam anvahaṃ bhavati jñātram  
eva gacchanti 
PB  ye vai vācam annam ādayanty annādā bhavanti ye vitarṣayanti rukṣā bhavanti
 PB  gaurīvitaṃ śyāvāśvaṃ nihava etāni vai sāmāni vāco 'nnam eteṣāṃ vāg annaṃ yad etāni na cyavante vācam eva tad annam ādayanti tena  
sarve 'nnādā bhavanti 
PB  abhikrāntāpakrāntāni bhavanty abhikrāntāpakrāntaṃ vai vāco rūpam
PB  plavo 'nvahaṃ bhavati
 PB  samudraṃ vā ete prasnānti ye saṃvvatsaram upayanti yo vā aplavaḥ samudraṃ prasnāti na sa tata udeti yat plavo bhavati svargasya 
PB  ati viśvāni duritā taremeti yad evaiṣāṃ duṣṭutaṃ duḥśastaṃ tad etena taranti
PB  okonidhanaṃ ṣaḍahamukhe bhavati
PB  parāṃ vā ete parāvataṃ gacchanti ye ṣaḍahasyāntaṃ gacchanti yadokonidhanaṃ ṣaḍahamukhe bhavati prajñātyai
PB  yadā vai puruṣaḥ svam oka āgacchati sarvaṃ tarhi prajānāti sarvam asmai divā bhavati
PB  ekāṣṭakāyāṃ dīkṣeran
PB  eṣā vai saṃvvatsarasya patnī yad ekāṣṭakaitasyāṃ vā gatāṃ rātriṃ vasati sākṣād eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhya dīkṣante
PB  tasya sāniryā yad apo' nabhinandanto 'bhyavayanti
PB  vicchinnaṃ vā ete saṃvvatsarasyābhidīkṣante ya ekāṣṭakāyāṃ dīkṣante 'ntanāmānāv ṛtū bhavete
PB  ārtaṃ vā ete saṃvvatsarasyābhidīkṣante ye 'ntanāmānāv ṛtū abhidīkṣante
PB  tasmād ekāṣṭakāyāṃ na dīkṣyam
PB  phālgune dīkṣeran
PB  mukhaṃ vā etat saṃvvatsarasya yat phālguno mukhata eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhya dīkṣante
PB  tasya sāniryā yat saṃmeghe viṣuvān saṃpadyate
PB  citrāpūrṇamāse dīkṣeran
 PB  cakṣur vā etat saṃvvatsarasya yac citrāpūrṇamāso mukhato vai cakṣur mukhata eva tat saṃvvatsaram ārabhya dīkṣante tasya na niryāsti 
PB  caturahe purastāt paurṇamāsyā dīkṣeran
PB  teṣām akāṣṭakāyāṃ krayaḥ saṃpadyate tenaikāṣṭakāṃ na saṃbaṭ kurvanti
PB  teṣāṃ pūrvapakṣe sutyā saṃpadyate pūrvapakṣe māsāḥ saṃtiṣṭhamānā yanti
pūrvapakṣa uttiṣṭhanti tān uttiṣṭhataḥ paśava oṣadhayo 'nūttiṣṭhanti tān kalyāṇī
vāg abhivadary arātsur ime sattriṇa iti te rādhnuvanti
PB  ā vā ete saṃvvatsaraṃ pyāyayanti ya utsṛjanti
PB  yathā vai dṛtir ādhmāta evaṃ saṃvvatsaro 'nutsṛṣṭo yan notsṛjeyur amehena pramāyukāḥ syuḥ
 PB  prāṇo vai saṃvvatsara udānā māsā yad utsṛjanti prāṇa evodānān dadhati yo dīkṣitaḥ pramīyate yā saṃvvatsarasyānutsṛṣṭasya śuk sā  
tam ṛcchati 
PB  tad āhur utsṛjyāṃ notsṛjyām iti
PB  yady utsṛjeyur ukthāny utsṛjeyus tad evotsṛṣṭaṃ tad anutsṛṣṭam
PB  atho khalv āhur ekatrikaṃ kāryaṃ tad eva sākṣād utsṛṣṭam abhyutṣuṇvanti
PB  chidro vā eteṣāṃ saṃvvatsara ity āhur ye stomam utsṛjantīti
PB  paśum ālabhante stomam eva tad ālabhante stomo hi paśuḥ
PB  śva utsṛṣṭāḥ sma iti vatsān apākurvanti prātaḥ paśum ālabhante tasya
vapayā pracaranti tatas savanīyenāṣṭākapālena tata āgneyenāṣṭākapālena tato dadhnaindreṇa
tataś caruṇā vaiśvadevena tat prātaḥsavanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhante
 PB  tataḥ paśupuroḍāśenaikādaśakapālena tataḥ savanīyenaikādaśakapālena tato marutvatīyenaikādaśakapālena tataś caruṇaindreṇa tan  
mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhante 
 PB  paśunā pracaranti tataḥ savanīyena dvādaśakapālena tato vaiśvadevena dvādaśakapālena tataś caruṇāgnimārutena tat tṛtīyaṃ savanaṃ 
PB  pṛṣadājyena pracarya patnīs saṃyājayanti
PB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa etam agniṣṭomam apaśyat tam āharat tenemāḥ prajā asṛjata
 PB  ekādaśena ca vai satā stotreṇāgniṣṭomasyāsṛjataikādaśena ca māsā saṃvvatsarasya tā dvādaśena ca stotreṇāgniṣṭomasya paryagṛhṇād  
dvādaśena ca māsā saṃvvatsarasya 
PB  tasmāt prajā daśamāso garbhaṃ bhṛtvaikādaśam anu prajāyante tasmād dvādaśaṃ
nābhyatiharanti dvādaśena hi parigṛhītās tad ya evaṃv veda pari jātāḥ prajā gṛhṇāti pra jātā janayanti
 PB  tāsāṃ parigṛhītānām aśvatary atyakrāmat tasyā anuhāya reta ādattā tad vaḍavāyāṃ nyamāḍ yasmād vaḍavā dviretās tasmād aśvatary aprajā  
āttaretā hi 
 PB  tasmād v adakṣiṇīyāti hi sā yajñam aricyatātiriktasya dakṣiṇā syāt salomatvāya ṣoḍaśinaḥ stotredeyātirikto vai ṣoḍaśy atirikta evātiriktāṃ 
PB  so 'kāmayata yajñaṃ sṛjeyeti sa mukhata eva trivṛtam asṛjata taṃ gāyatrī
cchando 'nyasṛjyatāgnir devatā brāhmaṇo manuṣyo vasanta ṛtus tasmāt trivṛt stomānāṃ
mukhaṃ gāyatrī cchandasām agnir devatānāṃ brāhmaṇo manuṣyāṇāṃ vasanta ṛtūnāṃ tasmād
brāhmaṇo mukhena vīryaṃ karoti mukhato hi sṛṣṭaḥ
PB  karoti mukhena vīryaṃ ya evaṃv veda
PB  sa urasta eva bāhubhyāṃ pañcadaśam asṛjata taṃ triṣṭup chando 'nvasṛjyatendro
devatā rājanyo manuṣyo grīṣma ṛtus tasmād rājanyasya pañcadaśa stomas triṣṭup chanda
indro devatā grīṣma ṛtus tasmād u bāhuvīryo bāhubhyāṃ hi sṛṣṭaḥ
PB  karoti bāhubhyāṃ vīryaṃ ya evaṃv veda
PB  sa madhyata eva prajananāt saptadaśam asṛjata taṃ jagatī cchando 'nvasṛjyata
viśve devā devatā vaiśyo manuṣyo varṣā ṛtus tasmād vaiśyo 'dyamāno na kṣīyate prajananād
dhi sṛṣṭas tasmād u bahupaśur vaiśvadevo hi jāgato varṣā hy asyartus tasmād brāhmaṇasya
ca rājanyasya cādyo 'dharo hi sṛṣṭaḥ
PB  sa patta eva pratiṣṭhāyā ekaviṃśam asṛjata tam anuṣṭup chando 'nvasṛjyata
na kā cana devatā śūdro manuṣyas tasmāc chūdra uta bahupaśur ayajñiyo videvo hi na
hi taṃ kā cana devatā 'nvasṛjyata tasmāt pādāv anejyaṃ nāti vardhate patto hi sṛṣṭas
tasmād ekaviṃśastomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā pratiṣṭhāyā hi sṛṣṭas tasmād anuṣṭubhaṃ chandāṃsi nānu vyūhanti
PB  pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai
PB  vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  yo vai stomān upadeśanavato vedopadeśanavān bhavati
 PB  prāṇo vai trivṛd ardhamāsaḥ pañcadaśaḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saptadaśa āditya ekaviṃśa ete vai stomā upadeśanavanta upadeśanavān bhavati  
ya evaṃv veda 
PB  ime vai lokās triṇavas triṇavasya vai brāhmaṇeneme lokās triṣ punar navā bhavanti
PB  eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃv veda
PB  devatā vāva trayastriṃśo 'ṣṭau vasava ekādaśa rudrā dvādaśādityāḥ prajāpatiś ca vaṣaṭkāraś ca trayastriṃśau
PB  sa devena yajñena yajate ya evaṃv veda
PB  yo vā adhipatiṃ vedādhipatir bhavati trayastriṃśo vai stomānam adhipatiḥ puruṣaḥ paśumān
PB  tasmān nyañco 'nye paśavo 'danty ūrdhvaḥ puruṣo 'dhipatir hi saḥ
PB  adhipatiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  eṣa vāva yajño yad agniṣṭomaḥ
PB  ekasmā anyo yajñaḥ kāmāyāhriyate sarvebhyo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
PB  dvādaśa stotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nu prajāyante tena paśavyaḥ samṛddhaḥ
 PB  dvādaśa stotrāṇi dvādaśa śastrāṇi tac caturviṃśatiś caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ saṃvvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nuprajāyante tena  
paśavyaḥ samṛddhaḥ 
PB  agnau stotram agnau śastraṃ pratitiṣṭhati tena brahmavarcasasya
PB  kiṃ jyotiṣṭomasya jyotiṣṭomatvam ity āhur virājaṃ saṃstutaḥ saṃpadyate virāḍ vai cchandasāṃ jyotiḥ
PB  jyotiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  jyeṣṭhayajño vā eṣa yad agniṣṭomaḥ
 PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmai śraiṣṭhyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa etam agniṣṭomam apaśyat tam āharat tato 'smai prajāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta 
PB  tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃv veda
PB  yat tv ity āhur gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ kva tarhi turīyaṃ cchando 'nuṣṭub
PB  chandasāṃ vā anvavaluptiṃ yajamāno 'nvavalupyate
PB  aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī hiṅkāro navama ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub dvādaśākṣarā jagatī cchandobhirevānuṣṭubham āpnoti yajamānasyānavalopāya
 PB  yo vā anuṣṭubhaṃ sarvatrāpiṃ savanāny anvāyattāṃ veda sarvatrāsyāpir bhavaty eṣā vā anuṣṭup sarvatrāpiḥ savanāny anvāyattā tad  
ya evaṃ vveda sarvatrāpir bhavati 
PB  yad vai rājāno 'dhvānaṃ dhāvayanti ye 'śvānāṃv vīryavattamās tān yuñjate
trivṛt pañcadaśa ekaviṃśa ete vai stomānāṃv vīryavattamās tān eva yuṅkte svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
PB  catuṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vai catuṣṭomaḥ pratiṣṭhityai
PB  prajāpatir devebhya ūrjaṃ vyabhajat tata udumbaraḥ samabhavat prājāpatyo
vā udumbaraḥ prājāpatya udgātā yad udgātaudumbarīṃ prathamena karmaṇānvārabhate svayaiva
tad devatayātmānam ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte
PB  tām ucchrayati dyutānas tvā māruta ucchrayatūd divaṃ stabhānāntarikṣaṃ pṛṇa dṛṃha pṛthivīm
PB  tām anvārabhata āyoṣ ṭvā sadane sādayāmy avataś chāyāyāṃ samudrasya hṛdaya iti
PB  yajño vā āyus tasya tat sadanaṃ kriyate
PB  yajño vā avati tasya sā cchāyā kriyate
PB  madhyato vā ātmano hṛdayaṃ tasmān madhye sadasa audumbarī mīyate
PB  namaḥ samudrāya namaḥ samudrasya cakṣuṣa ity āha vāg vai samudro manaḥ samudrasya cakṣus tābhyām eva tan namas karoti
PB  sāmā yūnarvāhāsīd ity āha sāma vai yūnarvā sāmna eva tan namaskaroty ārtvijyaṃ kariṣyan
PB  yo vā evaṃ sāmne namaskṛtya sāmnārtvijyaṃ karoti na sāmno hīyate nainaṃ sāmāpahate
PB  ya enam anuvyāharati sa ārtim ārchati
PB  ūrg asy ūrjodā ūrjaṃ me dehy ūrjaṃ me dhehy annaṃ me dehy annaṃ me dhehi
prajāpater vā etad udaraṃ yat sada ūrg udumbaro yad audumbarī madhye sadaso mīyate
madhyata eva tat prajābhyo 'nnam ūrjaṃ dadhāti
PB  tasmād yatraiṣā yātayāmā kriyate tat prajā aśanāyavo bhavanti
PB  sāma devānām annaṃ sāmany eva tad devebhyo 'nna ūrhaṃ dadhāti sa eva tad ūrji śritaḥ prajābhya ūrjaṃ vibhajati
PB  udaṅṅ āsīna udgāyaty udīcīṃ tādṛśam ūrjā bhājayati pratyaṅṅ āsīnaḥ prastauti
pratīcīṃ tādṛśam ūrjā bhājayati dakṣiṇāsīnaḥ pratiharati dakṣiṇāṃ tādṛśam ūrjā bhājayati
prāñco 'nya ṛtvija ārtvijyaṃ kurvanti tasmād eṣā diśāṃ vīryavattamaitāṃ hi bhūyiṣṭhāḥ prīṇanti
PB  brahmavādino vadanti kasmāt satyāt prāñco 'nya ṛtvija ārtvijyaṃ kurvantīti
viparikramyodgātāra iti diśām abhīṣṭyai diśām abhiprītyā iti brūyāt tasmāt sarvāsu
dikṣv annaṃv vidyate sarvā hy abhīṣṭāḥ prītāḥ
PB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti so 'śocat tasya śocata ādityo
mūrdhno 'sṛjyata so 'sya mūrdhānam udahan sa droṇakalaśo 'bhavat tasmin devāḥ śukram
agṛhṇata tāṃ vai sa āyuṣārtim atyajīvat
PB  āyuṣārtim atijīvati ya evaṃv veda 
PB  raṃ prohed vānaspatyo 'si bārhaspatyo 'si prājāpatyo 'si prajāpater mūrdhāsy atyāyupātram asīdam ahaṃ māṃ prāñcaṃ prohāmi tejase
PB  yad āha vānaspatya iti satyenaivainaṃ tat prohati
PB  yad āha bārhaspatya iti bṛhaspatir vai devānām udgātā tam eva tad yunakti
 PB  yad āha prājāpatya iti prājāpatyo hy eṣa devatāyā yad droṇakalaśo yad āha prajāpater mūrdheti prajāpater hy eṣa mūrdhna udahanyata 
PB  yad āhātyāyupātram ity ati hy etad anyāni pātrāṇi yad droṇakalaśo devapātraṃ droṇakalaśaḥ
PB  devapātrī bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  brāhmaṇaṃ pātre na mīmāṃseta yaṃ brāhmaṇam iva manyate pra devapātram āpnoti na manuṣyapātrāc chidyate
PB  vāg vai devebhyo 'pakrāmat sāpaḥ prāviśat tāṃ devāḥ punar ayācaṃs tā
abruvan yat punar dadyāma kiṃ nas tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayadhva ity abruvaṃs tā abruvan
yad evāsmāsu manuṣyā apūtaṃ praveśayāṃs tenāsaṃsṛṣṭā asāmeti
PB  śuddhā asmā āpaḥ pūtā bhavanti ya evaṃv veda
PB  sā punartātyakrāmat sā vanaspatīn prāviśat tān devāḥ punar ayācaṃs tāṃ
na punar adadus tān aśapan svena vaḥ kiṣkuṇā vajreṇa vṛścān iti tasmād vanaspatīn
svena kiṣkuṇā vajreṇa vṛścanti devaśaptā hi
 PB  tāṃv vanaspatayaś caturdhā vācaṃv vinyadadhur dundubhau vīṇāyām akṣe tūṇave tasmād eṣā vadiṣṭhaiṣā valgutamā vāg vā vanaspatīnāṃ  
devānāṃ hy eṣā vāg āsīt 
 PB  adho'dho 'kṣaṃ droṇakalaśaṃ prohanti tasyā vāco 'varudhyā uparyupary akṣaṃ pavitraṃ prayacchanty ubhayata eva vācaṃ parigṛhṇanti 
PB  yasya kāmayetāsuryam asya yajñaṃ kuryāṃv vācaṃv vṛñjīyeti droṇakalaśaṃ
prohan bāhubhyām akṣan upaspṛśed asuryam asya yajñaṃ karoti vācaṃv vṛṅkte yo 'sya
priyaḥ syād anupaspṛśann akṣaṃ prohet prāṇā vai droṇakalaśaḥ prāṇān evāsya kalpayati
PB  yan nv ity āhur vācānyān ṛtvijo vṛṇate kasmād udgātāro vṛtā ārtvijyaṃ kurvantīti
PB  yad droṇakalaśam upasīdanti tenodgātāro vṛtāḥ
PB  prājāpatyā vā udgātāraḥ prājāpatyo droṇakalaśo droṇakalaśa evainām ārtvijyāya vṛṇīte
PB  prāñca upasīdanti prāñco yajñasyāgre karavāmeti
PB  anabhijitā vā eṣodgātṝṇāṃ dig yat prācī yad droṇakalaśaṃ prāñcaṃ prohanti diśo 'bhijityai
PB  yan nv ity āhur antarāśvaḥ prāsevau yujyate 'ntarā śamya anaḍvān ka udgātṝṇāṃ
yoga iti yad droṇakalaśam upasīdanti sa eṣāṃ yogas tasmād yuktair evopasadyaṃ na hy ayukto vahati
 PB  grāvṇaḥ saṃsādya droṇakalaśam adhyūhanti viḍ vai grāvāṇo 'nnaṃ somo rāṣṭraṃ droṇakalaśo yad grāvasu droṇakalaśam adhyūhanti viśy  
eva tad rāṣṭram adhyūhanti 
 PB  yaṃ dviṣyād vimukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvedam aham amum amuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyā viśo 'muṣmād annādyān nirūhāmīti nirūhed viśa  
evainam annādyān nirūhati 
 PB  yo 'sya priyaḥ syāt saṃmukhān grāvṇaḥ kṛtvedam aham amuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram amuṣyāṃ viśy amuṣinn annādye 'dhyūhāmīty adhyūhed  
viśy evainam annādye 'dhyūhati 
PB  atho tad ubhayam anādṛtyedam ahaṃ māṃ tejasi brahmavarcasse 'dhyūhāmīty adhyūhet tejasy eva brahmavarcasa ātmānam adhyūhati
PB  yaḥ kāmayeta viśā rāṣṭraṃ hanyām iti vyūhya grāvṇo 'dho droṇakalaśaṃ sādayitvopāṃśusavanam
upariṣṭād abhinidadhyād idam aham amuyā viśā 'do rāṣṭraṃ hanmīti viśaiva tad rāṣṭraṃ hanti
PB  yo vai daivāni pavitrāṇi veda pūto yajñiyo bhavati cchandāṃsi vai daivāni pavitrāṇi tair droṇakalaśaṃ pāvayanti
PB  vasavas tvā gāyatreṇa cchandasā punantu rudrās tvā traiṣṭubhena cchandasā
punantv ādityās tvā jāgatena cchandasā punantv etāni vai daivāni pavitrāṇi pūto yajñiyo
bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  svarbhānur vā āsura ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat taṃ devā na vyajānaṃs te 'trim
upādhāvaṃs tasyātrir bhāsena tamo 'pāhan yat prathamam apāhan sā kṛṣṇāvir abhavad
yad dvitīyaṃ sā rajatā yat tṛtīyaṃ sā lohinī yayā varṇam abhyatṛṇat sā śuklāsīt
PB  tasmāc chuklaṃ pavitraṃ śukraḥ somaḥ sa śukratvāya
PB  yaṃ dviṣyāt tasyaiteṣāṃ varṇānām api pavitre kuryāt pāpmanaivainaṃ tamasā
vidhyati kṛṣṇam iva hi tamo yo 'sya priyaḥ syād āsaktiśuklaṃ kuryāj jyotir vai hiraṇyaṃ
jyotir evāsmin dadhāti
PB  tasmād ātreyaṃ candreṇecchanty atrir hi tasya jyotiḥ
PB  abhyatṛṇat pavitraṃv vigṛhṇanti hastakāryam eva tad yajñasya kriyata etad vā udgātṝṇāṃ hastakāryaṃ yat pavitrasya vigrahaṇam
PB  na hastaveṣyān nir ṛcchati ya evaṃv veda
PB  yo 'pi na vigṛhṇāti prāṇād enam antaryanti
PB  taṃ brūyād vepamānaḥ prameṣyasa iti vepamāna eva pramīyate
PB  pra śukraitu devī manīṣāsmad rathaḥ sutaṣṭo na vājīty udgātā dhārām anumantrayate
 PB  āyuṣe me pavasva varcase me pavasva viduḥ pṛthivyā divo janitrāc chṛṇvantv āpo 'dhaḥ kṣarantīḥ somehodgāyety āha mahyaṃ tejase 
PB  eṣa vai somasyodgītho yat pavate somodgītham eva sāma gāyati
PB  ācchinnaṃ pāvayanti yajñaṃ caiva prāṇāṃś ca saṃtanvanti saṃtataṃ pāvayanti yajñasya saṃtatyai
PB  bṛhaspatir vai devānām udagāyat taṃ rakṣāṃsy ajighāṃsan sa ya eṣāṃ lokānām adhipatayas tān bhāgadheyenopādhāvat
PB  sūryo mā divābhyo nāṣṭrābhyaḥ pātu vāyur antarikṣābhyo 'gniḥ pārthivābhyaḥ svāheti juhoti
PB  ete vā eṣāṃ lokānām adhipatayas tān bhāgadheyenopāsarat
PB  karoti vācā vīryaṃ na sadasyām ārtim ārcchati ya evaṃv veda
PB  vāg vai devebhyo 'pākrāmat tāṃ devā anvamantrayanta sā 'bravīd abhāgāsmi
bhāgadheyaṃ me 'stv iti kas te bhāgadheyaṃ kuryād ity udgātāra ity abravīd udgātāro
vai vāce bhāgadheyaṃ kurvanti
 PB  tasyai juhuyād bekurānāmāsi juṣṭā devebhyo namo vāce namo vācas pataye devi vāg yat te vāco madhumat tasmin mā dhāḥ sarasvatyai 
PB  vāh vai sarasvatī tām eva tad bhāgadheyenārabhate
PB  yaṃ dviṣyāt tasyaitām āhutiṃ juhuyād vācaṃ manasā dhyāyed vācam evāsya vṛṅkte
PB  bahiṣpavamānaṃ sarpanti svargam eva tal lokaṃ sarpanti
PB  prakvāṇā iva sarpanti pratikūlam iva hītaḥ svargo lokaḥ tsaranta iva sarpanti mṛgadharmo vai yajño yajñasya śāntyā apratrāsāya
PB  vācaṃ yacchanti yajñam eva tad yacchanti yad vyavavadeyur yajñaṃ nirbrūyus tasmān na vyavavadyam
PB  pañcartvijaḥ saṃrabdhāḥ sarpanti pānkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam eva saṃtanvanti
PB  yadi prastotāvacchidyate yajñasya śiraś chidyate brahmaṇe varaṃ dattvā sa eva punar vartavyaś chinnam eva tat pratidadhāti
PB  yady udgātāvacchidyate yajñena yajamāno vyṛdhyate 'dakṣiṇaḥ sa yajñakratuḥ saṃsthāpyo 'thānya āhṛtyas tasmin deyaṃ yāvad dāsyan
 PB  yadi pratihartā 'vacchidyate paśubhir yajamāno vyṛdhyate paśavo vai pratihartā sarvavedasaṃ deyaṃ yadi sarvavedasaṃ na dadāti sarvajyāniṃ 
PB  adhvaryuḥ prastaraṃ harati
PB  yajamāno vai prastaro yajamānam eva tat svargaṃl lokaṃ harati
PB  yajño vai devebhyo 'śvo bhūtvāpākrāmat taṃ devāḥ prastareṇāsamayaṃs tasmād
aśvaḥ prastareṇa saṃmṛjyamāna upāvarabhate yad adhvaryuḥ prastaraṃ harati yajñasya śāntyā apratrāsāya
PB  prajāpatiḥ paśun asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā aśanāyanto 'pākrāmaṃs tebhyaḥ
prastaram annaṃ prāyacchat enam upāvartanta tasmād adhvaryuṇā prastara īṣad iva vidhūyo
vidhūtim iva hi tṛṇaṃ paśava upāvartante
PB  upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃv veda
PB  prastaram āsadyodgāyed dhaviṣo 'skandāya
PB  yajamānaṃ tu svargāl lokā avagṛhṇāti
PB  aṣṭhīvatopaspṛśatodgeyaṃ tenāsya havir askannaṃ bhavati na yajamānaṃ svargāl lokād avagṛhṇāti
PB  cātvālam avekṣya bahiṣpavamānaṃ stuvanty atra vā asāv āditya āsīt ta
devā bahiṣpavamānena svargaṃl lokam aharan yac cātvālam avekṣya bahiṣpavamānaṃ stuvanti
yajamānam eva tat svargaṃl lokaṃ haranti
PB  sa tu vai yajñena yajetety āhur yasya virājaṃ yajñamukhe dadhyur iti
PB  navabhiḥ stuvanti hiṅkāro daśamo daśākṣarā virāḍ virājam evāsya yajñamukhe dadhāti
PB  navabhiḥ stuvanti prāṇāḥ prāṇair evainaṃ samarddhayanti hiṅkāro daśamas tasmān nābhir anavatṛṇṇā daśamī prāṇānām
PB  navabhiḥ stuvanti navādhvaryuḥ prātaḥsavane grahān gṛhṇāti tān eva tat pāvayanti teṣāṃ prāṇān utsṛjanti
PB  prajāpatir vai hiṅkāras trayo bahiṣpavamānyo yad dhiṅkṛtya prastauti mithunam evāsyā yajñamukhe dadhāti prajananāya
PB  eṣa vai stomasya yogo yad dhiṅkāro yad dhiṅkṛtya prastauti yuktenaiva stomena prastauti
PB  eṣa vai sāmnāṃ raso yad dhiṅkāro yad dhiṅkṛtya prastauti rasenaivaitā abhyudya prastauti
PB  āraṇyebhyo vā etat paśubhyaḥ stuvanti yad bahiṣpavamānam ekārūpābhiḥ stuvanti tasmād ekarūpā āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  parācībhiḥ stuvanti tasmāt parāñcaḥ prajāyante parāñco vitiṣṭhante
PB  apariśrite stuvanti tasmād aparigṛhītā āraṇyāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  bahiḥ stuvanty antar anuśaṃsanti tasmād grāmam āhṛtair bhuñjate
PB  grāmebhyo vā etat paśubhyaḥ stuvanti yad ājyair nānārūpaiḥ stuvanti tasmān nānārūpā grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  punarabhyāvartaṃ stuvanti tasmāt pretvaryaḥ pretya punar āyanti
PB  pariśrite stuvanti tasmāt parigṛhītā grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  amuṣmai vā etal lokāya stuvanti yad bahiṣpavamānaṃ sakṛd dhiṅkṛtābhiḥ parācībhiḥ stuvanti sakṛd dhīto 'sau parāṅ lokaḥ
PB  asmai vā etal lokāya stuvanti yad ājyaiḥ punarabhyāvartaṃ stuvanti tasmād ayaṃl lokaḥ punaḥpunaḥ prajāyate
PB  parāñco vā eteṣāṃ prāṇā bahvantīty āhur ye parācībhir bahiṣpavamānībhiḥ stuvata ity āvatīm uttamāṃ gāyet prāṇānāṃ dhṛtyai
 PB  cyavante vā ete 'smāl lokād ity āhur ye parācībhir bahiṣpavamānībhiḥ stuvata iti rathantaravarṇam uttamāṃ gāyed iyaṃ vai rathantaram  
asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati 
PB  upāsmai gāyata nara iti grāmakāmāyapratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  naro vai devānāṃ grāmo grāmam evāsmā upākaḥ
PB  upa vā annamannam evāsmā upākaḥ
PB  upoṣu jātam apturam iti prajākāmāya pratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  upa vai prajā tāṃ jātam ity evājījanat
PB  sa naḥ pasvasya śaṃ gava iti pratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  yāṃ samāṃ mahādevaḥ paśūn hanyāt sa naḥ pavasva śaṃ gava iti catuṣpade bheṣajaṃ karoti
PB  śaṃ janāyeti dvipade śam arvata ity ekaśaphāya
PB  viṣeṇa vai tāṃ samām oṣadhayo 'ktā bhavanti yāṃ samāṃ mahādevaḥ paśūn
hanti yac chaṃ rājann oṣadhībhya ity āhauṣadhīr evāsmai svadayaty ubhayyo 'smai svaditāḥ
pacyante 'kṛṣṭapacyāś ca kṛṣṭapacyāś ca
PB  pavasva vāco agriya iti pratipadaṃ kuryād yaṃ kāmayeta samānānāṃ śīreṣṭhaḥ syād iti
PB  pavasva vāco agriya ity agram evainaṃ pariṇayati
PB  śrīr vai vāco 'graṃ śriyam evāsmin dadhāti
PB  ete asṛgram indava iti bahubhyaḥ pratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  eta iti sarvān evainān ṛddhyai bhūtyā abhivadati
 PB  eta iti vai prajāpatir devān asṛjatāsṛgram iti manuṣyān indava iti pitṝṃs tiraḥ pavitra iti grahān āśava iti stotraṃv viśvānīti  
śastram abhi saubhagety anyāḥ prajāḥ 
PB  yad eta iti tasmād yāvanta evāgre devās tāvanta idānīm
PB  sarvān vṛddhim ārdhnuvaṃ sthiteva hy eṣā vyāhṛtiḥ
PB  yad asṛgram iti tasmān manuṣyāḥ śvaḥśvaḥ sṛjyante
PB  yad indava itīndava iva hi pitaraḥ
PB  mana iva
PB  yāntāḥ prajāḥ sṛṣṭā ṛddhim ārdhnuvaṃs tām ṛdhnuvanti yeṣām evaṃv vidvān etāṃ pratipadaṃ karoti
PB  chandāṃsi vai somam āharaṃs taṃ gandharvo viśvāvasuḥ paryamuṣṇāt tenāpaḥ
prāviśat taṃ devatā anvaicchaṃs taṃ viṣṇur apsu paryapaśyat sa vyakāṅkṣad ayaṃ nū
nā iti taṃ padā prāsphurat tasmāt pṛthag indavo 'sṛjyanta sa devatābhyo 'bhitas
tiṣṭhantībhya ete asṛgram indava iti prābravīd bahiṣpavamānena vai yajñaḥ sṛjyate
yad ete asṛgram indava iti prastauti yajñam eva tat sṛṣṭaṃ devatābhyaḥ prāha
PB  vyṛddhaṃ vā etad apaśavyaṃ yat prātaḥsavanam aniḍaṃ hi yad iḍām asmabhyaṃ saṃyatam ity āha prātaḥsavanam eva tad iḍāvat paśumat
PB  davidyūtatyā ruceti vrātāya pratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  davidyūtatyā receti vai gāyatryā rūpaṃ pariṣṭobhantyeti triṣṭubhaḥ kṛpety
anuṣṭubhaḥ somāḥ śukrā gavāśira iti jagatyāḥ sarveṣāṃ vā eṣā cchandasāṃ rūpaṃ cchandāṃsīva
khalu vai vratopadeṣā pratipad bhavati svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
PB  vṛddhā vā eta indriyeṇa vīryeṇa yad vrāta indriyaṃ vīryaṃ chandāṃsīndriyeṇaivainān vīryeṇa samardhayati
PB  agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti pratipadaṃ kuryād yeṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate
PB  apūtā iva vā ete yeṣāṃ dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate yady eṣāgnipāvamānī pratipad bhavaty agnir evainān niṣṭapati pavamānaḥ punāti
PB  yad āyūṃṣīty āha ya eva jīvanti teṣv āyur dadhāti
PB  ā no mitrāvaruṇeti jyogāmayāvine pratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  apakrāntau vā etasya prāṇāpānau yasya jyog āmayati prāṇāpānau mitrāvaruṇau prāṇāpānāv evāsmin dadhāti
PB  apaghnan pavate mṛdho 'pa somo arāvṇa ity anṛtam abhiśasyamānāya pratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  arāvāṇo vā ete ye 'nṛtam abhiśaṃsanti tān evāsmād apahanti
PB  gacchann indrasya niṣkṛtam iti pūtam evainaṃ yajñiyam indrasya niṣkṛtaṃ gamayati
PB  vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti rājanyāya pratipadaṃ kuryād vṛṣā vai rājanyo vṛṣāṇam evainaṃ karoti
PB  marutvate ca matsara iti maruto vai devānāṃ viśo viśam evāsmā anu niyunakty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
PB  viśvā dadhāna ojasety ojasaivāsmai vīryeṇa viśaṃ purastāt parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
PB  pavasvendo vṛṣāsuta iti pratipadaṃ kuryād yaḥ kāmayeta jane ma ṛdhyeteti
PB  kṛdhī no yaśaso jana iti janatāyām evāsmā ṛdhyate
PB  yuvaṃ hi sthaḥ svaḥ patī iti dvābhyāṃ pratipadaṃ kuryāt samāvadbhājāv evainau yajñasya karoty ubhau yajñayaśasenārpayati
PB  prāsya dhārā akṣarann iti vṛṣṭikāmāya pratipadaṃ kuryāt
PB  prāsya dhārā akṣarann iti divo vṛṣṭiṃ cyāvayati vṛṣṇaḥ sutasyaujasa ity antarikṣāt
PB  devāṃ anu prabhūṣata ity asmin loke pratiṣṭhāpayati
 PB  ojasā vā etad vīryeṇa pradīyate yad aprattaṃ bhavati yad vṛṣṇaḥ sutasyaujasa ity āhaujasaivāsmai vīryeṇa divo vṛṣṭiṃ prayacchati 
PB  tayā pavasva dhārayā yayā gāva ihāgamañ janyāsa up no gṛham iti pratipadaṃ
kuryād yaḥ kāmayetopa mā janyā gāvo nameyur vindeta me janyā gā rāṣṭram iti yad eṣā
pratipad bhavaty upainaṃ janyā gāvo namanti vindate 'sya janyā gā rāṣṭram
PB  ime vai lokā gāyatraṃ tryāvṛd geyaṃ trayo hīme lokā yat tryāvṛd gāyaty ebhir evainaṃ lokaiḥ saṃmimīte
PB  dvir avanarded dhiṅ kuryāt tṛtīyam
PB  yat trir avanardaty ati tad gāyatraṃ recayati
PB  yo vai gāyatreṇāpratihṛtenodgāyaty apratiṣṭhāno bhavati hiṅkāro vai gāyatrasya pratihāraḥ
PB  sa manasā dhyeyaḥ pratihṛtena gāyatreṇodgāyati pratitiṣṭhati
PB  yo vā ebhyo lokebhyo gāyatraṃ gāyati naibhyo lokebhya āvṛścyata ima enaṃ lokā ūrjjābhisaṃvasate
PB  mandram ivāgra ādadītātha tārataram atha tāratamaṃ tad ebhyo lokebhyo 'gāsīt
PB  aniruktaṃ geyam etad vai gāyatrasya krūraṃ yan niruktaṃ yad aniruktaṃ gāyati krūram evāsya parivṛṇakti
PB  prāṇo gāyatraṃ na vyavānyāt prāṇasyāvicchedāya yadi vyavāniti pramāyuko bhavati yadi na vyavāniti sarvam āyur eti
PB  yadi vyavānyān madhya ṛco vyavānyāt prāṇo vai gāyatraṃ prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇam eva tan madhyata ātman dadhāti sa sarvam āyur eti
PB  iḍāṃ paśukāmāya nidhanaṃ kuryāt svaḥ svargakāmāya yaśo brahmavarcasakāmāyāyur āmayāvine haṃsīty abhicarate
PB  ete vai gāyatrasya dohāḥ
PB  brahmavarcasasī paśumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
 PB  prajāpatir devebhya ātmānaṃ yajñaṃ kṛtvā prāyacchat te 'nyo 'nyasmā agrāya nātiṣṭhanta tān abravīd ājim asminn iteti ta ājim āyan  
yad ājim āyaṃs tad ājyānām ājyatvam 
PB  sa indro 'ved agnir vā idam agra ujjyeṣyatīti so 'bravīd yataro nāv idam
agra ujjayat tan nau saheti so 'gnir agra udajayad atha mitrāvaruṇāv athendro 'thaiṣaikā
hotrānujjitāsīt sa indro 'gnim abravīd yat sahāvocāvahī yan nau tad iti saiṣaindrāgny
adhyardham agne stotram adhyardham indrasya
PB  catvāri santi ṣaḍ devatyāni
PB  ṣaḍdhā vihito yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhate
PB  sarvāṇi svārāṇy ājyāni taj jāmi nānādevatyaiḥ stuvanty ajāmitāyai
 PB  grāmyebhyo vā etat paśubhyaḥ stuvanti yad ājyaiḥ punarabhyāvartaṃ stuvanti tasmāt parāñcaḥ prājyante pratyañcaḥ prajāyante tasmād  
u pretya punar āyanti 
PB  etāvatā vāva mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ pupuve
PB  tribhiś ca cchandobhiḥ pañcabhiś ca sāmabhiḥ
PB  yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti mādhyandinam eva tat savanaṃ pāvayanti
PB  etāvanti vāva sarvāṇi sāmāni yāvanti mādhyandine pavamāne
PB  gāyatraṃ nidhanavad anidhanam aiḍam
PB  yan mādhyandinena pavamānena stuvanti sarvair eva tat sāmabhiḥ stuvanti
PB  ātmā vai yajñasya pavamāno mukhaṃ gāyatrī prāṇo gāyatraṃ yad gāyatryāṃ gāyatreṇa stuvanti mukhata eva tat prāṇān dadhati
PB  prāṇāpānā vā etāni cchandāṃsi prāṇo gāyatrī vyāno bṛhaty apānas triṣṭub yad etaiś chandobhiḥ stuvanti prāṇāpānānām avicchedāya
 PB  ime vai lokā etāni cchandāṃsy ayam eva gāyatry ayaṃ madhyamo bṛhaty asāv uttamas triṣṭub yad etaś chandobhiḥ saṃhitaiḥ stuvanty  
eṣāṃ lokānām avicchedāya 
PB  yad anyac chando 'ntarā vyaveyād imāṃl lokān vicchindyāt
PB  gāyatreṇa stutvā nidhanavatā stuvantīyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva tad āyatanaṃ kriyate
PB  yad anidhanenāgre stuyur anāyatano yajamānaḥ syāt
PB  nidhanavatā stuvanti vīryaṃ vai gāyatrī vīryaṃ nidhanaṃ vīryeṇaiva tad vīryaṃ samardhayati
PB  aiḍena bṛhatīm ārabhante
PB  paśavo vā iḍā paśavo bṛhatī paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti
PB  bṛhatyāṃ bhūyiṣṭhāni sāmāni bhavanti
PB  tatrāpi triṇidhanam
PB  abaliṣṭha iva vā ayaṃ madhyami lokas tasyaiva tad āyatanaṃ kriyate
PB  triṇidhanaṃ bhavati trīṇi savanānāṃ chidrāṇi tāni tenāpidhīyante
PB  triṇidhanaṃ bhavati traya ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
 PB  triṇidhanaṃ bhavaty etena vai mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ yat triṇidhanaṃ na syād apratiṣṭhitaṃ mādhyandinaṃ  
savanaṃ syāt 
PB  dvyakṣarāṇi nidhanāni bhavanti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣthāpayati
PB  anidhanam antato bhavati svargasya lokasyānatipādāya
PB  yan nidhanavat syād yajamānaṃ svargāl lokān nirhanyāt
PB  svāraṃ bhavati
PB  svareṇa vai devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ prayacchati
PB  gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥ
PB  prāṇo vai gāyatraṃ prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇān evatad ubhayato dadhāti tasmād ubhayataḥ prāṇāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  yad gāyatraṃ purastād bhavati svāram antataḥ prāṇair eva praity apāne pratitiṣṭhati
PB  etad vai yajñasya svargyaṃ yan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ mādhyandinasya pavamānaḥ
pavamānasya bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante svargasyaiva tal lokasyāyatane dīyante
PB  devā vai cchandāṃsy abruvan yuṣmābhiḥ svargyaṃl lokam ayāmeti te gāyatrīṃ
prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvaṃs triṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayā na vyāpnuvañ jagatīṃ prāyuñjata
tayā na vyāpnuvann anuṣṭubhaṃ prāyuñjata tayālpakādi na vyāpnuvaṃs ta āsāṃ diśāṃ
rasān prabṛhya catvāry akṣarāṇy upādadhuḥ sā bṛhaty abhavat tayemāṃl lokān vyāpnuvan
PB  bṛhatī maryā yayemāṃl lokān vyāpāmeti tad bṛhatyā bṛhattvam
PB  paśūn vā asyāntān upādadhuḥ paśavo vai bṛhatī yad bṛhatyāḥ stotre dakṣiṇā dīyante sva eva tad āyatane dīyante
PB  yan nv ity āhur anyāni cchandāṃsi varṣīyāṃsi kasmād bṛhaty ucyata eṣā
hīmāṃl lokān vyāpnon nānyac chandaḥ kiṃ cana yāni sapta caturuttarāṇi cchandāṃsi
tāni bṛhatīm abhisaṃpadyante tasmād bṛhaty ucyate
 PB  yan nv ity āhur gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ jāgataṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ kasmād bṛhatyā madhyandine stuvantīti 
PB  bahiṣpavamānena vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃl lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃ
bṛhatyā madhyandine 'stabhnuvaṃs tasmād bṛhatyā madhyandinaṃ stuvanty ādityaṃ hy
eṣā madhyandine dādhāra
PB  yair u kaiś ca cchandobhir madhyandine stuvanti tāni triṣṭubham abhi saṃpadyante tasmāt triṣṭubho nayanti mādhyandināt savanāt
PB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa śocann amahīyamāno 'tiṣṭhat
sa etad āmahīyavam apaśyat tenemāḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā amahīyanta yad amahīyanta tasmād āmahīyavam
PB  tā asmāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tāsāṃ divi sad bhūmy ādada iti prāṇān ādatta
tā enaṃ prāṇeṣv ātteṣu punar upāvartanta tābhya ugraṃ śarma mahi śrava iti punaḥ
prāṇān prāyacchat tā asmād ud evāyodhaṃs tāsāṃ stauṣa iti manyūn avāśṛṇāt tato vai
tasmai tāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta
PB  tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃv veda
PB  prajānāṃ ca vā eṣā sṛṣṭiḥ pāpavasīyaś ca vidhṛtir yad āmahīyavam
PB  vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  devā vai yaśaskāmāḥ sattram āsatāgnir indro vāyur makhas te 'bruvsn yan
no yaśa ṛcchāt tan naḥ sahāsad iti teṣā makhaṃ yaśa ārcchat tad ādāyāpākrāmat tad
asya prāsahāditsanta taṃ paryayatanta svadhanuḥ pratiṣṭhābhyātiṣṭhat tasya dhanurārtnir
ūrdhvā patitvā śiro 'cchinat sa pravargyo 'bhavad yajño vai makho yat pravargyaṃ
pravṛñjanti yajñasyaiva tac chiraḥ pratidadhati
PB  tad devā yaśo vyabhajanta tasyāgnī rauravaṃ prābṛhata
PB  tad vai sa paśuvīryaṃ prābṛhata paśavo vai rauravam
PB  paśumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  agnir vai rūras tasyaitad rauravam
 PB  asurā vai devān paryayatanta tata etāv agnī rūrau viṣvañcau stobhāv apaśyat tābhyām enān pratyauṣat te pratyuṣyamāṇā aravanta yad
