aravanta tasmād rauravam 
PB  athendro yaudhājayaṃ prābṛhata tad vai sa vajraṃ prābṛhata vajro vai yaudhājayam
PB  vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati ya evaṃv veda
PB  indro vai yudhājit tasyaitad yaudhājayam
PB  yudhā maryā ajaiṣmeti tasmād yaudhājayam
PB  atha vāyur auśanaṃ prābṛhata
PB  tad vai sa prāṇvīryaṃ prābṛhata prāṇā vā auśanam
PB  sarvam āyur eti ya evaṃv veda
PB  vāyur vā uśanaṃs tasyaitad auśanam
 PB  uśanā vai kāvyo 'surāṇāṃ purohita āsīt taṃ devāḥ kāmadughābhir apāmantrayanta tasmā etāny auśanāni prāyacchan kāmadughā vā auśanāni 
PB  kāmadughā enam upatiṣṭhante ya evaṃv veda
PB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa tūṣṇīṃ manasādhyāyat tasya yan manasy āsīt tad bṛhat samabhavat
PB  sa ādadhīta garbho vai me 'yam antarhitas taṃv vācā prajanayā iti
PB  sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sā vāg rathantaram anvapadyata
PB  ratham aryāḥ kṣeplātārīd iti tad rathantarasya rathantaratvam
PB  tato bṛhad anu prājāyata bṛhan maryā idaṃ sa jyog antarabhūd iti tad bṛhato bṛhattvam
PB  yathā vai putro jyeṣṭha evaṃ bṛhat prajāpateḥ
PB  jyeṣṭhabrāhmaṇaṃ vā etat
PB  pra jyaiṣṭhyam āpnoti ya evaṃv veda
PB  yan nv ity āhur bṛhat pūrvaṃ prajāpatau samabhavat kasmād rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśa iti
PB  bṛhad eva pūrvaṃ samabhavad rathantaraṃ tu pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭyāsṛjata tasmāt pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe
 PB  tayoḥ samānaṃ nidhanam āsīt tasmin nātiṣṭhetāṃ ta ājim aitāṃ tayor has iti bṛhat prāṇam udajayad as iti rathantaram apānam abhisamaveṣṭata 
PB  prāṇāpānau vai bṛhadrathantare jyog āmayāvina ubhe kuryād apakrāntau vā etasya prāṇāpānau yasya jyog āmayati prāṇāpānāv evāsmin
PB  yan nv ity āhur ubhe bṛhadrathantare bahirṇidhane kasmād bṛhad bahirṇidhanāni bhajate 'ntarṇidhanāni rathantaram iti
PB  prāṇo bṛhat tasmād bahirṇidhanāni bhajate bahir hi prāṇo 'pāno rathantaraṃ tasmād antarṇidhanāni bhajate 'ntar hy apānaḥ
PB  mahāvṛkṣau vai bṛhadrathantare nidhanena samarpye
PB  yad vai mahāvṛkṣau samṛcchete bahu tatra vibhagnaṃ prabhagnaṃ śete
PB  airaṃ vai bṛhad aiḍaṃ rathantaraṃ mano vai bṛhad vāg rathantaraṃ sām
a vai bṛhad ṛg rathantaraṃ prāṇo vai bṛhad apāno rathantaram asau vai loko bṛhad
ayaṃ rathantaram etāni manasānvīkṣyodgāyet kḷptābhyām evābhyām udgāyati
PB  paśavo vai bṛhadrathantare aṣṭākṣareṇa prathamāyā 
ṛcaḥ prastauty aṣṭāśaphāṃs tat paśūn avarundhe
PB  dvyakṣareṇottarayor ṛcoḥ prastauti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  pañcākṣareṇa rathantarasya pratiharati pāṅktāṃs tat paśūn avarundhe
PB  caturakṣareṇa bṛhataḥ pratiharati catuṣpadas tat paśūn avarundhe
PB  na vai bṛhan na rathantaram ekaṃ chando 'yacchat tataḥ kakubhāv uttare
upādadhus tasmād bṛhatī prathamā kakubhāv uttare tasmād bṛhadrathantare ekarcena
kurvanti na hi te ekaṃ chando 'yacchat
PB  nava bṛhato rohān rohati nava prāṇāḥ prāṇān evāvarundhe
PB  trīn prathamāyāṃ rohati bhūtaṃ bhavad bhaviṣyat tān evāvarundhe trīn madhyamāyāṃ
rohaty ātmānaṃ prajāṃ paśūṃs tān evāvarundhe trīn uttamāyāṃ rohati traya ime lokā
eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  sarvān kāmān avarundhe ya evaṃv vidvān bṛhato rohān rohati
 PB  vajreṇa vā etat prastotodgātāram abhipravartayati yad rathantaraṃ prastauti samudram antardhāyodgāyed vāg ity ādeyaṃv vāg vai samudraḥ  
samudram evāntardadhāty ahiṃsāyai 
PB  balavad geyaṃ vajram evaṃ pravṛttaṃ pratyudgṛhṇāti
PB  balvalā kurvatā geyam abhilobhayateva vajram evābhilobhayati
PB  kṣipraṃ geyaṃ svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
PB  devaratho vai rathantaram akṣareṇākṣareṇa pratiṣṭhāpayatodgeyam areṇāreṇa hi rathaḥ pratitiṣṭhati
PB  yo vai devaratham ananvālabhyātiṣṭhaty avāsmāt padyata iyaṃ vai devaratha imām ālabhyodgāyen nāsmād avapadyate
PB  īśvaraṃ vai rathantaram udgātuś cakṣuḥ pramathitoḥ prastuyamāne saṃmīlet svardṛśaṃ prativīkṣeta nainaṃ cakṣur jahāti
PB  prajananaṃ vai rathantaraṃ yat tasthuṣa ity āhāsthāyukodgātur vāg bhavaty
api prajananaṃ hanty asthuṣa iti vaktavyaṃ susthuṣa iti vā sthāyukodgātur vāg bhavati
na prajananam api hanti
PB  pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta tair devāḥ svargaṃl lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ rathantaraṃ mahimnā nāśaknod utpatat
PB  tasya vaśiṣṭho mahimno vinidhāya tena stutvā svargaṃl lokam ait tān saṃbhṛtyodgāyet
PB  yas te goṣu mahimā yas te apsu rathe vā te stanayitnau ya u te yas te agnau mahimā tena saṃbhava rathantara draviṇavan na edhi
PB  apo vā ṛtvyam ārcchat tāsāṃv vāyuḥ pṛṣṭhe vyavartata tato vasu vāmaṃ samabhavat
tasmin mitrāvaruṇau paryapaśyatāṃ tāv abrūtāṃv vāmaṃ maryā idaṃ deveṣv ājānīti tasmād vāmadevyam
 PB  tat parigṛhṇantāv abrūtām idam avidāvedaṃ nau mābhyartiḍhvam iti tat prajāpatir abravīn mad vā etad dhy ajani mama vā etad iti tad  
agnir abravīn māṃ  
vā etad annam ajani mama vā etad iti tad indro 'bravīc chreṣṭhasthā vā etad ahaṃ
vaḥ śreṣṭho 'smi mama vā etad iti tad viśve devā abruvann asmaddevatyaṃ vā etad yad
adbhyo 'dhi samabhūd asmākaṃ vā etad iti tat prajāpatir abravīt sarveṣāṃ na idam
astu sarva idam upajīvāmeti tat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadhuḥ sarvadevatyaṃ vai vāmadevyam
PB  yat kavatīṣu tena prājāpatyaṃ ko hi prajāpatir yad aniruktāsu tena prājāpatyam anirukto hi prajāpatiḥ
PB  yad gāyatrīṣu tenāgneyaṃ gāyatracchandā hy agniḥ
PB  yat pṛṣṭheṣu nyadadadhus tenaindraṃ sarvāṇi hi pṛṣṭhānīndrasya niṣkevalyāni
PB  yan maitrāvaruṇo 'nuśaṃsati tena maitrāvaruṇam
PB  yad bahudevatyam uttamaṃ padaṃ tena vaiśvadevaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  prajāpatir vā etāṃ gāyatrīṃ yonim apaśyat sa ādīdhītāsmād yoneḥ pṛṣṭhāni sṛjā iti
PB  sa rathantaram asṛjata tad rathasya ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
PB  sa bṛhad asṛjata tat stanayitnor ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata sa vairūpam asṛjata tad vā tasya ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
PB  sa vairūpam asṛjata tad agner ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
PB  sa śakvarīr asṛjata tad apāṃ ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
PB  sa revatīr asṛjata tad gavāṃ ghoṣo 'nvasṛjyata
PB  etair vā etāni saha ghoṣair asṛjyanta
PB  sarve 'smin ghoṣāḥ sarvāḥ puṇyā vāco vadanti ya evaṃv veda
PB  pitā vai vāmadevyaṃ putrāḥ pṛṣṭhāni
PB  etasmād vā etāni yoner asṛjyanta
PB  tasmāt pṛṣṭhānāṃ stotraṃ vāmadevyenānuṣṭuvanti śāntyai
PB  yad dhi putro 'śāntaṃ carati pitā tac chamayati
PB  ayaṃ vai loko madhyamo vāmadevyam etasmād vā imau lokau viṣvañcāv asṛjyetāṃ bṛhac ca ratantaraṃ ca
PB  yad rathantareṇa stuvanti ye rathantarāḥ paśavo 'ntarīkṣaṃ ta upaśrayanti
yad bṛhatā stuvanti ye bārhatāḥ paśavo 'ntarīkṣaṃ ta upaśrayanti te vāmadevyasya stotreṇāvaruddhāḥ
PB  dhruva āsīno vāmadevyenodgāyet paśūnām upavṛtyai
PB  upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃv veda
PB  antarikṣaṃ vai vāmadevyam adhūnvatevodgeyam adhūtam ivāntarikṣaṃ paśavo vai vāmadevyam ahiṃsatevodgeyaṃ paśūnām ahiṃsāyai
PB  katham iva vāmadevyaṃ geyam ity āhuḥ
PB  yathāṅkulī putrān saṃdaśyāsaṃbhindantī harati yathā vāto 'psu śanair vāti
PB  svadhūr vāmadevyaṃ geyam
PB  yo vai svadhūr vāmadevyaṃ gāyati svadhūr bhavati
PB  yāty asyānyo niyānena nānyasya niyānena yāti
PB  na bṛhato na rathantarasyānurūpaṃ geyaṃ svenaivāyatanena geyam āyatanavān bhavati
PB  devā vai paśūn vyabhajanta te rudram antarāyaṃs tān vāmadevyasya stotra upekṣate
PB  aniruktaṃ geyam
PB  yan nirāha rudrāya paśūn apidadhāti rudras tāṃ samāṃ paśūn dhātuko bhavati
PB  revatīṣu vāmadevyena paśukāmaḥ stuvīta
PB  āpo vai revatyaḥ paśavo vāmadevyam adbhya evāsmai paśūn prajanayati
PB  anavartiḥ paśuto bhavati prajā svasya mīliteva bhavati
PB  kavatībhyo hy eti prajāpateḥ
PB  imau vai lokau sahāstāṃ tau viyantāv abrūtāṃv vivāhaṃv vivahāvahai saha nāv astv iti
PB  tayor ayam amuṣmai śyaitaṃ prāyacchan naudhasam asāv asmai
PB  tata enayor nidhane viparyakrāmatāṃ devavivāho vai śyaitanaudhase
PB  pravasīyāṃsaṃ vivāham āpnoti ya evaṃv veda
PB  ito vā ime lokā ūrdhvāḥ kalpamānā yanty amuto 'rvāñcaḥ kalpamānā āyanti
 PB  yad rathantareṇa stuvantīmaṃl lokaṃ tena yunakty antarikṣaṃv vāmadevyena naudhasenāmuṃ yad bṛhatā stuvanty amuṃl lokaṃ tena yanakty  
antarikṣaṃv vāmadevyena śyaitenemam 
PB  kḷptān imāl lokān upāste ya evaṃv veda
PB  bṛhadrathantare vai śaitanaudhase yad rathantarāya naudhasaṃ prati prayuñjanti
bṛhad evāsmai tat prati prayuñjanti bṛhad dhy etat paro'kṣaṃ yan naudhasaṃ yad bṛhate
śyaitaṃ prati prayuñjanti rathantaram evāsmai tat prati prayuñjanti rathantaraṃ hy
etat paro'kṣaṃ yac chyaitam
PB  ubhabhyāṃ bṛhadrathantarābhyāṃ stute ya evaṃv veda
PB  devā vai brahma vyabhajanta tāṃ nodhāḥ kākṣīvata āgacchat te 'bruvann
ṛṣir na āgaṃs tasmai brahma dadāmeti tasmā etat sāma prāyacchaṃs tasmān naudhasaṃ
brahma vai naudhasam
PB  brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavati
PB  athaitac chyaitam
PB  prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān etena sāmnābhivyāharat
te 'smā atiṣṭhanta te śetyā abhavan yac chetyā abhavaṃs tasmāc chyaitaṃ paśavo vai śyaitam
PB  paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati
 PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā aśocaṃs tāḥ śyaitena huṃmā ity abhyajighrat tato vai tāḥ samaidhanta samedhante tāṃ samāṃ prajā  
yatraivaṃ vidvāñ chyaitenodgāyati 
PB  eṣa vai yajamānasya prajāpatir yad udgātā yac chyaitena hiṅ karoti prajāpatir eva bhūtvā prajā abhijihgrati
PB  vasunidhanaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vasu paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃv vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanam abhicaraṇīyasya brahmasāma kuryād abhinidhanaṃ mādhyandine pavamāne
PB  deveṣur vā eṣā yad vaṣatkāro 'bhīti vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharad abhītyevāsmai vajraṃ prahṛtya deveṣv ā vaṣaṭkāreṇa vidhyati
PB  traikakubhaṃ paśukāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt tvam aṅga praśaṃsiṣa ity etāsu
PB  indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta rāyovājo
bṛhadgiriḥ pṛthuraśmis te 'bruvan ko naḥ putrān bhariṣyantīty aham intīndro 'bravīt
tāṃs trikakub adhinidhāyācarat sa etat sāmāpaśyad yat trikakub apaśyat tasmāt traikakubham
PB  sa ātmānam eva punar upādhāvat tvam aṅga praśaṃsiṣo devaḥ śaviṣṭha martyaṃ
na tvad anyo maghavann asti ca marḍitendra bravīmi te vaca iti sa etena ca pragāthenaitena
sāmnā sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata tān ebhyaḥ prāyacchat te pratyatiṣṭhan
PB  yaḥ paśukāmaḥ syād yah pratiṣṭhākāma etasmin pragātha etena sāmnā stuvīta pra sahasraṃ paśūn āpnoti pratitiṣṭhati
PB  trivīryaṃ vā etat sāma trīndriyam aindrya ṛca aindraṃ sāmaindreti nidhanam indriya eva vīrye pratitiṣṭhati
PB  traiśokaṃ jyogāmayāvine brahmasāma kuryāt
PB  ime vai lokāḥ sahāsaṃs te 'śocantaṃs teṣām indra etena sāmnā śucam apāhan yat trayāṇāṃ śocatām apāhaṃs tasmāt traiśokam
PB  yāsmād apāhan sā puṃścalīṃ prāviśad yām antarikṣāt sā klībaṃ yām amuṣmāt sainasvinam
PB  tasmāt teṣāṃ nāśaitavyā ya eṣām āśāmeti tasmā eva śuco 'pabhajate
PB  śucā vā eṣa viddho yasya jyog āmayati yat traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavati śucam evāsmād apahanti
PB  diveti nidhanam upayanti vyuṣṭir vai divā vy evāsmai vāsayati
PB  āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ pratiṣṭhākāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt
PB  kaṇvo vā etat sāmarte nidhanam apaśyat sa na pratyatiṣṭhat sa vṛṣadaṃśasyāṣiti
kṣuvata upāśṛṇot sa tad eva nidhanam apaśyat tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhad yad etat sāma
bhavati pratiṣṭhityai
PB  vasiṣṭhasya janitraṃ prajākāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt
PB  vasiṣṭho vā etat putrahataḥ sāmāpaśyat sa prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyata yad etat sāma bhavati prajātyai
PB  ātharvaṇaṃ lokakāmāya brahmasāma kuryāt
PB  atharvāṇo vā etal lokākāmāḥ sāmāpaśyaṃs tenāmartyaṃl lokam apaśyan yad etat sāma bhavati svargasya lokasya prajātyai
PB  abhīvartaṃ bhrātṛvyavate brahmasāma kuryāt
PB  abhīvartena vai devā asurān abhyavartanta yad abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavati bhrātṛvyasyābhivṛtyai
PB  śrāyantīyaṃ yajñavibhraṣṭāya brahmasāma kuryāt
 PB  prajāpatir uṣasam adhyait svāṃ duhitaraṃ tasya retaḥ parāpatat tad asyāṃ nyaṣicyata tad aśrīṇād idaṃ me mā duṣad iti tat sad akarot  
paśūn eva 
PB  yac chrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati śrīṇāti caivenaṃ sac ca karoti
PB  devāś ca vā asurāś caiṣu lokeṣv aspardhanta te devāḥ prajāpatim upādhāvaṃs
tebhya etat sāma prāyacchad etenainān kālayiṣyaddham iti tenainān ebhyo lokebhyo
'kālayanta yad akālayanta tasmāt kāleyam
PB  ebhyo vai lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ kālayate ya evaṃv veda
PB  stomo vai deveṣu taro nāmāsīd yajño 'sureṣu vidadvasus te devās tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomena yajñam asurāṇām āvṛñjata
PB  stomena yajñaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃv veda
PB  sāhdyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te 'vacchidya tṛtīyasavanaṃ mādhyandinena savanena
saha svargaṃl lokam āyaṃs tad devāḥ lokeyena samatanvan yat kāleyaṃ bhavati tṛtīyasavanasya saṃtatyai
PB  vidadvasu vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti prastauti tṛtīyasavanam eva tad abhyativadati
PB  sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇi kāleyaṃ yat padaprastāvaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ yad bṛhato
rohān rohati tena bārhataṃ yat stobhavān pratihāras tena bārhataṃ yad dravadiḍaṃ
tena rāthantaraṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  sādhyā vai nāma devā āsaṃs te sarveṇa yajñena saha svargaṃl lokam āyaṃs
te devāśīchandāṃsy abruvan somam āharateti te jagatīṃ prāhiṇvan sā trīṇy akṣarāṇi
hitvaikākṣarā bhūtvāgacchat triṣṭubhaṃ prāhiṇvan saikam akṣaraṃ hitvā tryakṣarā bhūtvāgacchad
gāyatrīṃ prāhiṇvaṃś caturakṣarāṇi vai tarhi cchandāṃsy āsan sā tāni cākṣarāṇi haranty
āgacchad aṣṭākṣarā bhūtvā trīṇi ca savanāni hastābhyāṃ dve savane dantair daṃṣṭvā
tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād dve aṃśumatī savane dhītaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ dantair hi tad daṃṣṭvā
dhayanty aharat tasya ye hriyamāṇasyāṃśavaḥ parāpataṃs te pūtīkā abhavan yāni puṣpāṇy
avāśīyanta tāny arjjunāni yat prāprothat te praprothās tasmāt tṛtīyasavana āśiram
avanayanti yam eva taṃ gāvaḥ somam adanti tasya taṃ rasam avanayanti sasomatvāya
PB  te triṣṭub jagatyai gāyatrīm abrūtām upa tvāyāveti sābravīt kiṃ me tataḥ
syād iti yat kāmayasa ity abrūtāṃ sābvravīn mama sarvaṃ prātaḥsavanam aham uttare
savane praṇayānīti tasmād gāyatraṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ gāyatry uttare savane praṇayati
PB  tān triṣṭup tribhir akṣarair upait saikādaśākṣarā bhūtvā prājāyata tāṃ jagaty ekenākṣareṇopait sā dvādaśākṣarā bhūtvā prājāyata
PB  tasmād āhur gāyatrī vāva sarvāṇi cchandāṃsi gāyatrī hy etān poṣān puṣyanty aid iti
PB  indras tṛtīyasavanād bībhatsamāna udakrāmat tad devāḥ svādiṣṭhayeti asvadayan
madiṣṭhayeti madvad akurvan pavasva soma dhārayety apāvayann indrāya pātave suta
iti tato vai tad indra upāvartata yat svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayeti prastauti tṛtīyasavanasya sendratvāya
PB  svādiṣṭhā vai deveṣu paśava āsan madiṣṭhā asureṣu te devāḥ svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayeti paśūn asurāṇām avṛñjata
PB  paśūn bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃv veda
PB  tāsu saṃhitam
 PB  sādhyā vai nāmadevā āsaṃs te 'vacchidya tṛtīyasavanaṃ mādhyandinena savanena saha svargaṃl lokam āyaṃs tad devāḥ saṃhitena samadadhur  
yat samadadhus tasmāt saṃhitam 
PB  kāleyaṃ purastād bhavati saṃhitam upariṣṭād etābhyāṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ saṃtāyate
 PB  sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇi saṃhitaṃ yat padaprastāvaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ yad bṛhato rohān rohati tena bārhataṃ yad padanidhanaṃ tena rāthantaraṃ  
sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati 
PB  uṣṇikkakubhāv ete bhavataḥ
PB  uṣṇikkakubbhyāṃ vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat kakubhi parākramatoṣṇihā
prāharat tasmāt kakubho madhyamaṃ padaṃ bhūyiṣṭhākṣaraṃ parākramaṇaṃ hi tad abhi
samauhat tasmād uṣṇiha uttamaṃ padaṃ bhūyiṣṭhākṣaraṃ puro gurur iva hi vajraḥ
PB  vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati ya evaṃv veda
 PB  nāsike vā ete yajñasya yad uṣṇikkakubhau tasmāt samānaṃ chandaḥ satī nānā yajñaṃv vahatas tasmāt samānāyā nāsikāyāḥ satyā nānā prāṇāv 
PB  prāṇā vā uṣṇikkakubhau tasmāt tābhyāṃ na vaṣaṭ kurvanti yad vaṣaṭ kuryuḥ prāṇān agnau pradadhyuḥ
PB  tāsu saphaṃ vipham iva vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ tṛtīyasavanasya saphatvāyāthauṣkalam
etena vai prajāpatiḥ puṣkalān paśūn asṛjata teṣu rūpam adadhād yad etat sāma bhavati
paśuṣv eva rūpaṃ dadhāti
PB  purojitī vo andhasa iti padyā cākṣaryā ca virājau bhavataḥ padyayā vai
devāḥ svargaṃl lokam āyann akṣaryayā ṛṣayo nu prājānān yad ete padyā cākṣaryā ca
virājau bhavataḥ svargasya lokasya prajñātyai
PB  tāsu śyāvāśvam
 PB  śyāvāśvam ārvanānasaṃ sattram āsīnaṃ dhanvodavahan sa etat sāmāpaśyat tena vṛṣṭim asṛjata tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhat tato gātum avindata  
gātuvid vā etat sāma 
PB  vindate gātuṃ pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
 PB  indras tṛtīyasavanād bībhatsamāna udakrāmat taṃ devāḥ śyāvāślvenaihāyi ehiyety anvāhvayan sa upāvartata yad etat sāma bhavati tṛtīyasavanasya 
PB  athaitad āndhīgavam andhīgur vā etat paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ
paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai madhye nidhanam aiḍaṃ bhavaty
etena vai tṛtīyasavanaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ yan madhye nidhanam aiḍaṃ na syād apratiṣṭhitaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ syāt
PB  daśākṣaraṃ madhyato nidhanam upayanti daśākṣarā virāḍ virājy eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  abhi priyāṇi pavata iti kāvaṃ prājāpatyaṃ sāma
PB  prajā vai priyāṇi paśavaḥ priyāṇi prajāyām eva paśuṣu pratitiṣtśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  raśmī vā etau yajñasya yad auśanakāve devakośo vā eṣa yajñam abhisamubjito yad ete antato bhavato yajñasyāriṣṭyai
PB  devā vai brahma vyabhajanta tasya yo raso 'tyaricyata tad yajñāyajñīyam abhavat
PB  brahmaṇo vā eṣa raso yad yajñāyajñīyaṃ yad yajñāyajñīyena stuvanti brahmaṇa eva rase yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  yonir vai yajñāyajñīyam etasmād vai yoneḥ prajāpatir yajñam asṛjata tasmād yajñāyajñīyam
 PB  tasmād vā etena purā brāhmaṇā bahiṣpavamānam astoṣata yoner yajñaṃ pratanavāmahā iti yajñaṃ tataḥ stuvanti yonau yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati 
PB  asureṣu vai sarvo yajña āsīt te devā yajñāyajñīyam apaśyaṃs teṣāṃ yajñāyajñā
vo agnaya ity agnihotram avṛñjata girāgirā ca dakṣasa iti darśapūrṇamāsau prapra
vayam amṛtaṃ jātavedasam iti cāturmāsyāni priyaṃ mitraṃ na śaṃsiṣam iti saumyam adhvaram
PB  yajñā vo agnaye girā ca dakṣase pra vayam amṛtaṃ jātavedasaṃ priyaṃ mitraṃ
na śaṃsiṣam iti vai tarhi cchandāṃsy āsaṃs te devā abhyārambham abhinivartyaṃ cchandobhir
yajñam asurāṇām avṛñjata
PB  chandobhir yajñaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃv veda
PB  etad dha sma vā āha kūśāmbaḥ svāyavo brahmā lātavyaḥ kaṃ svid adya śiśumārī yajñapathe 'pyastā gariṣyati
PB  eṣā vai śiśumārī yajñapathe 'pyastā yajñāyajñīyaṃ yad girāgirety āhātmānaṃ tad udgātā girati
PB  airaṃ kṛtvodgeyam irāyāṃ yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayaty apramāyuka udgātā bhavati
PB  vaiśvānare vā etad udgātātmānaṃ pradadhāti yat prapra vayam ity āha praprīṃ vayam iti vaktavyaṃv vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmati
PB  yo vai nihnuvānaṃ cchanda upaiti pāpīyān ujjagivān bhavaty etad vai nihnuvānaṃ
cchando yan na śaṃsiṣam iti nu śaṃsiṣam iti vaktavyaṃ suśaṃsiṣam iti vā na nihnuvānaṃ
chanda upaiti vasīyān ujjagivān bhavati
PB  yasya vai yajñā vāgantā bhavanti vācaś chidreṇa sravanty ete vai yajñā
vāgantā ye yajñāyajñīyāntā etad vācaś chidraṃ yad anṛtaṃ yad agniṣṭomayājy anṛtam
āha tad anv asya yajñaḥ sravaty akṣareṇāntataḥ pratiṣṭhāpyam akṣareṇaiva yajñasya
cchidram api dadhāti
PB  virājo vā etad rūpaṃ yad akṣaraṃ virājy evāntataḥ pratitiṣṭhati
PB  ito vai prātar ūrdhvāṇi cchandāṃsi yujyante 'muto 'vāñci yajñāyajñīyasya
stotre yujyante yajñā vo agnaye girā ca dakṣasa iti dvādaśākṣaraṃ pra vayam amṛtaṃ
jātavedasam ity ekādaśākṣaraṃ priyaṃ mitraṃn na śaṃsiṣam ity aṣṭākṣaram
PB  anuṣṭubham uttamāṃ saṃpādayatīyaṃ vā anuṣṭub asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  vāg vā anuṣṭub vācy eva pratitiṣṭhati jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jaiṣṭhya eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  katham iva yajñāyajñīyaṃ geyam ity āhur yathānaḍvān prasrāvayamāṇa ittham iva cettham iva ceti
 PB  vaiśvānaraṃ vā etad udgātānu prasīdann etīty āhur yad yajñāyajñīyasyarcaṃ saṃpratyāheti parikrāmatevodgeyaṃv vaiśvānaram eva parikrāmati 
 PB  vaiśvānare vā etad adhvaryuḥ sadasyān abhisṛjati yad yajñāyajñīyasya stotram upāvartayati prāvṛtenodgeyaṃv vaiśvānareṇānabhidāhāya 
PB  na ha tu vai pitaraḥ prāvṛtaṃ jānanti yajñāyajñīyasya vai stotre pitaro
yathāyathaṃ jijñāsanta ākarṇābhyāṃ prāvṛtyaṃ tad eva prāvṛtaṃ tad aprāvṛtaṃ jānanti
pitaro na vaiśvānaro hinasti
PB  apaḥ paścāt patnya upasṛjanti vaiśvānaram eva tac chamayanty āpo hi śāntiḥ
PB  atho reta eva tat siñcanty āpo hi retaḥ
PB  dakṣiṇān ūrūn abhiṣiñcanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyate
PB  mahad iva pratyūhyaṃ mana evāsya taj janayanti
PB  udgātrā patnīḥ saṃkhyāpayanti retodheyāya
PB  hiṅkāraṃ prati saṃkhyāpayanti hiṅkṛtād dhi reto 'dhīyata
PB  ātṛtīyāyāḥ saṃkhyāpayanti trivad dhi retaḥ
PB  devā vā agniṣṭomam abhijityokthāni nāśaknuvann abhijetuṃ te 'gnim abruvaṃs
tvayā mukhenedaṃ cayāmeti so 'bravīt kiṃ me tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayasa ity abruvan
so 'bravīn maddevatyāsūkthāni praṇayān iti
PB  tasmād āgneyīṣūkthāni praṇayanti
PB  tasmād u gāyatrīṣu gāyatracchandā hy agniḥ
PB  te 'gniṃ mukhaṃ kṛtvā sākam aśvenābhyakrāman yat sākam aśvenābhyakrāmaṃs tasmāt sākamaśvam
PB  tasmāt sākamaśvenokthāni praṇayanty etena hi tāny agre 'bhyajayan
 PB  sa indro 'bravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti varuṇas taṃv varuṇo 'nvatiṣṭhad indra āharat tasmād aindrāvaruṇam anuśasyate 
PB  sa evābravīt kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti bṛhaspatis taṃ
bṛhaspatir anvatiṣṭad indra āharat tasmād aindrābārhaspatyam anuśasyate sa evābravīt
kaś cāhaṃ cedam anvavaiṣyāva ity ahaṃ ceti viṣṇus taṃ viṣṇur anvatiṣṭad indra āharat
tasmād aindrāvaiṣṇavam anuśasyate
PB  paśūn vā ebhyas tān āharat paśavo vā ukthāni paśukāma ukthena stuvīta paśumān bhavati
PB  bṛhatā vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tasya tejaḥ parāpatat tat saubharam abhavat
PB  jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yad rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ rathantaraṃ
saṃdhir nāntarā bṛhatā stuvantīti yat saubhareṇa stuvanti bṛhataiva tad antarā stuvanti
bṛhato hy etat tejo yat saubharam
PB  yadi bṛhat sāmātirātraḥ syāt saubharam ukthānāṃ brahma sāma kāryaṃ bṛhad eva tat tejasā samardhayati
PB  yadi rathantarasāmnā saubharaṃ kuryād ajāmitāyai
PB  devānāṃ vai svargaṃl lokaṃ yatāṃ diśo 'vlīyanta tāḥ saubhareṇo ity udastaṃbhuvaṃs
tato vai tā adṛṃhanta tataḥ pratyatiṣṭhaṃs tataḥ svargaṃl lokaṃ prājānan yaḥ svargakāmaḥ
syād yaḥ pratiṣṭhākāmaḥ saubhareṇa stuvīta pra svargaṃl lokaṃ jānāti pratitṣṭhati
PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tāḥ sṛṣṭā āśanāyaṃs tābhyaḥ saubhareṇorg ity annaṃ prāyacchat tato vai tāḥ samaidhanta
PB  samedhante tāṃ samāṃ prajā yatraivaṃv vidvān saubhareṇodgāyati
PB  tā abruvan subhṛtaṃ no 'bhārṣīr iti tasmāt saubharam
PB  vṛṣṭiṃ vā abhyastāṃ prāyacchad annam eva
PB  yo vṛṣṭikāmaḥ syād yo 'nnādyakāmo yaḥ svargakāmaḥ saubhareṇa stuvīta
PB  hīṣiti vṛṣṭikāmāya nidhanaṃ kuryād ūrg ity annādyakāmāyo iti svargakāmāya
PB  sarve vai kāmāḥ saubharaṃ sarveṣv eva kāmeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  athaitan nārmedham
PB  nṛmedhasam āṅgirasaṃ sattram āsīnaṃ śvabhir abhyāhvayan so 'gnim upādhāvat
pāhi no agna ekayeti taṃv vaiśvānaraḥ paryudatiṣṭhat tato vai sa pratyatiṣṭhat tato gātum avindata
PB  gātuvid vā etat sāma vindate gātuṃ pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  naiva hy etad ahno rūpaṃ na rātrer yad ukthānām
PB  kakup prathamāthoṣṇig atha purauṣṇig anuṣṭup tenānuṣṭubho nayanty acchāvākasāmnaḥ
PB  hārivarṇaṃ bhavati
PB  asurā vā eṣu lokeṣv āsaṃs tān devā hariśriyam ity asmāl lokāt prāṇudanta virājasīty antarikṣād divodiva ity amuṣmāt
PB  tad ya evaṃ vedaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudyemāṃl lokān abhyārohati
PB  harivarṇo vā etat paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭaiḥ
PB  aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃl lokaṃ yato rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tāny etena harivarṇo 'pāhanta yad etat sāma bhavati rakṣasām apahatyai
PB  pṛṣṭhāni vā asṛjyanta teṣāṃ yat tejo raso 'tyaricyata tad devāḥ samabharaṃs tad udvaṃśīyam abhavat
PB  sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ tejo yad udvaṃśīyaṃ tasmād vā etat purā sajātāya nākran pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai
PB  eṣa hy eva pṛṣṭhais tuṣṭuvāno ya udvaṃśīyena stuvate
PB  sarvāṇi vai rūpāṇy udvaṃśīyam
PB  gāyanti tvā gāyatriṇa eti rathantarasya rūpam eti hi rathantaram
PB  ādir bṛhata ūrdhvam iva hi bṛhat
PB  pariṣṭobho vairūpasya pariṣṭubhaṃ hi vairūpam
PB  anutodo vairājasyānutunnaṃ hi vairājam
PB  ardheḍā śakvarīṇām atisvāro revatīnām
PB  ardheḍayā vai devā asurān avahatyātisvāreṇa svargaṃl lokam ārohan
PB  tad ya evaṃv vedārdheḍayaiva bhrātṛvyam avahatyātisvāreṇa svargaṃl lokam ārohati
PB  ardheḍayā vai pūrvaṃ yajñaṃ saṃsthāpayanty atisvāreṇottram ārabhante
PB  upainam uttaro yajño namati ya evaṃv veda
PB  pāṅktaṃ vā etat sāma pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavo yajña eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  āṣṭādaṃṣṭre ṛddhikāmāya kuryāt
PB  aṣṭādaṃṣṭro vairūpo 'putro 'prajā ajīryat sa imāṃl lokān vicicchidvāṃ
amanyata sa ete jarasi sāmanī apaśyat tayor aprayogād abibhet so 'bravīd ṛdhnavad
yobhe sāmabhyāṃ stavatā iti
PB  ṛṣer vā etat prāśodbhūtaṃ yad aṣṭādaṃṣṭre bhavata ṛdhyā eva
PB  gāyatrīṣu brahmavarcasakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur gāyatryāṃ brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā gāyatrī saṃpadyate
PB  tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe
PB  gāyatrīṣu paśukāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣoṣṇik saṃpadyate
PB  paśavo vā uṣṇik paśūn evāvarundhe
PB  gāyatrīṣu puruṣakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyuḥ kakubhi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā kakup saṃpadyate
PB  puruṣo vai kakup puruṣān evāvarundhe
PB  virāṭsv annādyakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣā virāṭ saṃpadyate
PB  annaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāvarundhe
PB  akṣarapaṅktiṣu jyaiṣṭhyakāmāyokthāni praṇayeyur uṣṇihi brahmasāmānuṣṭubhy acchāvākasāma saiṣānuṣṭup saṃpadyate
PB  jyaiṣṭhyaṃ vā anuṣṭub jyaiṣṭhyam avāvarundhe
PB  devā vā ukthāny abhijitya rātriṃ nāśaknuvann abhijetuṃ te 'surān rātriṃ
tamaḥ praviṣṭāṃ nānuvyapaśyaṃs ta etam anuṣṭupśirasaṃ pragāthm apaśyan virājaṃ jyotiḥ
tān virājā jyotiṣānupaśyanto 'nuṣṭubhā vajreṇa rātrer nirāghnan
PB  yad eṣo 'nuṣṭupśirāḥ pragātho bhavati virāḍ eva jyotiṣānupaśyann anuṣṭubhā vajreṇa rātrer bhrātṛvyaṃ nirhanti
PB  tān samantaṃ paryāyaṃ prāṇudanta yat paryāyaṃ prāṇudanta tat paryāyāṇāṃ paryāyatvam
PB  prathamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanti prathamasya paryāyasya
PB  prathamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāya prathamarātrāt prāṇudanta
PB  pāntam ā vo andhasa iti prastauti
PB  ahar vai pāntam andho rātrir ahnaiva tad rātrim ārabhante
PB  tāsu vaitahavyam
PB  vītahavyaḥ śrāyaso jyog niruddha etat sāmāpaśyat so 'vagacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhaty etena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  tam iva vā ete praviśantiye rātrim upayanti yad eko nidhanaṃ rātrer mukhe bhavati prajñātyai
PB  yadā vai puruṣaḥ svam oka āgacchati sarvaṃ tarhi prajānāti sarvam asmai divā bhavati
PB  te madhyamaṃ paryāyam aśrayanta teṣām aurdhvasadmanena vācam avṛñjata
PB  vācaṃ bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃv veda
PB  triṇidhanaṃ bhavati
PB  yathā vā ahno mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ triṇidhanāyatanam evam eṣa rātrer madhyamaḥ paryāyas triṇidhanāyatanaḥ salokatvāya
PB  madhyamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanti madhyamasya paryāyasya madhyamair hi padaiḥ punar ādāyaṃ madhyamarātrāt prāṇudanta
PB  ta uttamaṃ paryāyam aśrayanta teṣāṃ ghṛtaścyun nidhanena paśūn avṛñjata paśavo vai ghṛtaścyutaḥ
PB  paśūn bhrātṛvyasya vṛṅkte ya evaṃv veda
PB  uttamāni padāni punarādīni bhavanty uttamasya paryāyasyottamair hi padaiḥpunar ādāyam uttamarātrāt prāṇudanta
PB  tān sandhinābhipalāyanta
PB  tān āśvinenāsaṃhāyyam agamayan
PB  asaṃhāyyaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ gamayati ya evaṃv veda
PB  eṣā vā agniṣṭomasya saṃmā yad rātriḥ
PB  dvādaśa stotrāṇy agniṣṭomo dvādaśa strotrāṇi rātriḥ
PB  eṣā vā ukthasya saṃmā yad rātriḥ
PB  trīṇy ukthāni tridevatyaḥ sandhiḥ
PB  yathā vā ahna ukthāny evam eṣa rātreḥ sandhir nānārūpāṇy ahna ukthāni nānārūpā ete tṛcā bhavanti
PB  rathantaraṃ pratiṣṭhākāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt
PB  iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  bṛhat svargakāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt
PB  svargo loko bṛhat svarga eva loke pratitiṣṭhati
PB  vāravantīyaṃ vā vāmadevyaṃ vā śruddhyaṃ vai teṣām ekaṃ paśukāmāya sandhiṃ kuryāt
PB  paśavo vā etāni sāmāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  āśvinaṃ hotānuśaṃsati
PB  prajāpatir vā etat sahasram asṛjata tad devebhyaḥ prāyacchat tasmin na samarādhayaṃs te sūryaṃ kāṣṭhāṃ kṛtvājim adhāvan
PB  teṣām aśvinau prathamāv adhāvatāṃ tāv anvavadan saha no 'stv iti tāv
abrūtāṃ kiṃ tataḥ syād iti yat kāmayethe ity abruvaṃs tāv abrūtām asmaddevatyam idam
uktham ucyātā iti tasmād āśvinam ucyate
PB  sarvāḥ khalu devatāḥ śasyante
PB  kṣipraṃ śasyam ājim iva hy ete dhāvanty ā sūryasyodetoḥ śaṃset sūryaṃ hi kāṣṭhām akurvata
 PB  pāntam ā vo andhasa iti vaitahavyam anyakṣetraṃvā ete prayanti ye rātrim upayanti yad okonidhanaṃ rātrer mukhe bhavaty okaso 'pracyāvāya 
PB  pra va indrāya mādanam iti gaurīvitam
PB  brahma yad devā vyakurvata tato yad atyaricyata tad gaurīvitam abhavat
PB  atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atiriktam etat stotraṃ yad rātrir atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti
PB  vayam u tvā tad id arthā iti kāṇvam
PB  etena vai kaṇva indrasya sāṃvidyam agacchad indrasyaivaitena sāṃvidyaṃ gacchati
PB  indrāya madvane sutam iti śrautakakṣaṃ kṣatrasāma pra kṣatram evaitena bhavati
PB  ayaṃ ta indra soma iti daivodāsam
PB  agniṣṭomena vai devā imaṃl lokam abhyajayann antarikṣam ukthenātirātreṇāmuṃ
ta imaṃl lokaṃ punar abhyakāmayanta ta ihety asmiṃl loke pratyatiṣṭhan yad etat sāma
bhavati pratiṣṭhityai
PB  ūrdhvasadmanam api śarvarīṣu prohanti
PB  asurā vā eṣu lokeṣv āsaṃs tān devā ūrdhvasadmanenaibhyo lokebhyaḥ prāṇudanta
PB  tad ya evaṃv vedaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudya sva āyatane sattram āste
PB  ā tū na indra kṣumantam ity ākūpāram
PB  akūpārāṅgirasasyāsīt tasyā yathā godhāyās tvag eva tvag āsīt tām etena
triḥsāmnendraḥ pūtvā sūryatvacasam akarot tad vāva sā tarhy akāmayata yatkāmā etena
sāmnā stuvate sa ebhyaḥ kāmaḥ samṛdhyate
PB  abhi tvā vṛṣabhā sutaṃ ity ārṣabhaṃ kṣatrasāma kṣatram evaitena bhavati
PB  idaṃv vaso sutam andha iti gāram etena vai gara indram aprīṇāt prīta evāsyaitenendro bhavati
PB  idaṃ hy anv ojaseti mādhucchandasaṃ prajāpater vā eṣā tanūr ayātayāmnī prayujyate
PB  ā tv etā niṣīdateti daivātitham
 PB  devātithiḥ saputro 'śanāyaṃś carann araṇya urvārūṇy avindat tāny etena sāmnopāsīdat tā asmai gāvaḥ pṛśnayo bhūtvodatiṣṭhan yad  
etat sām a bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai 
PB  yogeyoge tavastaram iti saumedhaṃ rātriṣāma rātrer eva samṛdhyai
PB  indra suteṣu someṣv iti kautsam
PB  kutsaś ca luśaś cendraṃ vyahvayetāṃ sa indraḥ kutsam upāvartata taṃ śatena
vārdhrībhir āṇḍayor abadhnāt taṃ luśo 'bhyavadat pramucyasva pari kutsād ihāgahi
kim u tvāvān āṇḍayor baddha āsātā iti tās saṃcchidya prādravat sa etat kutsaḥ sāmāpaśyat
tenainam anvavadat sa upāvartata
PB  yad etat sāma bhavati sendratvāya
 PB  yadi sattrāya dīkṣerann atha sāmy uttiṣṭhet somam apabhajya viśvajitātirātreṇa yajeta sarvavedasena sarvasmā eva dīkṣate sarvam 
PB  yā id dakṣiṇā dadāti tābhir iti prayuṅkte
PB  yadi paryāyair astutam abhivyucchet pancadaśabhir hotre stuyuḥ pañcabhiḥpañcabhir itarebhyaḥ
 PB  agne vivasvad uṣasa iti sandhinā stuyuḥ prāṇā vai trivṛt stomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā rathantaraṃ sāmnāṃ prāṇāṃs caivopayanti pratiṣṭhāṃ ca 
PB  ṣaṣṭiṃ ca trīṇi ca śatāni hotā śaṃsati
PB  tāvatyaḥ saṃvatsarasya rātrayaḥ saṃvatsarasaṃmitābhir eva tad ṛgbhir āśīvinam āpnoti
PB  yad arvāk stuvanti tad astutaṃ yat samprati stuvanti tat stutaṃ yad atiṣṭuvanti tat suṣṭutam
PB  yady arvāk stuyur yāvatībhir na stuyus tāvatībhir vātiṣṭuyur bhūyo 'kṣarābhir vā
PB  yady atiṣṭuyur yāvatībhir atiṣṭuyus tāvatībhir vā na stuyuḥ kanīyo 'kṣarābhir vā
PB  yady arvāk stuyus trīḍam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ nidhanam ekeḍayā ye dve tābhyām eva tat samaṃ kriyate
PB  yady atiṣṭuyuḥ svāram agniṣṭomasāma kāryam ūnam iva vā etat sāmno yat svaras tenaiva tat samaṃ kriyate
PB  yadi somau saṃsutau syātāṃ mahati rātreḥ prātaranuvākam upākuryāt
PB  pūrvo vācaṃ pūrvaś chandāṃsi pūrvo devatā vṛṅkte
PB  vṛṣaṇvatīṃ pratipadaṃ kuryād indro vai vṛṣā prātaḥsavanād evaiṣām indraṃv vṛṅkte
PB  atho khalv āhuḥ savanamukhesavanamukhe kāryā savanamukhātsavanamukhād evaiṣām indraṃv vṛṅkte
PB  susamiddhe hotavyam agnir vai sarvā devatāḥ sarvā eva devatāḥ paśyañ juhoti
PB  saṃveśāyopaveśāya gāyatryai cchandase 'bhibhūtaye svāhā saṃveśāyopaveśāya
triṣṭubhe cchandase 'bhibhūtaye svāhā saṃveśāyopaveśāya jagatyai cchandase 'bhibhūtaye svāheti juhoti
PB  cchandāṃsi vā abhibhūtayas tair evainān abhibhavaty ubhe bṛhadrathantare kārye
 PB  yatra vā indrasya harī tad indraḥ indrasya vai harī bṛhadrathantare yad ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavataḥ pūrva evendrasya harī ārabhante 
PB  tair aśravase kārye
PB  turaśravasaś ca vai pārāvatānāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata ete turaśravāḥ
sāmanī apaśyat tābhyām asmā indraḥ śalmalināṃ yamunāyā havyaṃ nirāvahat yat tair
aśravase bhavato havyam evaiṣāṃv vṛṅkte
PB  pūrve 'bhiṣuṇuyuḥ
PB  yā vai pūrvāḥ prasnānti tāḥ pūrvās tīrthaṃ jayanti pūrva evendram ārabhante
PB  vihavyaṃ śasyam
 PB  jamadagneś ca vā ṛṣīṇāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata etaj gamadagnir vihavyam apaśyat tam indra upāvartata yad vihavyaṃ hotā śaṃsatīndram  
evaiṣāṃv vṛṅkte 
 PB  yadītaro 'gniṣṭomaḥ syād ukthaḥ kāryo yady uktho 'tirātro yo vai bhūyān yajñakratuḥ sa indrasya priyo bhūyasaivaiṣāṃ yajnakratunendraṃv 
PB  atho khalv āhur duṣprāpa iva vai paraḥ panthā yam evāgre yajñakratum ārabheta tasmān neyād iti
PB  sajanīyaṃ śasyam agastyasya kayāśubhīyaṃ śasyam
PB  asyā amuṣyā adyaśvān mithunād ahorātrābhyām evainān nirbhajati
PB  yadi somam akrītam apahareyur anyaḥ kretavyaḥ
PB  yadi krītaṃ yo 'nyo 'bhyāśaṃ syāt sa āhṛtyaḥ somavikrayaṇe tu kiṃ cid dadyāt
PB  yadi somaṃ na vindeyuḥ pūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyur yadi na pūtīkān arjjunāni
PB  gāyatrī somam āharat tasyā anu visṛjya somarakṣiḥ parṇam acchinat tasya
yo 'ṃśuḥ parāpatat sa pūtīko 'bhavat tasmin devā ūtim avindann ūtīko vā eṣa yat pūtīkān
abhiṣuṇvanty ūtim evāsmai vindanti
PB  pratidhuk ca prātaḥ pūtīkāś ca śṛtaṃ ca madhyandine pūtīkāś ca dadhi cāparāhṇe pūtīkāś ca
 PB  somapītho vā etasmād apakrāmatīty āhur yasya somam apaharantīti sa oṣadhīś ca paśūṃś ca praviśati tam oṣadhibhyaś ca paśubhyaś cāvarundhe 
PB  indro vṛtram ahaṃs tasya yo nastaḥ somaḥ samadhāvat tāni babhrutūlāny
arjunāni yo vapāyā utkhinnāyās tāni lohitatūlāni yāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni tāny
abhiṣuṇuyād etad vai brahmaṇo rūpaṃ sākṣād eva somam abhiṣuṇoti
PB  śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma kāryaṃ sad evainaṃ karoti
PB  yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi prohed vācaivainaṃ samardhayati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam indriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai
PB  pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ
PB  pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhate
PB  avabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣeta
PB  tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt
PB  yadi kalaśo dīryeta vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ brahmasāma kuryāt
 PB  avaṣaṭkṛto vā etasya somaḥ parāsicyate yasya kalaśo dīryate yad vaṣaṭkāraṇīdhanaṃ brahmasāma bhavati vaṣaṭkṛta evāsya somo bhavati 
PB  vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ samane bahūnām ity etāsu kāryam
PB  eṣa hi bahūnāṃ samane dīryate yat kalaśaḥ
PB  tad āhur na vā ārtyārtir anūdyārtyā vā eṣa ārtim anuvadati yaḥ kalaśo dīrṇe dadrāṇavatīṣu karotīti
PB  śrāyantīyam eva kāryam
 PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etac chrāyantīyam apaśyat tenātmānaṃ samaśrīṇāt prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa 
 PB  dugdha iva eṣa riricāno yasya kalaśo dīryate yac chrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati punar evātmānaṃ saṃśrīṇāti prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa 
PB  yadi śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma syād vaiṣṇavīṣv anuṣṭupsu vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ kuryāt
PB  yad vai yajñasya sravati vācaṃ pratisravati vāg anuṣṭup yajño viṣṇur vācaiva yajñasya cchidram apidadhāti
PB  yad vai yajñasya sravaty antataḥ sravati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ yajñasyaiva cchidraṃ vārayate
PB  yadi prātassavanāt somo 'tiricyeta asti somo ayaṃ suta iti marutvatīṣu gāyatreṣu stuyuḥ
PB  mādhyandinaṃ vā eṣa savanaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yaḥ prātassavanād
atiricyate tasmān marutvatīṣu stuvanti marutvad dhi mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ tasmād u
gāyatrīṣu gāyatraṃ hi prātassavanam
PB  yasmāt stomād atiricyate sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāya
PB  aindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati
PB  vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhati
PB  yadi mādhyandināt savanād atiricyeta baṇ mahāṃ asi sūryety ādityavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ
PB  tṛtīyasavanaṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo mādhyandināt savanād
atiricyate tasmād ādityavatīṣu stuvanty ādityaṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād u bṛhatīṣu
bārhataṃ hi mādhyandinaṃ savanam
 PB  yasmāt stomād atiricyeta sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāyaindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe 
PB  yadi tṛtīyasavanād atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ
PB  yajño vai viṣṇuś śipiviṣṭo yajña eva viṣṇau pratitiṣṭhaty atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti
PB  etad anyat kuryur ukthāni praṇayeyur ukthāni vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate
yo 'gniṣṭomād atiricyate yady ukthyebhyo 'tiricyetātirātraḥ kāryo rātriṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno
'bhyatiricyate ya ukthyebhyo 'tiricyate yadi rātrer atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu
bṛhatā stuyur eṣu tu vā atiricyata ity āhur yo rātrer atiricyata iti
PB  amuṃ vā eṣa lokaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo rātrer atiricyate bṛhatā stuvanti bṛhad amuṃ lokam āptum arhati tam evāpnoti
PB  yadi dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate dagdhvāsthīny upanahya yo nediṣṭhī syāt taṃ dīkṣayitvā saha yajeran
PB  etad anyat kuryur abhiṣutyānyat somam agṛhītvā grahān yāsau dakṣiṇā sraktis tad vā stuyur mārjālīye vā
PB  api vā etasya yajñe yo dīkṣitaḥ pramīyate tam etena niravadayante
PB  yāmena stuvanti yamalokam evainaṃ gamayanti
PB  tisṛbhiḥ stuvanti tṛtīye hi loke pitaraḥ
PB  parācībhiḥ stuvanti parāṅ hīto 'sau lokaḥ
PB  sarparājñyā ṛgbhiḥ stuvanti
PB  arbudaḥ sarpa etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata mṛtām evaitābhis tvacam apaghnate
PB  tā ṛco 'nubruvantas trir mārjālīyaṃ pariyanti savyān ūrūn āghnānāḥ
PB  stutam anuśaṃsaty amuṣminn evainaṃ loke nidhnuvanti
PB  yanti vā ete patha ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīty aindravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇate punaḥ panthānam apiyanti
PB  agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti pratipatkāryā ya eva jīvanti teṣv āyur dadhāti
PB  saṃvatsare 'sthīni yājayeyuḥ saṃvvatsaro vai sarvasya śāntir yat purā saṃvvatsarād yājayeyur vācam aruṣkṛtāṃ krūrām ṛccheyuḥ
PB  vṛtaḥ pavamānāḥ syuḥ saptadaśam itarat sarvam
 PB  yat trivṛtaḥ pavamānā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān evopayanti yat saptadaśam itarat sarvaṃ prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajatim 
 PB  prāṇāpānair vā ete vyṛdhyanta ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīti maitrāvaruṇāgrān grahān gṛhṇate prāṇāpānau mitrāvaruṇau prāṇāpānair  
eva samṛdhyante 
PB  yasya kalaśa upadasyati kalaśam evāsyopadasyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ
PB  tad āhuḥ payo 'vanayed iti
PB  atho khalv āhur antarhitam iva vā etad yat payo hiraṇyam evāpo'bhyavanayed dhiraṇyam abhyunnayed iti
PB  prāṇā vā āpo 'mṛtaṃ hiraṇyam amṛta evāsya prāṇān dadhāti sa sarvam āyur eti
PB  yasya nārāśaṃsa upavāyati nārāśaṃsam evāsyopavāyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ
PB  yam adhvaryur antato grahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tasyāptum avanayet
PB  prāyaścityai vai graho gṛhyate prāyaścityevāsmai prāyaścittiṃ karoti
PB  yadi pītāpītau somau saṃgaccheyātām antaḥ paridhyaṅgārān nirvartya juhuyāt hutasya cāhutasya cāhutasya hutasya ca 
pītāpītasya somasyendrāgnī pibataṃ sutaṃ svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
PB  prajāpataye svāhety abhakṣaṇīyasya juhuyād uttarārdhyapūrvārdhya uparavaḥ
PB  indur indum avāgād ity avavṛṣṭasya bhakṣayet
PB  tasya ta indrav indrapītasyendriyāvatas sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
PB  hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra ity ājyenābhyupākṛtasya juhuyād agnīdhraṃ
paretya bhūtānāṃ jātaḥ patir eka āsīt sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyām utemāṃ tasmai ta indo
haviṣā vidhema svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
PB  yadi grāvāpi śīryate paśubhir yajamāno vyṛdhyate paśavo vai grāvāṇo dyutānasya mārutasya sāmnā stuyuḥ
PB  mārutā vai grāvāṇaḥ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
PB  yadi somam abhidahed grahān adhvaryuḥ spāśayeta stotrāṇy udgātā śastrāṇi
hotātha yathāpūrvaṃ yajñena careyuḥ pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas
tam ārabhate 'vabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣate tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt purā
dvādaśyā dīkṣeta yad dvādaśīm atinayed antardhīyeta
PB  yadi mahāvīro bhidyeta taṃ bhinnam abhimṛśed ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ 
saṃdhātā saṃdhiṃ maghavā purūvasur niṣkartā vihrutaṃ punaḥ mā bhema niṣṭyā ivendra tvad araṇā iva 
vanāni na prajahitāny adrivo duroṣāso amanmahi 
amanmahīd anāśavo 'nugrābhaś ca vṛtrahan 
sakṛt sute mahatā śūra rādhasānu stomaṃ mademahīti mahāvīraṃ bhinnam abhimṛśet saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
 PB  asuryaṃ vā etasmād varṇaṃ kṛtvā teja indriyaṃ vīryam annādyaṃ prajāḥ paśavo 'pakrāmanti yasya yūpo virohati sa īśvaraḥ pāpīyān 
PB  tvāṣṭraṃ paśuṃ bahurūpam ālabheta tvaṣṭā vai paśūnāṃ rūpāṇāṃ vikartā
tam eva tad upadhāvati sa enaṃ tejaseindriyeṇa vīryeṇānnādyena prajayā paśubhiḥ punas
samardhayati saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
PB  agninā pṛthivyauṣadhibhis tenāyaṃ lokas trivṛd vāyunāntarikṣeṇa vayobhis
tenaiṣa lokās trivṛd yo 'yam antar ādityena divā nakṣatrais tenāsau lokas trivṛd
etad eva trivṛta āyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  tam u pratiṣṭhetyāhus trivṛd dhy evaiṣu lokeṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ
PB  ardhamāsa eva pañcadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  taṃ caujo balam ity āhur ardhamāsaśo hi prajāḥ paśava ojo balaṃ puṣyanti
PB  saṃvatsara eva saptadaśasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcadartava etad eva saptadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  tam u prajāpatir ity āhuḥ saṃvatsaraṃ hi prajāḥ paśavo 'nuprajāyante
 PB  āditya evaikaviṃsasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcavartas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśa etad evaikaviṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā 
PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  tam u devatalpa ity āhuḥ pra devatalpam āpnoti ya evaṃv veda
PB  trivṛd eva triṇavasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  tam u puṣṭir ity āhus trivṛd dhy evaiṣa puṣṭaḥ
PB  devatā eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanaṃ trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśa etad eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  tam u nāka ity āhur na hi prajāpatiḥ kasmai canākam
PB  chandāṃsy eva chandomānām āyatanam eṣaiṣāṃ bandhutā
PB  āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
PB  tān u puṣṭir ity āhuḥ paśavo hi chandomāḥ
PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata so 'tāmyat tasmai vāj jyotir udagṛhṇāt so 'bravīt
ko me 'yaṃ jyotir udagṛhṇād iti svaiva te vāg ity abravīt tām abravīd virājaṃ tvā
cchandasāṃ jyotiṣkṛtvā yajāntā iti
PB  tasmād yo virājaṃ stomaṃ saṃpadyate taṃ jyotiṣṭomo 'gniṣṭoma ity ācakṣate virāḍ ḍhi chandasāṃ jyotiḥ
PB  jyotiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃv veda
 PB  anuṣṭup ca vai saptadaśaś ca samabhavatāṃ sānuṣṭup caturuttarāṇi chandāṃsy asṛjata ṣaḍuttarān stomān saptadaśas tāv etān madhyataḥ 
PB  trivṛc ca triṇavaś ca rāthantarau tāv ajaś cāśvaś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau rāthantaraṃ prācīnaṃ pradhūnutaḥ
PB  pañcadaśaś caikaviṃśaś ca bārhatau tau gauś cāviś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau bārhataṃ prācīnaṃ bhāskurutaḥ
PB  evaṃ vai vidvāṃsam āhur api grāmyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ vāca ājānāti
PB  prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa ātmann ṛtvyam apaśyat tata
ṛtvijo 'sṛjata yad ṛtvyād asṛjata tad ṛtvijām ṛtviktvaṃ tair etaṃ dvādaśāham upāsīdat so 'rādhnot
PB  pitā no 'rātsīd iti māsā upāsīdaṃs te dīkṣayaivārādhnuvann upasatsu trayodaśam
adīkṣayan so ' nuvyam abhavat tasmād upasatsu didīkṣāṇo 'nuvyaṃ bhavaty eva ca hi
trayodaśaṃ māsaṃ cakṣate naiva ca
 PB  eko dīkṣetaiko hi prajāpatir arādhnod dvādaśa dīkṣeran dvādaśa hi māsā arādhnuvaṃś caturviṃśatir dīkṣeraṃś caturviṃśatir hy ardhamāsā 
 PB  yadi pañcadaśo dīkṣeteme pañceme pañceme pañceme pañceme catvāro 'sāv eka iti nirdiśeyur yasmā arāddhikāmāḥ syus tam evārāddhir  
anveti sarva itare rādhnuvanti 
PB  yo vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiṃ vedāśnute gārhapataṃ pra gārhapatam āpnoti
PB  saṃvatsaro vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiḥ sa eva prajāpatis tasya māsā eva saha dīkṣiṇaḥ
PB  vindate saha dīkṣiṇo 'śnute gārhapatyaṃ pra gārhapatyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃv veda 
 PB  yo vai chandasāṃ svarājaṃ vedāśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti bṛhatī vāva chandasāṃ svarāḍ aśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ  
āpnoti ya evaṃv veda 
 PB  tām etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ dvādaśa dīkṣā svādaśopasado dvādaśa prasutaḥ ṣaṭriṃśad etā rātrayo bhavanti  
ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarā bṛhatī 
PB  jāyate vāva dīkṣayā punīta upasadbhir devalokam eva sutyayāpyeti
PB  etāvad vāva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ yad etā rātrayo dvādaśa pūṛnamāsyo
dvādaśaikaṣṭakā dvādaśāmāvāsyā yāvad eva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ tad etenāptvāvarundhe dvādaśāhena
PB  triṃśadakṣarā vā eṣā virāḍ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva virājā pratitiṣṭhaty ṛtubhir virāji
 PB  dvātriṃśadakṣarā vā eṣānuṣṭub vāg anuṣṭup catuṣpādaḥ paśavo vācā paśūn dādhāra tasmād vācā siddhā vācāhūtā āyanti tasmād u nāma 
 PB  bhūtaṃ pūrvo 'tirātro bhaviṣyad uttaraḥ pṛthivī pūrvo 'tirātro dyaur uttaro 'gniḥ pūrvo 'tirātra āditya uttaraḥ prāṇaḥ pūrvo 'tirātra  
udāna uttaraḥ 
PB  cakṣuṣī atirātrau kanīnike agniṣṭomau yasmād antarā agniṣṭomāv atirātrābhyāṃ tasmād antare satyau kanīnike bhuṅktaḥ
PB  saṃvatsarasya vā etau daṃṣṭrau yad atirātrau tayor na svaptavyaṃ saṃvatsarasya daṃṣṭrayor ātmānaṃ ned apidadhānīti
PB  tad āhuḥ ko 'svaptum arhati yad vāva prāṇo jāgāra tad eva jāgaritam iti
 PB  gāyatrīṃ vā etāṃ jyotiḥpakṣām āsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham aṣṭau madhya ukthā agniṣṭomāv abhito māsā svargṃ lokam etyājarasaṃ brahmādyam  
annam atti dīpyamānaḥ 
PB  triṣpurastād rathantaraṃ upayanti tryāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ tanvate
 PB  jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yat triṣpurastād rathantaram upayantīti saubharam ukthānāṃ brahmasāma bhavati tenaiva tad ajāmi 
PB  pratnavatyaḥ prāyaṇīyasyāhnaḥ pratipado bhavanti teno eva tad ajāmi
PB  trir vevopariṣṭād rathantaram upayanti trāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhād uttiṣṭhanti
PB  trayo vā ete trirātrā yad eṣa dvādaśāho gāytramukhaḥ prathamo gāyatramadhyo dvitīyo gāyatrottamas tṛtīyaḥ
PB  yasmād gāyatramukhaḥ prathamas tasmād ūrdhvo 'gnir dīdāya yasmād gāyatramadhyo dvitīyas tasmāt tiryaṅ vāyuḥ pavate

PB 
PB  tejasā vā ete prayanti tejo madhye dadhati tejo 'bhyudyanti jyotiṣā vā
ete prayanti jyotir madhye dadhati jyotir abhyudyanti cakṣuṣā vā ete prayanti cakṣur
madhye dadhati cakṣur abhyudyanti prāṇena vā ete prayanti prāṇaṃ madhye dadhati prāṇam
abhyudyanti ye gāyatryā prayanti gāyatrīṃ madhye dadhati gāyatrim abhyudyanti
PB  tantraṃ vā etad vitāyate yad eṣa dvādaśāhas tasyetair 
mayūkhā yad gāyatry asaṃvyāthāya
PB  girikṣidauccāmanyaveti hovācābhipratārī kākṣaseniḥ kathaṃ dvādaśāha iti
yathārān nemiḥ paryety evam enaṃ gāyatrī paryeti avisraṃsāya yathārā nābhau dhṛtā
evam asyāṃ dvādaśāho dhṛtaḥ
PB  anuṣṭubhaṃ vā etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham
PB  aṣṭābhir vā akṣair anuṣṭup prathamaṃ dvādaśāhasyāhar duyacchaty ekādaśabhir dvitīyaṃ dvādaśābhis tṛtīyam
PB  akṣaraṃ tryakṣaram ucchiṣyate tad evottaraṃ trirātram anuvidadhāti
PB  chandāṃsy evāsyās tṛtīyaṃ trirātraṃ vahanti
PB  tāṃ vā etāṃ pratīcīṃ tiraścīṃ parācīm āsate 'nnādyāya tasmāt pratyañcaṃ tiryañcaṃ parāñcaṃ prajāḥ paśum upajīvanti
PB  chandāṃsi vā anyo'nyasya lokam abhadhyāyan gāyatrī triṣṭubhas triṣṭub
jagatyā jagatī gāyatryās tāni vyauhan yathālokaṃ tato vai tāni yaṃyaṃ kāmam akāmayanta tam asanvan
PB  yatkāmo vyūḍhacchandasā dvadaśāhena yajate so 'smai kāmaḥ samṛdhyate
 PB  oko vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho yatho vai manuṣyā imaṃ lokam āviṣṭā evaṃ devatā dvādaśāham āviṣṭā devatā ha vā etena yajate ya evaṃv  
vidvān dvādaśāhena yajate 
PB  gṛhā vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho nāgṛhatāyā bhayyam
PB  yo vai dvādaśāham agniṣṭomena kalpamānaṃ veda kalpate 'smai prātaḥsavanenaiva
prathamas trirātraḥ kalpate mādhyandinena dvitīyas tṛtīyasavanena tṛtīyo 'gniṣṭomasāmnaiva
daśamam ahaḥ kalpate
PB  kalpate 'smai ya evaṃv veda
 PB  eti prety āśumad vītimad rukmat tejasvad yuñjānaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpaṃ trivṛtaḥ stomasya gāyatrasya chandaso rathantarasya sāmnaḥ 
PB  vṛṣavad vṛtravad rayimad viśvavad upasthitaṃ dvitīyasyāhno rūpaṃ pañcadaśasya stomasya traiṣṭubhasya chandaso bṛhataḥ sāmnaḥ
PB  udvat trivad digvat gomaṭ ṭaṣabhavat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ saptadaśasya stomasya jāgatasya chandaso vairūpasya sāmnaḥ
PB  rājanvaj janavadvat sūryavad virāḍanutodavac caturthasyāhno rūpam ekaviṃśasya stomasyānuṣṭubhasya chandaso 
rājasya vai sāmnaḥ
 PB  citravac chiśumat paṅktiḥ śakvarī dyūnākṣarā gomad ṛṣabhavad vajryabhimat pañcamasyāhno rūpaṃ triṇavasya stomasya pāṅktena chandaso  
śakvarīṇāṃ sāmnaḥ 
 PB  parivat prativat saptapadā dvipadā vinārāśaṃsā gomad ṛṣabhavat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ trayastriṃśasya stomasya sarveṣāṃ chandasāṃ rūpaṃ 
revatīnāṃ sāmnaḥ
PB  yasmād eṣā samānā satī ṣaḍahavibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād virūpaḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ
PB  virūpam enam anuprajāyate ya evaṃv veda
PB  agna iti prathamasyāhno rūpam agnivibhakter agnim iti dvitīyasyāgnineti tṛtīyasyāgnir iti caturthasya
PB  devā vai śriyam aicchaṃs tān na prathame 'hany avindan na dvitīye na
tṛtīye tāñ caturthe 'hany avindan vindate śriyaṃ ya evaṃ vedāgner iti pañcamasya
teno śrīḥ pratyupoditety āhuḥ
PB  aprativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  agna iti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti
PB  yasmād eṣā samānā saty agnivbhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv ādityas tapati
PB  indreti prathamasyāhno rūpam indravibhakter indram iti dvitīyasyendreṇeti
tṛtīyasyendra iti caturthasyendrād iti pañcamasyendreti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa
prayanti tad abhyudyanti yasmād eṣā samānā satīndravibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv oṣadhayaḥ pacyante
PB  yad ṛcā prastauti tat prathamasyāhno rūpam svaravibhakter yat purastāt
stobhaṃ tad dvitīyasya yad ubhayataḥ stobhaṃ tat tṛtīyasya yad anutunnaṃ tac caturthasya
yad abhyārabdhaṃ tat pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam
PB  svarāṇāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī svaravibhaktir nnānārūpā tasmād yathartu vāyuḥ pavate
PB  padanidhanaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam nidhanavibhakter bahirṇidhanaṃ dvitīyasya
niṃnidhanaṃ tṛtīyasyenidhanañ caturthasyāthakāraṇidhanaṃ pañcamasya yad ihākāreṇābhyastaṃ
tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī nidhanavibhaktir nnānārūpā
tasmād ime lokāḥ saha santo nānaiva
PB  dravadiḍaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam iḍāvibhakter ūrdhveḍaṃ dvitīyasya pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ
tṛtīyasyeḍābhir aiḍaṃ caturthasyādhyardheḍaṃ pañcamasya yad ihākāreṇābhyastaṃ tat
ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam iḍānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satīḍāvibhaktir nnānārūpā tasmāt samānāḥ
santaḥ paśavo nānārūpāḥ
PB  bharadvājāyanā vai sattram āsata tān apṛcchan kiṃ prathamenāhnā kuruteti
praivaimeti kiṃ dvitīyenety avasam evākurmahīti kiṃ tṛtīyeneti pary evāplavāmahīti
kiṃ caturtheneti sataiva sad apyadadhmeti kiṃ pañcameneti prāṇān eva vicchindanta
aimeti kiṃ ṣaṣṭhenetīdam evāgacchāmeti iti
PB  yasya padena prastauty atha svāram abhi vāva tena devāḥ paśūn apaśyan
yat purastāt stobhaṃ atha svāram ud eva tenāsṛjanata yad ubhayataḥ stobham atha svāram
ebhya eva tena lokebhyo devāḥ paśubhyo 'nnādyaṃ prāyacchan yad anutunnam atha svāram
upaiva tenāśikṣan yasya madhye nidhanam atha svāraṃ garbhāṃs tenādadhata tāni havatāsvāreṇa prājanayan
PB  imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ padanidhanenābhy ajayann amuṃ bahirṇidhanenāntarikṣaṃ
diṅnidhanenāmṛtatvam īnidhanenāgacchan brahmavarcasam athanidhanenāvārundhatāsminn
eva loka ihanidhanena pratyatiṣṭhan
PB  imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ dravadiḍenābhy ajayann amum ūrdhveḍenāntarikṣaṃ
pariṣṭubdheḍena pratiṣṭhām iḍābhir aiḍenāvārundhata pratiṣṭhāyādhyardheḍena vyajayantāsminn
eva loka iheḍena pratyatiṣṭhan
PB  na vāk saṃvatsaram ativadatīḍaiva saṃvatsaram ativadati garbheṇa saṃvatsare paryāvṛtya prajāyete tenātivadati
PB  tā vā etāś catasraḥ ṣaḍahaṃ parācya iḍā atiyanty eṣā nūtaiṣā viṣūcy eṣā pratīcy etad vīḍam
PB  saṃvatsaro 'gnir vāk samvatsaro yad agnir vibhajyate vācam eva tad vibhajanti
PB  dve dve akṣare vibhajanti dvau dvau hi māsāv ṛturatho māsānām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
 PB  ṣaḍ ahāni vibhajanti ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyā ṛtūnāṃ pratiṣṭhityā atho ṛtūnām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate ṣaḍ u puruṣā yān agnir anuvihriyate 
PB  yad idaṃ bahudhāgnir vihriyate tad asāv ādityaḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ pratyaṅ tasmād ete devate vibhaktim ānaśāte nāto 'nyā kā cana
PB  stomo yujyate sattriyebhyo ' harbhyaḥ pratnavatībhiś copavatībhiś ca
PB  yat pratnavatyo upavatībhyaḥ pūrvā yujyante brahma tat pūrvaṃ kṣatrād yujyate brahma hi pūrvaṃ kṣatram
PB  manas tat pūrvaṃ vāco yujyate mano hi yad dhi manasābhigacchati tad vācā vadati
PB  bṛhat tat pūrvaṃ rathantarād yujyate bṛhad dhi pūrvaṃ rathantarād vijityā tu vai rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe
PB  sambhāryās tṛcā bhavanti yathāśiṣṭhān vahiṣṭhān sambhared evam evaitān sambharanti gatyai
 PB  nava bhavanti navāhasya yuktyā ṛcarcaivāhar yunakti yathāprārthasya śamyā avadadhyād evam evaitan navāhasya śamyā avadadhāti gatyai 
PB  trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
PB  ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu
PB  nirāhāvanty ājyāni bhavanti yuktam eva tair āhvayati
PB  agna āyāhi vītaya ā no mitrāvaruṇāyāhi suṣamā hi ta indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ iti
PB  pra somāso vipaścita iti gāyatrī bhavati pretyā abhidroṇāni babhrava
ity abhikrāntyai stutā indrāya vāyava iti saṃskṛtyai pra soma deva vītaya iti pretyai
pra tu draveti pretyai pra vā etenāhnā yanti
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati
PB  yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  āśvaṃ bhavati
PB  aśvo vai bhūtvā prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa prājāyata bahur abhavat prajāyate bahur bhavaty āśvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  ekākṣaraṃ nidhanam upayanti rathantarasyānativādāya
PB  anativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  somasāma bhavati
PB  yathā vā imā anyā oṣadhayaḥ evaṃ soma āsīt sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat somasāmāpaśyat
tena rājyamādhipatyam agacchad yaśo 'bhavad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati yaśo bhavati
somasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  yaudhājayaṃ bhavati yad eva yaudhājayasya brāhmaṇam
PB  auśanaṃ yad auśanasya stomaḥ
PB  abhi tvā śūra no nu ma ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti kavatyas tena prājāpatyāḥ ko hi prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai
 PB  taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣahaṃ vasor mandānam andhaso 'bhivatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad 
PB  indraṃ gīrbhir havāmaha iti havanta evainam
 PB  tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomo vai taro yajño vidadvasuḥ stomena vai yajño yujyate yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum ity āha yajñam  
eva tad yunakti 
PB  rathantaraṃ bhavati brahma vai rathantaraṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad brahmākramya prayanti
PB  iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate
 PB  vāmadevyaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai prājāpatyaṃ vai vāmadevyaṃ prajāpatāv eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate 
PB  naudhasaṃ bhavati brahma vai naudhasaṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad rahmākramante
 PB  kāleyaṃ bhavati samānaloke vai kāleyañ ca rathantarañ ceyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ paśavaḥ kāleyam asyāñ caiva paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāya 
PB  dravadiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
PB  pra somāso madacyuta iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavṛt tṛtīyasavanaṃ
madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāty ayā pasvasva devayur ity eti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ
hy etad ahaḥ pavate 'har yato harir iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bṛhad eva tad etasminn ahani
yunakti tad yuktaṃ śva ārabhante pra sunvānāyāndhasa iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṇyam
iva hy etad ahar abhi priyāṇi pavate ca nohita ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  yajñā yajñā vo agnaya ity agner vai yajño yajña eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  saṃhitaṃ bhavati vyakṣaraṇidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai pratiṣṭhāyaiva sattram āsate
PB  saphaṃ bhavati
PB  saphena vai devā imān lokān samāpnuvvan yat samāpnuvaṃs tat saphasya saphatvam imān evaitena lokān samāpya sattram āsate
PB  ākṣāraṃ bhavati
PB  aṣṭau vā etāḥ kādughā āsaṃs tāsām 
ekā samaśīryata sā kṛṣir abhavad ṛdhyate 'smai kṛṣau ya evaṃ veda
PB  tāsu devāsurā aspardhanta te devā asurān kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇānudanta nudate bhrātṛvyaṃ kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  ebhyo vai lokebhyo raso 'pākrāmat taṃ prajāpatir ākṣāreṇākṣārayad yad ākṣārayat tad ākṣārasyākṣāratvam
PB  tasmād yaḥ purā puṇyo bhūtvā paścāt pāpīyān syād ākṣāraṃ brahma sāma kurvītātmany eved indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam ākṣārayati
PB  januṣaikarco bhavato 'hno dhṛtyai yad vā etasyāhno 'dhṛtaṃ tad etābhyāṃ dādhāra
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
PB  gaurīvitir vā etac chāktyo brāhmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavat
PB  atiriktaṃ vā etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitenāhīnāñ chavastanavad bhavaty api prajāyā upakḷptam
PB  vṛṣā vā etad vājisāma vṛṣabho retodhā adya stuvanti śvaḥ prajāyate
PB  anuṣṭubhi chandasāṃ kriyate 'nuṣṭub bhi chandasāṃ yoniḥ svāyām eva tad yonau reto dhatte prajātyai
PB  prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda
 PB  dvyudāsaṃ bhavaty etau vā udāsau svargasya lokasyāvasānadarśau pūrveṇa pūrvam ahaḥ saṃsthāpayanty uttareṇottaram ahar abhyativadanti 
PB  tad yathādaḥ pūrvedyuḥ spaṣṭaṃ tṛṇodakam anvavasyanto yanty evam eva tābhyāṃ svargaṃ lokam anvavasyanto yanti
PB  gautamaṃ bhavati
PB  sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  yad u caivānuṣtṭubhasya madhye nidhanasya brāhmaṇaṃ tad du caitasya
PB  kāvaṃ bhavati
PB  lokabinduḥ sāma vindate lokaṃ kāvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  svārasu svareṇa svareṇa hi devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pra yacchati
PB  yajñāyajñīyaṃ bhavati
PB  vāg yajñāyajñīyaṃ vāci yajñaḥ pratiṣṭhito vācy eva tad yajñam antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti taṃ vāco 'dhi śva ārabhante
PB  trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
PB  pratipad bhavati
PB  samārabhate dvirātrasyāvrisraṃsāya
PB  pavasvendo vṛṣāsuta ity anurūpyo bhavati vṛṣāvad vā eta aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  pūrvam u tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam
PB  anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
PB  stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  vṛṣaṇvantas tṛcā bhavatīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyai
PB  tṛca uttamo bhavati
PB  yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  pañdadaśa eva stomo bhavati
PB  ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhati ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ
PB  ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu
PB  nirāhopasthitāny ājyāni bhavanti
 PB  agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha indram id gāthino bṛhad indro agnā namo bṛhad iti bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati 
PB  vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
PB  vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  punānas soma dhārayeti dhṛtyai
PB  vṛṣā śoṇo abhikanikradad gā iti
PB  vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa samṛddhā vṛṣaṇvad vā etad aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  yauktāśvaṃ bhavati
PB  yuktāśvo va āṅgirasaḥ śiśū jātau viparyaharat tasmān mantro 'pākrāmat
sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad yauktāśvam apaśyat taṃ mantra upāvartata tad vāva sa tarhy
akāmayata kāmasani sama yauktāśvaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  āyāsye bhavataḥ
 PB  ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annādyam āśnāt taṃ śug ārcchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa ete āyāsye apaśyat tābhyāṃ śucam apāhatāpa  
śucaṃ hata āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ 
PB  ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tām ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayati vṛṣṭim āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  annādyaṃ vāva tad ebhyo lokebhyo 'pākrāmat tad ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayaty annādyam āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati
 PB  vasiṣṭho vā etena vaiḍavaḥ stutvāñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ 
PB  tvām id dhi havāmaha iti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  abhipravaḥ surādhasam iti yuñjate vai pūrveṇāhnā hy etena prayanti
PB  tvām idā hyo nara ity adya caiva hyaś ca samārabhate dvirātrasyāvisraṃsāya
PB  bṛhad bhavati varṣma vai bṛhad varṣma dvitīyam ahar varṣmaṇa eva tad varṣmākramante
PB  śyetaṃ bhavati sāmnorvāho yajñasya santatyai
PB  mādhucchandasaṃ bhavati sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  ūrdhveḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
PB  yas te mado vareṇya iti gāyatrī bhavati
PB  madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
PB  pavasva madhumattama iti pavanta iva hy etenāhnā madhumattama ity annaṃ vai madhv annādyam eva tad yajamāne dadhāti
PB  indram accha sutā ima itīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyai
PB  ayaṃ pūṣā rayir bhaga iti
PB  anuṣṭubhaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  vṛṣāmatīnāṃ pavate vicakṣaṇa iti jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  hāviṣmataṃ bhavati
PB  haviṣmāṃś ca vai haviṣkṛc cāṅgirasāv āstāṃ dvitīye 'hani haviṣmān arādhnon navame 'hani haviṣkṛt
PB  ayaṃ haviṣmān ity eva jātam ahar jātaṃ somaṃ prāha devebhyaḥ sāmnaivāsmā āśiṣam āśāste sāma hi saty āśīḥ
PB  śaṅku bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai yad vā adhṛtaṃ śaṅkunā tad dādhāra
 PB  tad u sīdantīyam iy āhur etena vai prajāpatir ūrdhva imān lokān asīdad yad asīdat tat sīdantīyasya sīdantīyatvam ūrdhva imān  
lokān sīdati sīdantīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ 
PB  sujñānaṃ bhavati
PB  svarvad vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ svarṇadhanaṃ bārhatam
PB  svarṇadhanaṃ bhavati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
PB  pluvau vā etāv upohante svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  krauñcaṃ bhavati
PB  vāg vai krauñcaṃ vāg dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai
PB  yāmaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai yamo 'napajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam āśnutānapajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam aśnute yāmena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  etena vai yamī yamaṃ svargaṃ lokam agamayat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
PB  ehy ū ṣu bravāṇi ta ity ehivatyai bhavanti tṛtīyasyāhna upahavāya santatyai
PB  apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāya
PB  evāhy asi vīrayur iti samānaṃ vadantīdam ittham asad iti
PB  indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhann ity avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitayā vardhanti
PB  sākam aśvaṃ bhavaty ukthānām abhijityā abhikrāntyai
PB  etena hy agra ukthāny adhyajayann etenābhyakrāman
PB  āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kḷptiś cānnādyañ ca samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyata idam ittham asad iti
PB  kṣatraṃ vā etad ahar abhinirvadati yat pañcadaśaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahmasāma
bhavati brahma caiva tat kṣatrañ ca sayujī karoti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhati
brahmaṇe kṣatrañ ca viśañ cānuge karoti
PB  brahma vai pūrvam ahaḥ kṣatraṃ dvitīyaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahma sāma bhavati brahma tad yaśasārdhayati brahma hi gāyatrī
PB  tad u samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyate samṛddhyai
PB  āṣṭādaṃṣṭre bhavataḥ
PB  aiyāhā iti vā indro vṛtram ahann aiyādohoveti nyagṛhṇād vārtraghne sāmanī vīryavatī
PB  ojo evaitābhyāṃ vīryam avarundhe
PB  pañcadaśa eva stomo bhavaty ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ
PB  davidyutaty āruceti tṛtīyasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
PB  davidyutatī vai gāyatrī pariṣṭobhantī triṣṭub gavāśīr jagatī trīṇi rūpāṇi samārabhate trirātrasyāvisraṃsāya
PB  ete asṛgram indava ity anurūpo bhavati
PB  eta iti vai prajāpatir devān asṛjatāsṛgram iti manuṣyān indava iti pitṛṃs tad eva tad abhivadati
 PB  pūrvam u caiva tad repam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpaṇo 'nuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ  
putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda 
PB  stotrīyānurūpau tṛco bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  rājā medhābhir īyate pavamāno manāv adhy antarikṣeṇa yātava iti
PB  antarikṣadevatyas tṛco bhavaty antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  pañcarcau bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhy upayānti
PB  saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
PB  agnināgniḥ samidhyata ity āgreyam ājyaṃ bhavati
PB  pūrve eva tad ahanī samiddhe tṛtīyam ahar abhisamindhe
PB  mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam iti rāthantaram maitrāvaruṇam
PB  huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpam
PB  rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati
PB  indreṇa saṃ hi dṛkṣusa ity aindram
PB  sam iva vā ime lokā dadṛśire 'ntarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  tā huve yayor idam iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
PB  huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
PB  uccā te jātam andhasa iti gāyatrī bhavati
PB  udvad vā etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  andhasvatī bhavaty ahar vā andho 'hna ārambhaḥ
PB  abhi somāsa āyava iti
PB  abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ
PB  tisro vāca īrayati pravahnir iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante
PB  triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  vaiṣṭambhaṃ bhavati
PB  ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā vaiṣṭambhair vyaṣṭabhnuvaṃs tad vaiṣṭambhasya vaiṣṭambhatvam
PB  diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
PB  paurūmadgaṃ bhavati
 PB  ahar vā etad avlīyamānaṃ tad rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tasmād devāḥ paurūmadgena rakṣāṃsy apāghnann apa pāpmānaṃ hate paurūmadgena 
 PB  devāś ca vāsurāś cāspardhanta te devā asurāṇāṃ paurūmadgena puro 'majjayan yat puro 'majjayaṃs tasmāt paurūmadgaṃ pāpmānam evaitena  
bhrātṛvyaṃ majjayati 
PB  gautamaṃ bhavati
PB  yad eva gautamasya brāhmaṇam
PB  ubhayataḥ stotraṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
PB  antarikṣaṃ bhavati
PB  antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyam antarikṣa eva tad antarikṣeṇa stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavati
PB  as iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ has iti bārhataṃ tṛtīyam eva tad rūpam upayanti samṛdhyai
PB  aṅgirasāṃ saṃkrośo bhavati
PB  etena vā aṅgirasaḥ saṃkrośamānāḥ svargaṃ lokam āpan svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
PB  yady āva indra te śatam iti śatavatyo bhavanti
PB  śatavad vai paśūnāṃ rūpaṃ sahasravat paśūnām evaitābhī rūpam avarūndhe
PB  vayaṅ ghatvā sutāvanta iti satobṛhatyo varṣīyaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
PB  taraṇir it siṣāsati vājaṃ purandhyā yujā
āva indraṃ puruhūtaṃ na me girety āvad akṣaram uddhatam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad eva tāvad akṣaraṃ bhavaty ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  pañcanidhanaṃ vairūpaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati diśāṃ dhṛtyai
PB  pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annāghasyāvarūdhyai
PB  diśāṃ vā etat sāma yad vairūpaṃ diśo hy evaitenābhivadati
PB  atha yat pañcanidhanaṃ tenartūnāṃ pañca hy ṛtavaḥ
 PB  ṛtubhiś ca vā ime lokā digbhiś cāvṛtās teṣv evobhayeṣu yajamānaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati yajamānaṃ vā anupratitiṣṭhantam udgātā pratitiṣṭhati  
ya evaṃ vidvān vairūpeṇodgāyati 
PB  digvad bhavati bhrātṛvyasyāpanutyai
PB  diśaṃ viśam iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
PB  has ity upariṣṭād diśāṃ nidhanam upayanti tena bārhatam
PB  rāthantaro vā ayaṃ loko bārhato 'sāv ubhe eva tad bṛhadrathantarayo rūpeṇāparādhnoti
PB  anaḍvāhau vā etau devayānau yajamānasya yad bṛhadrathantare tāv eva tad yunakti svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
PB  aśvavad bhavati prajātyai
PB  yathā maṇḍūka āṭ karoty evaṃ nidhanam upayanty ayātayāmatāyai
PB  dvādaśa vairūpāṇi bhavanti dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  mahāvaiṣṭambhaṃ brahmasāma bhavaty annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  yadā vai puruṣo 'nnam atty athāntarato viṣṭabdhaḥ
PB  diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
PB  sato bṛhatīṣu stuvanti pūrvayor ahnoḥ pratyudyamāya
PB  rauravam acchāvākasāma bhavati
PB  agnir vai rūro rūdro 'gniḥ
PB  agnir vā etasya paśūn apakramayati yasya paśavo 'pakrāmanty agnir eva tasya paśūn abhikramayati yasya paśavo 'bhikrāmanti
PB  abhy abhy evāsya paśavaḥ krāmanti ya evaṃ vidvān rauraveṇa stuvate
PB  pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
PB  ''tisro vāca udīrata'' iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante
PB  udvad vā etat trivad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  ''ā sotā pariṣiñcata'' iti parivatyo bhavanti
PB  anto vai tṛtīyam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
PB  ''sakhāya āniṣīdata'' ity uddhattam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad āha niṣīdatety ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  ''sutāso madhumattamā'' ity anuṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspata'' iti
PB  vitatam iva vā idam antarikṣam antareme antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  pāṣṭhauhaṃ bhavati
 PB  paṣṭhavāḍ vā etenāṅgirasaś caturthasyāhno vācaṃ vadantīm upāśṛṇot sa ho vāg iti nidhanam upait tad asyābhyuditaṃ tad ahar avasat 
PB  vācaḥ sāma bhavati
PB  vāg vai dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai
PB  niṣkirīyāḥ sattram āsata te tṛtīyam ahar na prājānaṃs tān etat sāma
gāyamānān vāg upāplavat tena tṛtīyam ahaḥ prājānaṃs te 'bruvann iyaṃ vāva nas tṛtīyam
ahar adīdṛśad iti tṛtīyasyaivaiṣāhno dṛṣṭiḥ
PB  śauktaṃ bhavati
PB  śuktir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  tvāṣṭrīsāma bhavati
PB  indraṃ vā akṣyāmayiṇaṃ bhūtāni nāsvāpayaṃs tam etena tvāṣṭrayo 'svāpayaṃs tad vāva tās tarhy akāmayanta
PB  kāmasani sāma tvāṣṭrīsāma kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
 PB  indro vṛtrād vibhyad gāṃ prāviśat taṃ tvāṣṭrayo 'bruvaṃ janayāmeti tam etaiḥ sāmabhir ajanayaṃ jāyāmahā iti vai sattram āsate 
PB  ariṣṭaṃ bhavati
PB  devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta yaṃ devānām aghnan na sa samabhavad
yam asurāṇāṃ saṃ so 'bhavat te devās tapo 'tapyanta ta etad ariṣṭam apaśyaṃs tato
'yaṃ devānām aghnat saṃ so 'bhavad yam asurāṇāṃ na sa samabhavad anenāriṣāmeti tad
ariṣṭasyāriṣṭatvam ariṣṭayā evāriṣṭam antataḥ kriyate
PB  trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai
PB  dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti caturthasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ
PB  pramaṃhiṣṭhāya gāyateti
PB  yad gāyateti mahasa eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
PB  ''taṃ te mad aṅgaṇīm asīti madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
PB  ''śrudhī havaṃ tiraścyā'' iti śrutyā eva
PB  pramaṃhiṣṭhīya bhavati
 PB  pramaṃhiṣṭhīyena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāvartayat tam astṛṇuta bhrātṛvyavān pramaṃhiṣṭhīyenokthāni praṇayeta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyaṃ  
vasīyāṃ ātmanā bhavati 
PB  hārivarṇaṃ bhavati
PB  indraś ca vai namuciś cāsuraḥ samadadhātāṃ na no naktan na divāhanan
nārdreṇa na śuṣkeṇeti tasya vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditye 'pāṃ phenena śiro 'chinad etad
vai na naktaṃ na divā yat vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditya etan nārdran na śuṣkaṃ yad apāṃ
phenas tad enaṃ pāpīyāṃ vācaṃ vadad anvavartata vīrahan na druho druha iti tan narcā
na sāmnāpahantum aśaknot
PB  hārivarṇasyaiva nidhanenāpāhata
PB  apaśucaṃhate hārivarṇasya nidhanena śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  tairaścayaṃ bhavati
PB  aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ yanto rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tāny etena tiraścāṅgirasas
tiryaṅ paryavaid yat tiryaṅ aparyavait tasmāt tairaścyaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata
taṃ tairaścyenāpāghnatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate tairaścyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
PB  ''pra ta āśvinīḥ pavamānadhenava'' iti caturthasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
PB  āpte trirātre rūpeṇa gāyatryo dvitīyaṃ prayanti prati vai gāyatryā rūpam
PB  jagatī pratipad bhavati jāgatam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ jagatyā eva taj jagatīm abhisaṃkrāmanti
PB  yad ato 'nyā pratipatsyāt pratikūlaṃ vānukūlaṃ vā syāt
PB  pavamāno ajījanad ity anurūpo bhavati
PB  janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati
PB  pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam
PB  anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
PB  stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  ṣaḍṛcau bhavata ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai
PB  tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
PB  ''janasya gopā ajaniṣṭa jāgṛviḥ'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
PB  janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati
PB  ''ayaṃ vāṃ mitrāvarūṇā'' iti bārhataṃ maitrāvarūṇam
PB  bṛhad etat parokṣaṃ yad vairājaṃ bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati
PB  ''indro dadhīco asthabhir'' iti dādhīcas tṛco bhavati
PB  dadhyaṅ vā āṅgiraso devānāṃ purodhānīya āsīd annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhā annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  ''iyaṃ vāmasya manmana'' ity aindrāgnam
 PB  ''indrāgnī pūrvyastutir abhrād vṛṣṭir ivājani'' ity ānuṣṭubhī vai vṛṣṭir ānuṣṭubham etad ahar yac caturthaṃ samīcyau virājau dadhāty  
annādyāya stomaḥ 
PB  ''payasva dakṣasādhana'' iti gāyatrī bhavati sidhyai
PB  yat pavasveti tad bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''tavāhaṃ soma rāraṇa sakhya indo dive dive
purūṇi babhro nicaranti mām ava paridhīṃr atitāṃ ihi'' iti
PB  ati hy āyañ chakunā iva paptim ety ati hy apatat
PB  punāno akramīd abhīti
PB  gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  caturṇidhanam ātharvaṇaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai
PB  catuṣpadānuṣṭubhānuṣṭubham etad ahar yac caturtham
PB  bheṣajaṃ vātharvaṇāni bheṣajam eva tat karoti
PB  nidhanakāmaṃ bhavati
PB  ekaṃ vā anyena niruktena nidhanena kāmaṃ sanoty athaitan nidhanakāmaṃ sarveṣāṃ kāmānām avarudhyai
PB  āṣṭādaṃṣṭraṃ bhavati
PB  yad evāṣṭādaṃṣṭrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  ābhīśavaṃ bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
PB  yad vā adhṛtam abhīśunā tad dādhāra
PB  anutunnaṃ gāyati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
PB  caturṇidhanam āṅgirasaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai
PB  svaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
PB  sattrāsāhīyaṃ bhavati
PB  yad vā asurāṇām asoḍham āsīt tad devāḥ sattrāsāhīyenāsahanta sattrainān asakṣmahīti tat sattrāsāhīyasya sattrāsāhīyatvam
PB  sattrā bhrātṛvyaṃ sahate sattrāsāhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  vṛṣaṇvatyo gāyatrayo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān nayanti stomaḥ
PB  ''pibā somam indra mandatu tvā yante suṣāva haryaśvādriḥ
sotur bāhubhyāṃ suyato nārvā'' ity ayatam iva vai caturtham ahas tasyaiva yatyai
PB  viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhibhṛtarannara ity atijagatī varṣīyayaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
PB  apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yaj jayāyasaś chandasaḥ kanīyaś chanda upaiti yad eṣā caturthe 'hany atijagatī kriyate 'napabhraṃśāya
PB  yo rājā carṣaṇīnām iti
PB  rājye hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan rājyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
 PB  chandobhir vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃ vairājasya nidhanenādṛṃhaṃs tasmāt parāṅ cārvāṅ cādityas tapati  
parāṅ cārvāṅ cekāraḥ 
PB  prastāvaṃ prastutya viṣṭambhān viṣṭabhnoti mukhata eva tad annādyaṃ dhatte mukhaṃ hi sāmnaḥ prastāvaḥ
PB  daśakṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti daśākṣarā virāṅ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  triṃśatkṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti bhūyaso 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  vairājaṃ sāma bhavati virāṭsu stuvanti vairājā viṣṭambhāḥ samīcīr virājo dadhāty annādyāya
PB  anutunnaṃ gāyati retodheyāyānutunnād dhi reto dhīyate
PB  dakṣiṇa ūrāv udgatur agniṃ manthanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyate
PB  upākṛte 'hiṅkṛte manthanti jātam abhihiṅkaroti
PB  tasmāj jātaṃ putraṃ paśavo 'bhihiṅkurvanti
PB  tasmai jātāyāmīmāṃsanta gārhapatye praharāmā āgnīdhrā āhavanīyā iti
PB  āhavanīye praharanty etad āyatano vai yajamāno yadā havanīye svam eva tad āyatanaṃ jyotiṣmat karoti
PB  jyotiṣmān brahmavarcasī bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  abhijuhoti śāntyai
PB  ājyenābhijuhoti tejo vā ājyaṃ teja eva tad ātman dhatte
PB  ''preddho agne dīdihi puro na'' iti virājābhijuhoty annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavati
PB  atijagatīṣu stuvanty ahna utkrāntyā ud vā etenāhnā krāmanti
PB  diveti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyā apapāpmānaṃ hate traiśokena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  bhāradvājasya pṛśny achāvākasāma bhavati
PB  annaṃ vai devāḥ pṛśnīti vadanty annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  iḍābhir aiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
PB  ''paripriyā divaḥ kavir'' iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai caturtham ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
PB  tvaṃ hy aṅga daivyeti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  somaḥ punāna ūrmiṇā vyaṃvāraṃ vidhāvati
agre vācaḥ pavamānaḥ kanikradad iti
PB  agraṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchann agram evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
PB  ''puro jitīvo andhasā'' iti virājau vairājaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''somaḥ pavate janitā matīnām'' iti prātassavane ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītaṃ taṃ tṛtīyasavane prajanayanti
PB  triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  aurṇāyavaṃ bhavati
PB  aṅgiraso vai sattram āsata teṣām āptaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo loka āsīt panthānaṃ
tu devayānaṃ na prājānaṃs teṣāṃ kalyāṇa āṅgiraso dhyāyam udavrajat sa ūrṇāyuṃ gandharvam
apsarasāṃ madhye preṅkhayamāṇam upait sa iyām iti yāṃ yām abhyadiśat sainam akāmayata
tam abhyavadat kālyāṇā ity āso vai vaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ
na prajānīthedaṃ sāma svargyaṃ lokam eṣy atha mā tu vocoham adarśam iti
PB  sa ait kalyāṇaḥ so 'bravīd āpto vai naḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ
tu devayānaṃ prajānīma idaṃ sāma svargyaṃ tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam eṣyāma iti kas
te 'vocad ity aham evādarśam iti tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam āyann ahīyata kalyāṇo
'nṛtaṃ hi so 'vadat sa eṣaḥ śvitraḥ
PB  svargyaṃ vā etat sāma svargalokaḥ puṇyaloko bhavaty aurṇāyavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  bṛhatkaṃ bhavati
PB  sāmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ tvaṃ hīty annādyasyāvarudhyai hīti vā annaṃ pradīyate ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati
PB  ātīṣādīyaṃ bhavati
PB  āyur vā ātīṣādīyam āyuṣo 'ṣarudhyai
PB  ātamitor nidhanam upayanty āyur eva sarvam āpnuvanti
PB  nānadaṃ bhavati
PB  jyāyo 'bhyārambham atihāya pañcam ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhna ārambhas tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
PB  ṣoḍaśākṣareṇa prastauti ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati
PB  āndhīgavaṃ bhavati
PB  kayor annādyam avarūndha āndhīgavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vātsapraṃ bhavati
PB  etasmin vai vairājaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ pratitiṣṭhati vātsapreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
 PB  vatsaprīr bhālandanaḥ śraddhāṃ nāvindata sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad vātsapram apaśyat sa śraddhām avindata śraddhā vindāmahā iti  
vai sattram āsate vindate śraddhām 
PB  īnidhanaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
PB  ''agniṃ vo vṛdhantam'' iti
PB  avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam eva tathā vardhayanti
PB  ''vayam u tvām apūrvya'' ity apūrvāṃ hy etarhi prajāpates tanūm agacchann apūrvam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
 PB  ''imam indra sutaṃ piba jyeṣṭham amartyaṃ madam'' iti jyaiṣṭhaṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan jyaiṣṭhyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti 
PB  saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati
 PB  sindhukṣid vai rājanyarṣir jyog aparuddhaś caran sa etat saindhukṣitam apaśyat so 'vāgacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhati  
saindhukṣitena tuṣṭuvānaḥ 
PB  saubharaṃ bhavati bṛhatas tejaḥ
PB  pannam iva vai caturtham ahas tad etena bṛhatas tejasottabhnoti saubhareṇa
PB  vasiṣṭhasya priyaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai vasiṣṭha indrasya premāṇam agacchat premāṇaṃ devatānāṃ gacchati vāsiṣṭhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
PB  indraś ca bṛhac ca samabhavatāṃ tam indraṃ bṛhad ekayā tanvāty aricyata
tasyā abibhedanayā mābhibhaviṣyatīti so 'bravīt ṣoḍaśī te 'yaṃ yajñakratur astv iti
sa ṣoḍaśy abhavat tad asya janma
PB  atiśriyā bhrātṛvyaṃ ricyate yo gāyatrīṣu dvipadāsu bṛhatā ṣoḍaśinā stute
PB  ''upa no haribhiḥ stutam'' ity etā vai gāyatryo dvipadā etāsu stotavyam
 PB  indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etām anuṣṭubham apaharasaṃ prāyacchat tayā nāstṛṇuta yad astṛtā vyanadat tan  
nānadasya nānadatvam 
PB  taṃ punar upādhāvat tasmai saptānāṃ hotrāṇāṃ haro nirmāya prāyacchat tam astṛṇuta
PB  stṛṇute taṃ yaṃ tustūrṣate ya evaṃ veda
PB  tasmād dharivatīṣu stuvanti harivatīḥ śaṃsanti harivatīṣu graho gṛhyate haro hy asmai nirmāya prāyacchat
PB  ekaviṃśāyatano vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī sapta hi prātassavane hotrā vaṣaṭkurvanti sapta mādhyandine savane sapta tṛtīyasavane
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
PB  gaurīvitir vā etac chāktyo brahmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam
abhavad atiriktaṃ etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinaṃ śvastanavān
bhavaty api prajāyā upakḷptaḥ
 PB  viśālaṃ libjayā śrūtyābhyadhād iti hovācopoditir gopāleyo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadam akar gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinam astoṣṭāñjasā śriyam upāgān  
na śriyā avapadyata iti 
 PB  eṣa vai viśālaṃ libjayā bhūtyābhidadhāti yo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadaṃ kṛtvā gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinā stute 'ñjasā śriyam upaiti na śriyā 
PB  śakvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta vajrī syām iti
PB  vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vajraḥ śakvaryo vajreṇaivāsmai vajraṃ spṛṇoti vajrī bhavati
PB  anuṣṭupsu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta na mā vāg ativadet
PB  vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vāg anuṣṭub vajreṇaivāsmai vācaṃ spṛṇoti nainaṃ vāg ativadati
PB  ''asāvi soma indra ta'' ity etāsu stotavyam
PB  virāṭsv annādyakāmaḥ ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vairājam annaṃ vajreṇaivāsmā annaṃ spṛṇoty annādo bhavati
PB  ''pra vo mahe vṛdhe bharadhvam'' ity etāsu stotavyam
PB  trayastriṃśadakṣarā vā etā virājo yad ekaviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhā sā yad dvādaśa prajātiḥ sā
PB  pratiṣṭhāya prajāyate no cāntasthāyāṃ jīryate ya evaṃ veda
PB  atha vā etā ekapadās tryakṣarā viṣṇoś chando bhurijaḥ śakvaryaḥ
PB  etābhir vā indro vṛtram ahan kṣipraṃ vā etābhiḥ pāpmānaṃ hanti kṣipraṃ vasīyān bhavati
PB  catustriṃśadakṣarāḥ saṃstuto bhavati trayastriṃśaddevattāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpatim evopayanty ariṣṭyai
PB  hiraṇyaṃ sampradāyaṃ ṣoḍaśinā stuvate jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati
PB  aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa upatiṣṭhati sāmyekṣayāya bhrātṛvyalokam eva sa vidhamaṃs tiṣṭhati
PB  ekākṣaraṃ vai devānām avamaṃ chanda āsīt saptākṣaraṃ paramaṃ navākṣaram
asurāṇām avamaṃ chanda āsīt pañcadaśākṣaraṃ paramaṃ devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta
