tān prajāpatir ānuṣṭubho bhūtvāntarātiṣṭhat taṃ devāsurā vyahvayanta sa devān upāvartata
tato devā abhavan parāsurāḥ
PB  bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  te devā asurāṇām ekākṣareṇaiva pañcadaśākṣaram avṛñjata dvyakṣareṇa
caturdaśākṣaraṃ tryakṣareṇa trayodaśākṣaraṃ caturakṣareṇa dvādaśākṣaraṃ pañcākṣareṇaikādaśākṣaraṃ
ṣaḍakṣareṇa daśākṣaraṃ saptākṣareṇa navākṣaram aṣṭābhir evāṣṭāv avṛñjata
PB  evam eva bhrātṛvyād bhūtiṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
 PB  aparuddhayajña iva vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī kanīyasvina iva vai tarhi devā āsan bhūyasvino 'surāḥ kanīyasvina bhūyasvinaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ  
vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda 
PB  ''yasmād anyo na paro 'sti jāto ya ābabhūva bhuvanāni viśvā
prajāpatiḥ prajayā samvidānas trīṇi jyotīṃ ṣi sacate sa ṣoḍaśī'' ity udgātā graham avekṣate
PB  jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
PB  ''govit pavasva vasuvid dhiraṇyavid'' iti pañcamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
PB  govid vā etad vasuvid dhiraṇyavidyac chakvaryaḥ
PB  paśavaś śakvaryaḥ sarvaṃ paśubhir vindate
PB  ''tvaṃ suvīro asi somaviśvavid'' ity eṣa yāva suvīro yasya paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  tās te kṣarantu madhumad ghṛtaṃ paya'' iti madhumad vai ghṛtaṃ payaḥ paśavaḥ kṣaranti tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  ''pavamānasya viśvavid'' ity anurūpo bhavati
PB  viśvam eva tadvit tam abhivadati viśvaṃ hi paśubhir vindate
PB  ''pra te sargā asṛkṣata'' iti sṛṣṭānīva hy etarhy ahāni
PB  pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam
anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurupau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  saptarcau bhavataḥ chandasāṃ dhṛtyai
PB  caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhy udyanti
PB  triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭaḥ
PB  ''tava śriyo varṣasy eva vidyuta'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
PB  śrīr vai paśavaḥ śrīḥ śakvaryaḥ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  ''agneś cikitra uṣasām ivetaya'' itītānīva hy etarhy ahānīti
PB  ''ā te yatente rathyo yathā pṛthag'' ity eva hy etarhy ahāni yatante
PB  ''purūruṇā cid dhy asty avo nūnaṃ vāṃ varuṇa'' iti maitrāvaruṇam
PB  yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajati
PB  ''uttiṣṭhann ojasā saha'' ity aindram
PB  pañca vā ṛtava utthānasya rūpam ojasā sahety ojasaiva vīryeṇa sahottiṣṭhanti
PB  ''indrāgnī yuvām ima'' iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
PB  rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yac chakvaryo rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
PB  ''arṣā soma dyumattama'' iti viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti
PB  brahma vai gāyatrī yajño viṣṇur brahmaṇy eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  ''soma uṣvāṇas sotṛbhir'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaitās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
PB  ''yat soma citram ukthyam'' iti gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  yaṇvaṃ bhavati paśavo vai yaṇvaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
PB  santataṃ gāyati yajñasya santatye
PB  adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
PB  śākalaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai śakalaḥ pañcame 'hani pratyatiṣṭhat pratitiṣṭhati śākalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vārśaṃ bhavati
PB  vṛśo vaijānas tryaruṇasya traidhātavasyaikṣvākasya purohita āsīt sa
aikṣvāko 'dhāvayat brāhmaṇakumāraṃ rathena vyacchinat sa purohitam abravīt tava mā
purodhāyām idam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata
kāmasani sāma vārśaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
PB  mānavaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai manuḥ prajāpatiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati mānavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  ānūpaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai vadhryaśva ānūpaḥ paśūnāṃ bhūmānam āśnuta paśūnāṃ bhūmānam aśnuta ānūpena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vāmraṃ bhavati
PB  māmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ yaṃ vai gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ praśaṃsanti vāma iti taṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti
PB  adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
PB  triṇidhanam āgneyaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
 PB  agriḥ sṛṣṭo nodadīpyata taṃ prajāpatir etena sāmnopādhamat sa udadīpyata dīptiś ca vā etat sāma brahmavarcasaṃ ca dīptiś caivaitena  
brahmavarcasaṃ cāvarundhe 
PB  śaiśavaṃ bhavati
PB  śiśur vā āṅgiraso mantrakṛtāṃ mantrakṛd āsīt sa pitṛn putrakā ity āmantrayata
taṃ pitaro 'bruvan na dharmaṃ karoṣi yo naḥ pitṛn sataḥ putrakā ity āmantrayama iti
so 'bravīd ahaṃ vāva vaḥ pitāsmi yo mantrakṛd asmīti
taṃ deveṣv apṛcchanta te devā abuvann eṣa vāva pitā yo mantrakṛd iti tad vai sa udajayad ujjayati śaiśavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ
PB  indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etac chandobhya indriyaṃ
vīryaṃ nirmāya prāyacchad etena śaknuhīti tac chakvarīṇāṃ śakvarītvaṃ sīmānam abhinat
tat simā mahnyam akarot tan mahnyā mahān ghoṣa āsīt tan mahānāmnyaḥ
PB  diśaḥ pañcapadā dādhārartūn ṣaṭpadā chandāṃsi saptapadā puruṣaṃ dvipadā
PB  dvyopaśāḥ saṃstutā bhavanti tasmād dvyopaśāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  iḍe abhito 'thakāraṃ tasmāc chṛṅge tīkṣṇīyasī stūpāt
PB  upakṣudrā gāyati tasmād upakṣudrāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  aṃsaśliṣṭā gāyati tasmād asaṃśliṣṭāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  nānārūpā gāyati tasmān nānārūpāḥ paśavaḥ
PB  āpo vai kṣīrarasā āsaṃste devāḥ pāpavasīyasād abibhayur yad apa upanidhāya stuvate pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai
PB  vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  gāyatram ayanaṃ bhavati brahmavarcasakāmasya svarṇidhanaṃ madhunāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhate
traiṣṭubham ayanaṃ bhavaty ojaskāmasyāthakāraṇidhana mājyenāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhate
jāgatam ayanaṃ bhavati paśukāmasyeḍānidhanaṃ payasāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhate
PB  añjasāryo mālyaḥ śakvarīḥ prārautsīd iti hovācālammaṃ pārijānataṃ rajanaḥ
kauṇayo yady enāḥ pratiṣṭhāpaṃ śakṣyatīty etad vā etāsām añjayati pratiṣṭhitā ya
ābhiḥ kṣipraṃ prastutya kṣipram udgāyati
PB  śakvarībhiḥ stutvā purīṣeṇa stuvate
PB  paśavo vai śakvaryo gauṣṭhaḥ purīṣaṃ goṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartyanty avisraṃsāya
PB  ''indro madāya vāvṛdha'' ity avardhanta hy etarhi
PB  tāsu bārhadgiram
PB  ''svādor itthā viṣuvata'' iti viṣuvān vai pañcamam ahas tāsu rāyovājīyam
PB  indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta pṛthuraśmir
bṛhadgirī rāyovājas te 'bruvan ko na imān putrān bhariṣyatīty aham itīndro 'bravīt
tān ādhinidhāya paricāryaṃ carad 
vardhayaṃs tān vardhayitvābravīt kumārakā varān vṛṇīdhvam iti
 kṣatraṃ mahyam ity abravīt pṛthuraśmis tasmā etena pārthuraśmena kṣatraṃ prāyacchat kṣatrakāma etena stuvīta kṣatrasyaivāsya prakāśo bhavati 
brahmavarcasaṃ mahyam ity abravīt bṛhādgiris tasmā etena bārhadgireṇa prāyacchat brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavati
paśūn mahyam ity abravīd rāyovājas tasmā etena rāyovājīyena paśūn prāyacchat paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati
 PB  pārthuraśmaṃ rājanyāya brahmasāma kuryāt bārhadgiraṃ brāhmaṇāya rāyovājīyaṃ vaiśyāya svenaivenāṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati stomaḥ 
PB  ''asāvy aṃśur madāya'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
PB  ''abhi dyumnaṃ bṛhadyaśa'' ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayos saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ
PB  ''prāṇā śiśur mahīnām'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ mahyo hi simāḥ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
PB  ''pavasva vājasātaya'' iti vaiṣṇavyo 'nuṣṭubho bhavanti
PB  yajño vai viṣṇur yad atra nāpi kriyate tad viṣṇunā yajñenāpi karoti
PB  ''indur vājī pavate gonyoghā'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
PB  triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  santani bhavati pañcamasyāhnas santatyai
PB  vāg vā eṣā pratatā yad dvādaśāhas tasyā eṣa viṣuvān yat pañcamam ahas tām evaitena santanoti
PB  cyāvanaṃ bhavati
PB  prajātir vai cyāvanaṃ prajāyate bahur bhavati cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
 PB  ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tāṃ prajāpatiś cyāvanenācyāvayad yad acyāvayat tac cyāvanasya cyāvanatvaṃ cyāvayati vṛṣṭiṃ  
cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ 
PB  kroṣa bhavati
PB  etena vā indra indrakrośe viśvāmitrajamadagnī imā gāva ity ākrośat paśunām avarudhyai krośaṃ kriyate
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  ṛṣabhaḥ śākvaro bhavati
PB  paśavo vai śakvaryaḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apy arjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
PB  pārthaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai pṛthur vainya ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśunām ādhipatyam aśnute pārthena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  aṣṭeḍaḥ padastobho bhavati
 PB  indro vṛtrāya vajram udayacchat taṃ ṣoḍaśabhir bhogaiḥ paryabhujat sa etaṃ padastobham apaśyat tenāpāveṣṭayad apāveṣṭayann iva  
gāyet pāpmano 'pahatyai 
PB  pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ padastobhenāpāhatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate padastobhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  pador uttamam apaśyat tat padastobhasya padastobhatvam
PB  dvādaśanidhano bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  dāśaspatyaṃ bhavati
PB  yāṃ vai gāṃ praśaṃsanti dāśaspatyeti tāṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti
PB  nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
PB  ''āte agna idhīmahi'' iti
PB  apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva
PB  ''indrāya sāma gāyata'' iti pūrṇāḥ kakubhas tenānaśanāyuko bhavati
PB  puruṣo vai kakup puruṣam eva tan madhyataḥ prīṇāti
PB  ''asāvi soma indra ta'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
PB  sañjayaṃ bhavati
PB  devāś ca vā asurāś ca samadadhata yatare naḥ sañjayāṃs teṣāṃ naḥ paśavo
'sān iti te devā asurān sañjayena samajayan yat samajayaṃs tasmāt sañjayaṃ paśūnām
avarudhyai sañjayaṃ kriyate
PB  saumitraṃ bhavati
PB  dīrghajihvī vā idaṃ rakṣo yajñahā yajñiyān avalihaty acarat tām indraḥ
kayācana māyayā hantuṃ nāśaṃsatātha ha sumitraḥ kutsaḥ kalyāṇa āsa tam abravīd imām
acchā brūṣveti tām acchā brūta sainam abravīn nāhaitan na śuśruva priyam iva tu me
hṛdayasyeti tām ajñapayat tāṃ saṃskṛte 'hatāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani
sāma saumitraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
 PB  sumitraḥ san krūram akar ity enaṃ vāg abhyavadat taṃ śug ārcchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat saumitram apaśyat tena śucam apāhatāpaśucaṃ  
hate saumitreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ 
PB  mahāvaiśvāmitraṃ bhavati
PB  pāpmānaṃ hatvā yad amahīyanta tan mahāvaiśvāmitrasya mahāvaiśvāmitratvam
PB  hāyā ihayā ohā oheti paśūn evaitena nyauhanta
PB  trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai
PB  dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ santatyai
PB  triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭhaḥ
PB  ''jyotir yajñasya pavate madhupriyam'' iti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
 PB  jyotir vai gāyatrī chandamāṃ jyotiḥ revatī sāmnāṃ jyotis trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ jyotir eva tat samyak saṃdadhāsy api ha putrasya  
putro jyotiṣmān bhavati 
PB  ''madhu priyam'' iti paśavo vai revatyo madhupriyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  ''madintamo matsara indriyo rasa'' itīndriyaṃ vai vīryaṃ rasaḥ paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati
PB  ''amṛkṣata pravājina'' ity anurūpo bhavati
PB  sṛṣṭānīva hy etarhy ahāni
PB  pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa
rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurūpau
tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  daśarcau bhavato daśākṣarā virāṭ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  uttaro daśarco bhavati sodarka indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya
PB  yatra ve devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
PB  caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  dhvasre vai puruṣantī tarantapurumīḍhābhyāṃ vaitadaśvibhyāṃ sahasrāṇy
aditsatāṃ tāv aikṣetāṃ kathaṃ nāv idam āttam apratigṛhītaṃ syād iti tau praty etāṃ
dhvasrayoḥ puruṣantyor ā sahasrāṇi dadmahe daprahe
tarat sa mandī dhāvatīti tato vai tat tayor āttam apratigṛhītam abhavat
PB  āttam asyāpratigṛhītaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  vinārāśaṃso bhavaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvarudhyai mānuṣasya ca daivasya ca
PB  tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
PB  ''imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedasa'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati sodarkam
indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
PB  ''prativāṃ sūra udita'' iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam
PB  anto vai sūro 'nta etat ṣaṣṭham ahar ahnām anta eva tad ante stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
 PB  ''bhindhi viśvā apadviṣa'' ity aindraṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs  
tad anunyatudan 
 PB  ''yajñasya hi stha ṛtvija'' ity aindrāgnaṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam  
apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan stomaḥ 
PB  ''indrāyendo marutvata'' iti marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti
PB  marutvad dhi mādhyandinaṃ savanam
PB  ''mṛjyamānaḥ suhastya'' iti simānāṃ rūpam
PB  samānaṃ vai simānāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ ca simābhyo hy adhirevatyaḥ prajāyante
PB  ''etam u tyaṃ daśa kṣipa'' ity ādityā ādityā vā imāḥ prajās tāsām eva madhyataḥ pratitiṣṭhati
PB  gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  iṣovṛdhīyaṃ bhavati
PB  paśavo vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ paśūnām avarudhyā iṣe vai pañcamam ahar vṛdhe ṣaṣṭham avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitena vardhayanti
PB  krauñcaṃ bhavati
PB  kruṅṅ eṣyam ahar avindad eṣyam iva vai ṣaṣṭham ahar evaitena vindanti
PB  vājadāvaryo bhavanti
PB  annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai yadā hi vā annam atha gaur athāśvo 'tha puruṣo vājī
PB  revatyo bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  ṣaṇṇidhanī ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai
PB  āpo vai revatyas tā yat pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryur apaśur yajamānaḥ syāt paśūn asya
nirdaheyur yatra vā āpo vivartante tad oṣadhayo jāyante 'tha yatrāvatiṣṭhante nirmṛtukās
tatra bhavanti tasmāt pavamāne kurvanti parācā hi pavamānena stuvate
PB  methī vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ rajjuḥ krauñcaṃ vatso vājadāvaryo revatyo mātaro yad etāny evaṃ sāmāni kriyanta evam eva prattāṃ dugdhe
PB  aukṣṇorandhre bhavataḥ
PB  ukṣṇorandhro vā etābhyāṃ kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vājajid bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvaṃ vā ete vājaṃ jayanti ye ṣaṣṭham ahar āgacchanti
PB  annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  varuṇasāma bhavati
PB  etena vai varuṇo rājyam ādhipatyam agacchad yaśo 'bhavad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati yaśo bhavati varuṇasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  aṅgirasāṃ goṣṭho bhavati
PB  paśavo vai revatyo gauṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartayanty avisraṃsāya
PB  ihavad vāmadevyaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai vāmadevo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhā annasyāvarudhyai
PB  gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarñcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ
PB  yātayāmāny anyāni chandāṃsy ayātayāmā gāyatrī tasmād gāyatrīṣu stuvanti
PB  ''surūpa kṛtnum ūtaya'' ity abhyārambheṇa ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
PB  ''ubhe yad indra rodasī'' iti ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
PB  revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
 PB  apāṃ vā eṣa raso yad revatyo revatīnāṃ raso yad vāravantīyaṃ sarasā eva tad revatīḥ prayuṅkte yad vāravantīyena pṛṣṭhena stuvate 
PB  revad vā etad raivatyaṃ yad vāravantīyam asya revān revātyā jāyate
PB  revān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  keśine vā etad dālbhyāya sāmāvir abhavat tad enam abravīd agātāro mā
gāyanti mā mayodgāsiṣur iti kathaṃ ta āgā bhagava ity abravīd āgeyam evāsmy āgāyann
iva gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai tad alammaṃ pārijānataṃ paścādakṣaṃ śayānam etām āgāṃ gāyantam
ajānāt tam abravīt puras tvā dadhā iti tam abruvan ko nv ayaṃ kasmā alam ity alaṃ
nu vai mahyam iti tad alammasyālammatvam
PB  iheheti gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  ṛṣabho raivato bhavati
PB  paśavo vai raivatyaḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
PB  śyeno bhavati
PB  śyeno ha vai pūrvapretāni vayāṃsy āpnoti pūrvapretānīva vai pūrvāṇy ahāni teṣām āptyai śyenaḥ kriyate
 PB  śyeno vā etad ahaḥ sampārayitum arhati sa hi vayasām āśiṣṭhas tasyānapahananāya sampāraṇāyaitat kriyate 'nto hi ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ  
saptamaṃ ca 
PB  brahmavādino vadanti yad bṛhad āyatanāni pṛṣṭhāny athaite dve gāyatryau dve jagatyau kva tarhi bṛhatyo bhavantīti
PB  ye dve jagatyoḥ pade te gāyatryā upasampadyete tat sarvā bṛhatyo bhavanty āyatane pṛṣṭhāni yātayatyāyatanavān bhavati
PB  ṣaṭpadāsu stuvanti ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai
PB  saptapadayā yajati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ
PB  ''parisvāno giriṣṭhā'' iti parivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti sarvasya paryāptyai
PB  ''sasunveyo vasūnām'' iti paśavo vai vasu paśūnām avarudhyai
PB  ''taṃ vassakhāyo madāya'' iti vālakhilyāḥ
PB  vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca
PB  yad etau vālakhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva vyatiṣaṅgayāvyatisraṃsāya santatyai
PB  ''somāḥ pavanta indava'' ity anuṣṭubho nibhasado bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  ''ayā pavā pavasvainā vasūni'' iti triṣṭubhas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brahmāṇam
PB  vaidanvātāni bhavanti
 PB  vidanvān vai bhārgava indrasya pratyahaṃs taṃ śug ārcchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etāni vaidanvatāny apaśyat taiḥ śucam apāhatāpaśucaṃ  
hate vaidanvatais tuṣṭuvānaḥ 
PB  bharadvājasya lomata bhavati
PB  paśavo vai loma paśūnām avarudhyai
PB  tad u dīrgham ity āhur āyur vai dīrgham āyuṣo 'varudhyai
PB  kārṇaśravasaṃ bhavati śṛṇvanti tuṣṭuvānam
PB  karṇaśravā vā etad āṅigarasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati gaur
ivitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  madhuścyunnidhanaṃ bhavati
PB  paramasyānnādyasyāvarudhyai paramaṃ vā etad annādya yan madhu
 PB  prajāpater vā etau stanau yad ghṛtaścyunnidhanaṃ ca madhuścyunnidhanaṃ ca yajño vai prajāpatis tam etābhyāṃ dugdhe yaṃ kāmaṃ  
kāmayate taṃ dugdhe 
PB  krauñce bhavataḥ
PB  śnauṣṭhaṃ bhavati
PB  śnuṣṭir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāt lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  agner vā etad vaiśvānaraṃ sāma dīdihīti nidhanam upayanti dīdā eva hy agnir vaiśvānaraḥ
PB  nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
PB  brahmavādino vadanti prāyaṇato dvipadāḥ kāryā udayanatā iti
PB  udayanata eva kāryāḥ puruṣo vai dvipadāḥ pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  vācā vai sarvaṃ yajñaṃ tanvate tasmāt sarvāṃ vācaṃ puruṣo vadati sarvā hy asmin saṃstutā pratitiṣṭhati
PB  gūrdo bhavati
PB  gopāyanānāṃ vai sattram āsīnānāṃ kirātakulyāv asuramāye antaḥparidhy
asūn prākiratāṃ te ''agre tvan no antama'' ity agnim upāsīdaṃs tenāsūn aspṛṇvaṃs
tad vāva te tarhy akāmayanta kāmasani sāma gūrdaḥ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  gotamasya bhandra bhavati
PB  āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ
PB  etena vai gotamo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchat tasmād ye ca parāñco gotamād ye cārvāñcas ta ubhaye gotamā ṛṣayo bruvate
PB  udvaṃśaputrā bhavati
PB  yad vā udvaṃśīyaṃ tad udvaṃśaputraḥ
PB  ardheḍām atisvarati
PB  tasmād ūdhardhārā ati carantīḍāyām antataḥ paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  kḷpta upariṣṭād ṛk sāma ca vimucyete abhy u svareṇa saptamam ahaḥ svarati santatyai
PB  ūhuṣīva vā etarhi vāg yadā ṣaḍahaḥ santiṣṭhate na bahu vaden nānyaṃ pṛcchen nānyasmai prabrūyāt
PB  madhu vāśayed ghṛtaṃ vā yathehuṣo bahaṃ pratyanakti tathā tat
PB  trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
PB  āpyante vā etat stomāś chandāṃsi yat ṣaḍaha āpyate
PB  āpte ṣaḍahe chandāṃsi stomān kṛtvā prayanti
PB  ''pra kāvyam uśanevara bruvāṇa'' iti gāyatryā rūpeṇa prayanti
PB  iyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya prayanti
PB  triṣṭup pratipad bhavati
PB  ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭubojasyeva vīrye parākramya prayanti
PB  stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
PB  dvādaśarcau bhavataḥ
PB  dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram eva tatpūrvasmai ṣaḍahāya pratyudyacchati savīvadhatāyai
 PB  caturviṃśatir bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram eva tatpūrvasmai ṣaḍahāya pratyudyacchati savīvadhatāyai 
 PB  dṛta aindrota iti hovācābhipratārī kākṣasenir ye mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ gacchanti ka te tato bhavanti prarājan pakṣiṇaḥ patanty avāpakṣāḥ 
PB  ye vai vidvāṃsas te pakṣiṇo ye 'vidvāṃsas te 'pakṣās trivṛt pañcadaśāv eva stomau pakṣau kṛtvā svarga lokaṃ prayanti
PB  caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati teja se brahmavarcasāya
PB  ''mūrdhānaṃ divo aratim pṛthivyā'' ity āgreyam ājyaṃ bhavati
PB  mūrdhā vā eṣa divo yas tṛtīyas trirātraḥ
PB  ''vaiśvānaram ṛta ājātam agnim'' iti vaiśvānara iti vā agneḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
 PB  ''pra vo mitrāya gāyata'' iti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ maitrāvaruṇaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī vai mitrāvaruṇayoḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainau tad dhāmnā  
parokṣam upaśikṣati 
PB  ''indrāyāhi citrabhānav'' ity ārbhavam aindram ṛbhavo vā indrasya priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
PB  ''tam īḍiṣva yo arciṣā'' ity aniruktam aindrāgnaṃ devatānām anabhidharṣāyottamārdhe 'nirāha devatānām apraṇāśāya stomaḥ
PB  ''vṛṣā pavasva dhāraya'' iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
PB  vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''punānaḥ soma dhāraya'' iti dhṛtyai
PB  ''pro ayāsīd indur indrasya niṣkṛtam'' iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṣeṇyam iva hy etad ahaḥ
PB  jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
PB  santani bhavati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai
 PB  yathā vai vyokasau vipradravata evam ete ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ saptamaṃ ca vipradravatas tau yathā samānīya saṃyujyād evam evaite etena  
sāmnā saṃyunakti 
 PB  yajño vai devebhyo 'pākrāmat sa suparṇarūpaṃ kṛtvācarat taṃ devā etaiḥ sāmabhirārabhanta yajña iva vā eṣa yac chandomā yajñasyaivaiṣa 
PB  rohitakūlīyaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai
PB  etena vai viśvāmitro rohitābhyāṃ rohitakūla ājim ajayat
PB  viśvāmitro bharatānāṃ manassatyāyāt so 'dantibhir nāma janatayāṃśaṃ
prāsyate māṃ māṃ yūyaṃ astikāṃ jayāthemāni mahyaṃ yūyaṃ pūrayātha yadīmāv idaṃ rohitāv
aśmācitaṃ kūlam udvahāta iti sa ete sāmanī apaśyat tābhyāṃ yuktvā prāsedhat sa udjayat
PB  ājir vā eṣa pratato yad dvādaśāhas tasyaite ujjityai
PB  kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati tejo vā etad rathantarasya yat kaṇvarathantaram
PB  sarasam eva tad rathantaraṃ prayuṅkte yat kaṇvarathantareṇa saptame 'hani stuvate
PB  jāmi dvādaśāhasyāstīti ha smāhogradevo rājanir bārhataṃ ṣaṣṭham ahar bārhataṃ saptamaṃ yat kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati tenājāmi
PB  gauṅgavaṃ bhavati
PB  agnir akāmayatānnādaḥ syām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad gauṅgavam apaśyat
tenānnādo 'bhavad yad annaṃ vitvā gardadyad agaṅgūyat tad gauṅgavasya gauṅgavatvam
annādyasyāvarudhyai gauṅgavaṃ kiyate
PB  yat sāma devatā praśaṃyati tena yajamānāḥ satyāśiṣaḥ satyāśiṣo 'sāmeti vai sattram āsate satyāśiṣa eva bhavanti
PB  āyāsyaṃ bhavati tiraścīnanidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annam āśnāt sa vyabhraṃśata
sa etāny āyāsyāny apaśyat tair ātmānaṃ samaśrīṇād vibhraṣṭam iva vai saptamam ahar
yad etat sāma bhavaty ahar eva tena saṃśrīṇāti
PB  pravadbhargavaṃ bhavati
PB  ''vayaṃ ghatvā sutāvanta'' iti bṛhatyo varṣīyaśchanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
PB  ''nakiṣ ṭaṃ karmaṇā naśad'' iti bṛhatyaḥ satyo 'bhyārambheṇa jagatyaḥ
 PB  apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yaj jyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etā abhyārambheṇa jagatyo bhavanty ahna eva pratyuttambhāya 
PB  abhinidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavita
PB  abhinidhanena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tam astṛṇuta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyam abhinidhanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsaṃs tān rahasyur devamalimluḍ munimaraṇe 'mārayat taṃ devā abruvan kva tarṣayo 
'bhūvānn iti tān praiṣam aicchat tān nāvindat sa imān lokān ekadhāreṇāpunāt tān munimaraṇe
'vindat tān etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vaikhānasaṃ
kāmam evaitenāvarundhe stomaḥ
PB  ''yas te mado vareṇya'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
PB  ''eṣasya dhārayā suta'' iti kakubhaḥ satyo 'bhyārambheṇa triṣṭubhaḥ
 PB  apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yat jyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etā abhyārambheṇa triṣṭubho bhavanty ahna eva pratyuttambhāya 
 PB  ''sakhāya āniṣīdata'' iti vālakhilyā vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca yad etau vākhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva  
vyatiṣaṅgāyāvyavasraṃsāya santatyai 
PB  ''purojitī vo andhasa'' iti virāḍ annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  ''pra vājy akṣār'' ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtiḥ
PB  atho etad  dhy evaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante
 PB  brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā ity etac chandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt 
PB  ''ye somāsaḥ parāvati'' iti parāvatam iva vā etarhi yajño gatas tam evaitenānvicchanti
PB  dakṣaṇidhanaṃ bhavati
 PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmāt sṛṣṭā abalā ivācchadayaṃs tāsv etena sāmnā dakṣāyety ojo vīryam adadhād yad etat sāma bhavaty  
oja eva vīryam ātman dhatte 
PB  śārkaraṃ bhavati
PB  indraṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny astuvan sa śarkaraṃ śiśumārarṣim upetyābravīt
stuhi meti so 'paḥ praskandann abravīd etāvato 'haṃ tvāṃ stuyām iti tasmād apāṃ vegam
avejayat sa hīna ivāmanyata sa etat sāmāpaśyat tenāpo 'nusamāśnuta tad vāva sa tarhy
akāmayata kāmasani sāma śārkaraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  plavo bhavati
 PB  samudraṃ vā ete prasnāntīty āhur ye dvādaśāham upayantīti yo vā aplavaḥ samudraṃ prarunāti na sa tata udeti yata plavo bhavati  
svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai 
PB  ativiśvāni duritā taremeti yad evaiṣāṃ duṣṭutaṃ duśśastaṃ tad etena taranti
PB  ekādaśākṣaraṇidhano bhavaty ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub ojīvīryaṃ triṣṭub ojasy eva vīrye pratitiṣṭhati
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brahmaṇam
PB  kārtayaśaṃ bhavati
PB  hīti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyai
PB  apa pāpmānaṃ hate kārtayaśena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  sāhaiviṣaṃ bhavati
PB  suhavir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  brahmāvādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś
chandomā iti puruṣaś chandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
PB  jarābodhīyaṃ bhavaty annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  annaṃ vai jarābodhīyaṃ mukhaṃ gāyatrī mukha eva tad annaṃ dhatte 'nnam atti
PB  annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  iḍāntāḥ pāvamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍāḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
PB  ''ā te vatso mano yamad'' ity apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva
PB  ''tvaṃ na indrābhara'' iti pūrṇāḥ kakubhaḥ
PB  apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yaj jayāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etāḥ pūrṇāḥ kakubho bhavanty anapabhraṃśāya
PB  vatsaś ca vai medhātithiś ca kāṇvāv āstāṃ taṃ vatsaṃ medhātithir ākrośad
abrāhmaṇo 'si śūdrāputra iti so 'bravīd ṛtenāgniṃ vyayāva yataro nau brahmīyān iti
vātsena vatso vyain maidhātithena medhātithis tasya na loma ca nauṣat tad vāva sa
tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vātsaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  sauśravasaṃ bhavati
PB  upagur vai sauśravasaḥ kutsasyauravasya purohita āsīt sa kutsaḥ paryaśapad
ya indraṃ yajātā iti sa indraḥ suśravasam upetyābravīd yajasva māśanāyāmivā iti tam
ayajata sa indraḥ puroḍāśas taḥ kutsam upetyābravīd ayakṣata mā kva te pariśaptam
abhūd iti kas tvā yaṣṭeti suśravā iti sa kutsa aurava upāgāḥ sauśravasasyodgāyata
audumbaryā śiro 'cchinat sa śuśravā indram abravīt tvattanād vai medam īdṛg upāgād
iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma sauśravasaṃ
kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  vīṅkaṃ bhavati
PB  cyavano vai dādhīco 'śvinoḥ priya āsīt so 'jīryat tam etena sāmnāpsu
vyaiṅkayatāṃ taṃ punaryuvānam akurutāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani sāma
vīṅkaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
PB  ''śiśuṃ jajñānaṃ haryataṃ mṛjanti'' ity aṣṭam asy āhnaḥ pratid bhavati
PB  śiśur iva vā eṣa saptamenāhnā jāyate tam aṣṭamenāhnā mṛjanti
PB  stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
PB  navarcā bhavanti
PB  pañcarco bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  bāṇavān bhavaty anto vai bāṇo 'nta etad aṣṭamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  trayas tṛcā bhavanti prāṇāpānānāṃ santatyai
PB  ''agniṃ vo devam agnibhiḥ sajoṣā'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
PB  agnibhir ity eva pūrvāṇy ahāni abhi samiddhāny aṣṭamam ahar abhisamindhe
PB  ''mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha'' iti bārhataṃ maitrāvaruṇam
 PB  ugragādham iva vā etac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyātiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya 
PB  ''tam indraṃ vājayāmasi'' ity aindram
PB  aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayan navamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena vājayanti
PB  ''indre agnā namo bṛhad'' iti bārhatam aindrāgnam
 PB  ugragādham iva vā etad yac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rape vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya 
PB  ''adhvaryo adribhiḥ sutam'' iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
PB  gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubhorūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''abhi somāsa āyava'' ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ
PB  ''dhartā divaḥ pavate kṛtvyo rasa'' ity adhṛta iva vā eṣas tryaho yad dharteti dhṛtyā eva
PB  jagatyas satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubho loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  vairūpaṃ bhavati
PB  paśavo vai vairūpaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  āśu bhārgavaṃ bhavati
PB  ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā āśunābhyadhinvaṃs tad āśor āśutvam
PB  mārgīyavaṃ bhavati
 PB  devaṃ vā etaṃ mṛgayur iti vadanty etena vai sa ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam aśnute mārgīyaveṇa 
PB  saumitraṃ bhavati
PB  yad eva saumitrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  aiṭataṃ bhavati
PB  iṭan vā etena kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  sākamaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva sākamaśvasya brāhmaṇam
PB  tad u dhurāṃ sāmety āhuḥ prāṇā vai dhuraḥ prāṇānām avarudhyai
PB  vilambasauparṇaṃ bhavati
PB  ātmā vā eṣa sauparṇānāṃ yad aṣṭame 'hani pakṣāv etāv abhito bhavato
ye saptamanavamayor vīva vā antarātmā pakṣau lambate yadantarātmā pakṣau vilambate
tasmād vilambasauparṇam
PB  svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai sauparṇaṃ kriyate
PB  dvitīyaṃ hy etad rūpaṃ yac chandomāḥ
PB  paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn saṃdadhāti
PB  gāyatrapārśvaṃ bhavati
PB  ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā gāyatrapārśvena samatanvaṃs tasmād gāyatrapārśvam
PB  trirātro yad vyaśīryata tam etaiḥ sāmabhir abhiṣajyan gāyatrapārśvenopāyacchan
santaninā samatanvan saṃkṛtinā samaskurvan pratiṣṭhitau pūrvau trirātrāv apratiṣṭhita
eṣa yad etāny eva sāmāni kriyanta etasyaiva pratiṣṭhityai
PB  pauruhanmanaṃ bhavati
PB  puruhanmā vā etena vaikhānaso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  abhyāghātyaṃ bhavaty abhyāghātyasāmāno hi chandomāḥ
PB  dvaigataṃ bhavati
PB  dvigad vā etena bhārgavo dviḥ svargaṃ lokam agacchad āgatya punar agacchat dvayoḥ kāmayor avarudhyai dvaigataṃ kriyate
PB  hārāyaṇaṃ bhavati
PB  indras tejaskāmo haraskāmas tapo 'tapyata
sa etad dhārāyaṇam apaśyat tena tejo haro 'vārundha tejasvī harasvī bhavati hārāyaṇena tuṣtuvānaḥ
PB  achidraṃ bhavati
PB  yad vā etasyāhnaś chidram āsīt tad devā acchidreṇāpy auhaṃs tad acchidrasyācchidratvam
PB  bārhadukthaṃ bhavati
PB  bṛhaduktho vā etena vāmneyo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhām annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  udvad bhārgavaṃ bhavati
PB  pravatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan
PB  nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
PB  ''ka īṃ veda sute sacā'' iti satobṛhatyaḥ
PB  apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yas saptame 'hani satobṛhatyo bhavanti nāṣṭame tasmād aṣṭame kāryā anapabhraṃśāya
 PB  tadāhuḥ śithilam iva vā etac chando yat satobṛhātīty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā bṛhatī yā punaḥpadā yad indra prāg apāg udag iti diśāṃ  
vimarśaḥ pratiṣṭityai 
PB  tāsu naipātithaṃ brahmasāma
PB  sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  ''ubhayaṃ śṛṇavac ca na'' iti
PB  yac ca pṛṣṭhāni yāni caitāny ahāni teṣām ubhayeṣāṃ santatyai
PB  tāsu vaiyaśvam
PB  vyaśvo vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyā etat pṛṣṭhānām antataḥ kriyate stomaḥ
 PB  ''pavasva deva āyuṣag indraṃ gacchatu te mada'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti 
PB  ''prāṇā śiśur mahīnām'' iti prāṇavatyo bhavanti prāṇān eva tad yajamāne dadhāti
PB  ''abhī no vājasātamam'' ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''pavasva soma mahān samudra'' ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir
atho etad dhy evaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ
kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā
ity etac chandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
PB  ''hinvanti sūram usraya'' iti gāyatryaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  svāśirām arko bhavati
PB  annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai prāṇā vai svāśiraḥ prāṇānām arudhyai
PB  surūpaṃ bhavati
PB  paśavo vai surūpaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
PB  bhāsaṃ bhavati bhāti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
 PB  svarbhānur vā āsura ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat sa na vyarocata tasyātrir bhāsena tamo 'pāhan sa vyarocata yad vai tad bhā abhavat  
tad bhāsasya bhāsatvam 
PB  tama iva vā etāny ahāni yac chandomās tebhya etena sāmnā vivāsayati
PB  kākṣīvataṃ bhavati
PB  kākṣīvān vā etenauśijaḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kākṣīvatena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  āsitaṃ bhavati
PB  asito vā etena daivalas trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ dṛṣṭim apaśyat trayāṇāṃ kāmānām avarudhyā āsitaṃ kriyate
PB  aiṣiraṃ bhavati
PB  traitaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  nāthavindu sāma vindate nāthaṃ nāthavindūny etāny ahāni yat chandomā nātham evaitair vindate
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  kautsaṃ bhavati
 PB  etena vai kutso 'ndhaso vipānam apaśyat sa ha sma vai surādṛtinopavasathaṃ dhārayaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvarudhyai kautsaṃ kriyate 
PB  śuddhāśuddhīyaṃ bhavati
 PB  indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat so 'śuddho 'manyata sa etac chuddhāśuddhīyam apaśyat tenāśudhyac  
chudhyati śuddhāśuddhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ 
PB  krauñcaṃ bhavati yad eva krauñcasya brāhmaṇaṃ yat dvitīye 'hani
PB  rayiṣṭhaṃ bhavati
PB  paśavo vai rayiṣṭhaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
PB  audalaṃ bhavati
PB  udalo vā etena vaiśvāmitraḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavaty audalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś
chandomā iti puruṣachandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadāś chandomānām ayātayāmatayau
PB  viśoviśīyaṃ bhavati
PB  agnir akāmayata viśo viśo 'tithis syāṃ viśo viśa ātithyam aśnuvīyeti
sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad viśoviśīyam apaśyat tena viśo viśo 'tithir abhavat viśo
viśa ātithyam aśnuta viśo viśo 'tithir bhavati viśo viśa ātithyam aśnute viśoviśīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  iḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
PB  ''preṣṭhaṃ vo atithim'' ity ātithyasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
PB  ''aindra no gadhi priya'' itīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyai
PB  ''purāṃ bhindur yuvā kavir amitaujā ajāyata
indro viśvasya karmaṇo dhartā vajrī puruṣṭuta'' iti dhṛtyā eva
PB  auśanaṃ bhavati
PB  uśanā vai kāvyo 'kāmayata yāvān itareṣāṃ kāvyānāṃ lokas tāvantaṃ spṛṇuyām
iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad auśanam apaśyat tena tāvantaṃ lokam aspṛṇod yāvān itareṣāṃ
kāvyānām āsīt tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāmauśanaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
PB  sāṃvartaṃ bhavati
PB  devānāṃ vai yajñaṃ rakṣāṃsy ajighāṃsaṃs tāny etena indraḥ saṃvartam
apāvapad yat saṃvartam apāvapat tasmāt sāṃvartaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata taṃ sāṃvartenāpāghnatāpa
pāpmānaṃ hate sāṃvartena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  mārutaṃ bhavati
PB  māsā vai raśmayo maruto raśmayo maruto vai devānāṃ bhūyiṣṭhā bhūyiṣṭhā
asāmeti vai sattram āsate bhūyiṣṭhā eva bhavanty ṛtumanti pūrvāṇy ahāny anṛtavaḥ
chandomā yad etat sāma bhavati tenaitāny ahāny ahāny ṛtumanti bhavanti
PB  catuścatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavaty ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīrye triṣṭup
PB  ''akrān samudraḥ parame vidharmann'' iti navamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
PB  paramaṃ vā etad ahar vidharma vidharma vā etad anyair aharbhir ahar yan navamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ hi variṣṭham
PB  ''matsi vāyum iṣṭaye rādhase na'' iti vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati
PB  stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
PB  daśarco bhavati daśākṣarā virāṭa vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  saprabhṛtayo bhavāntīndriyasya vīryasya rasasyānaticārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
PB  aṣṭarco bhavati
PB  aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti
aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe
PB  ṣaḍṛcā bhavanty ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai
PB  catvāraḥ ṣaḍṛcā bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  savān uttamaḥ ṣaḍṛco bhavaty ubhayasya parokṣapratyakṣasyāvarudhyai
PB  tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
PB  aṣṭācatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
PB  ''aganma mahā namasā yaviṣṭham'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
PB  gacchantīva vā ete ye navamam ahar gacchanti
PB  ''yo dīdāya samiddhasve duroṇa'' iti dīdāyeva hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhis
tuṣṭuvānaḥ ''svāhutam'' iti svāhuto hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhir āhuto ''viśvataḥ
pratyañcam'' iti viśvato hy eṣa pratyaṅ
PB  ''tvaṃ varuṇa uta mitro agna'' iti vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati
PB  ''mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam'' iti rāthantaraṃ maitrāvaruṇam
 PB  ugragādham iva vā etad yac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya 
PB  ''mahāṃ indro ya ojasā'' ity aindram aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayann avamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena mahayanti
PB  ''tā huve yayor idam'' iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
 PB  ugragādham iva vā etad yac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya 
PB  ''pavamānasya jighnato hareś candrā asṛkṣata'' iti harivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
 PB  ''pavamānasya jighnata'' iti vai bṛhato rūpaṃ ''hareś candrā asṛkṣata'' iti jagatyā ubhayoḥ saharūpam upaiti sāmnaś ca chandasaś 
PB  ''parīto ṣiñcatā sutam'' iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai navamam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
PB  ''asāvi somo aruṣo vṛṣā harir'' iti jagatyas satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  bharadvājasyādārasṛd bhavati
PB  divodāsaṃ vai bharadvājapurohitaṃ nanājanāḥ paryayanta sa upāsīdad ṛṣe
gātuṃ me vindeti tasmā etena sāmnā gātum avindad gātuvid vā etatsāmānena dāre nāsṛnmeti
tad adārasṛto 'dārasṛttvaṃ vindate gātuṃ na dāre dhāvaty adārasṛtā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  surūpaṃ bhavati yad eva surūpasya brāhmaṇam
PB  hariśrīnidhanaṃ bhavati
PB  paśavo vai hariśriyaḥ paśūnām avarudhyai śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati yad eva saindhukṣitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  gatanidhanaṃ vābhravaṃ bhavati gatyai
PB  vabhrur vā etena kaumbhyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  iḍānāṃ saṃkṣāro bhavati
PB  paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti
PB  ṛṣabhaḥ pāvamāno bhavati
PB  paśavo vai chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
PB  pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
PB  pṛṣṭhaṃ vā etad ahnāṃ yan navamaṃ pṛṣṭha eva tat pṛṣṭhena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  kaulmalabarhiṣaṃ bhavati
PB  kulmalabarhir vā etena svargaṃ lokam apaśyat prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kaulmalabarhiṣeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  arkapuṣpaṃ bhavati
PB  annaṃ vai devā arka iti vadanti rasam asya puṣpām iti sarasam evānnādyam avarundhe 'rkapuṣpeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  dairghyaśravasaṃ bhavati
PB  dīrghaśravā vai rājanya ṛṣir jyog aparuddho 'śanāyaṃś caran sa etad
dairghaśravasam apaśyat tena sarvābhyo digbhyo 'nnādyam avārundha sarvābhyo adigbhyo
'nnādyam avārundhe dairghaśravasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vaiyaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva vaiyaśvasya brāhmaṇam
PB  abhīśavaṃ yad ābhīśavasya
PB  devasthānaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai saṃskṛti bhavati saṃṃskṛtyai
PB  ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā devasthāne tiṣṭhantaḥ saṃkṛtinā samaskurvaṃs
tat saṃkṛteḥ saṃkṛtitvaṃ devasthānena vai devāḥ svarge loke pratyatiṣṭhan svarge
loke pratitiṣṭām ety etat
 PB  varuṇāya devatā rājyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa etad devasthānam apaśyat tato vai tās tasmai rājyāyātiṣṭhanta tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śreṣṭhyāya 
PB  kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
PB  bhargo bhargeṇa tuṣṭuvāno bhavati yaśo yaśasā
PB  vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati yad eva vāsiṣṭhasya brāhmaṇam
PB  dīrghatamaso 'rko bhavaty annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  sāmarājaṃ bhavati sāmrājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati sāmarājñā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  tad u saṃvad ity āhuḥ saṃvatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan
PB  nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
PB  ''śrāyanta iva sūryam'' iti sūryavatyo bhavanti
PB  ādityadevatyaṃ hy etad ahar anto vai sūro 'nta etan navamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  ''yata indra bhayāvahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi
maghavañ chagdhi tava tan na ūtaye vidviṣo vimṛdho jahi'' iti dviṣaś caiva mṛdhaś ca navamenāhnā vihatya daśamenāhnottiṣṭhanti
PB  śrīr vai śrāyantīyaṃ śrīr navamam ahaḥ śriyam eva tac chriyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  samantaṃ bhavati
PB  samantena paśukāmaḥ stuvīta purodhākāmaḥ samantena stuvīta
PB  āgneyī pṛthivy āgneyo brāhmaṇa aindrī dyaur aindro rājanyo 'ntarikṣeṇa
dyāvāpṛthivī samante antarikṣeṇaivainaṃ samantaṃ karoti vindate paśūn pra purodhām
āpnoti ya evaṃ vidvān samantena stuvate stomaḥ
PB  ''tvaṃ somāsi dhārayur'' iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''tvaṃ hy aṅga daivyā'' iti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''pavasva deva vītaya'' iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
PB  ''parityaṃ haryataṃ harim'' iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai navamam ahasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
PB  ''pavasva soma mahe dakṣāya'' ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir atho
etad dhy evaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ
kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā
ity etac chandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
PB  ''upoṣu jātam apturam'' iti gāyatryas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāt jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brahmaṇam
PB  āśvasūktaṃ bhavati
PB  agniṃ vai pūrvair aharbhir ājuhoty athaitad ādityadaivatyam ahaḥ śukra āhuta ity asau vā ādityaḥ śukras tam evaitenājuhoti
PB  śāmmadaṃ bhavati
PB  śammad vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ
PB  dāvasur vā etad āṅgirasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjat yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
PB  pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ bhavati
PB  parācībhir vā anyābhir iḍābhī reto dadhad athaitat pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ
prajātyai tasmāt parāñco garbhāḥ sambhavanti pratyañcaḥ prajāyante tasmād ute 'vācīnabilebhyo
nāvapadyanta etena hy eva te dhṛtāḥ
PB  hāviṣkṛtaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai kṛtānuvāda eva saḥ
PB  sauparṇaṃ bhavati yad eva sauparṇasya brahmaṇam
PB  vaiśvamanasaṃ bhavati
 PB  viśvamanasaṃ vā ṛṣim adhyāyam udvrajitaṃ rakṣo 'gṛhṇāt tam indro 'cāyad ṛṣiṃ vai rakṣo 'grahīd iti tam abhyavadad ṛṣe kas tvaiṣa 
sthāṇur iti brūhīti rakṣo 'bravīt
sa sthāṇur ity abravīt tasmai vā etena praharety asmā iṣīkāṃ vajraṃ prayacchann abravīt
tenāsya sīmānam abhinat saiṣendreṇateṣīkā pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ vaiśvamanasenāpāhatāpapāpmānaṃ
hate vaiśvamanasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  nihavo bhavaty annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  hīti vā annaṃ pradīyata īty āgrir annam atti
 PB  ṛṣayo vā indraṃ pratyakṣa nāpaśyan sa vasiṣṭho 'kāmayata katham indraṃ pratyakṣaṃ paśyeyam iti sa etan nihavam apaśyat tato vai  
sa indraṃ pratyakṣam apaśyat 
sa enam abravīd brāhmaṇaṃ te vakṣyāmi yathā tvatpurohitā bharatāḥ prajaniṣyante 'tha
mānyebhya ṛṣibhyo mā pravoca iti tasmā etān stomabhāgān abravīt tato vai vasiṣṭhapurohitā
bharatāḥ prājāyanta sendraṃ vā etat sāma yad etat sāma bhavati sendratvāya
PB  yad vāhiṣṭhīyaṃ bhavati
PB  brahmayaśasaṃ vā etāni sāmāny ṛcā śrotrīyāṇi brahmāyaśasī bhavati yad vāhiṣṭhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  āsitaṃ bhavati yad evāsitasya brāhmaṇam
PB  sādhraṃ bhavati siddhyai
PB  ākūpāraṃ bhavati
PB  akūpāro vā etena kaśyapo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchaj jemānaṃ mahimānaṃ gacchaty ākūpāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
PB  vidharma bhavati dharmasya vidhṛtyai
PB  brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś
chandomā iti puruṣacchandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
PB  śrudhyaṃ bhavati
PB  paśavo vai śrudhyaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
 PB  prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān etena sāmnā śrūdhiyā ehiyety anvahvayat ta enam upāvartanta yad etat sāma  
bhavati paśūnām upāvṛtyai 
PB  upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃ veda
PB  gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti
tam abhyudyantīḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva
tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
PB  āgreyīṣu pūrveṣām ahnām ukthāni praṇayanty athaitasyāhna āgneyy aindrayāṃ praṇayanty ubhayor eva rūpayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati
PB  aidhmavāhaṃ bhavati
 PB  āgneyy aindrīṣu stuvanti brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca sayujīkaroti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhāti brāhmaṇe kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ  
cānuge karoti 
PB  traikakubhaṃ bhavati
PB  ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ traikakubham
PB  udvaṃśīyaṃ bhavati yad evodvaṃśīyasya brāhmaṇam
PB  aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
PB  gāyatraṃ vai saptamam ahas traiṣṭubham aṣṭamaṃ jāgataṃ navamam athaitad ānuṣṭubham ahar yad daśamam
PB  tad āhur yad ānuṣṭubhaṃ stomyāṃ pratyakṣam upeyuḥ parāṃ parāvataṃ yajamāno
gacchen na pratitiṣṭhed iti yā vai caturviṃśatir gāyatryas tā aṣṭādaśānuṣṭubho 'nuṣṭubham
eva tat stomyāṃ parokṣam upayanti pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
 PB  prajāpatiṃ vā etenāhnā pariveviṣati tatra vyavavadyaṃ yad vai śreṣṭhe pariviṣyamāṇo vadaty annādyasya so 'vagrahas tasmān na vyavavadyam 
PB  tad u vyavavadyaṃ yathā śreṣṭhāya baliṃ hriyamāṇaṃ panthānaṃ paryanuvedayati gatyai tathā tat
PB  yāvaty anuṣṭup tāvatīṃ vācaṃ sampādya vibrūyus tad v anatiriktaṃ svasyo caiva yajñasyāriṣṭyai
PB  abhi vā ete devān ārohantīty āhur ye daśabhir aharbhiḥ stuvata iti pañcānām
ahnām anurūpaiḥ pratyavayanti yathābhyāruhya pratyavarohet tathā tan navarco bhavati
yā evāmūḥ prayacchan yā avadadhāti tā etā udasyati
 PB  vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajaty ādityaiṣā bhavatīyaṃ vā aditir asyām eva 
PB  caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmarcasāya
PB  ''suṣamiddho na āvaha'' ity āpriya ājyāni bhavanti
PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricānāmanyata sa etāny āpriya ājyāny
apaśyat tair ātmānam āprīṇāt dugdha iva vā eṣa riricāno yo daśabhir aharbhis tuṣṭuvāno
yad etāny āpriya ājyāni bhavanty ātmānam evaitair āprīṇāti
PB  ''yad adya sūra udita'' iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam
PB  anto vai sūro 'nta etad daśamam ahnām anta eva tadantena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  ''ut tvā madantu somā'' ity udvad aindram utthānasya rūpam
PB  ''indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam'' iti yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti stomaḥ
PB  ''uccā te jātam andhasa'' ity udvatyo gāyatryo bhavanty utthānasya rūpam
PB  ''punānas soma dhāraya'' iti panthānam eva tat paryavayanti
PB  ''ā jāgṛvir vipra ṛtaṃ matīnām'' iti yad āpte pravatīḥ kuryur atipadyer anyad āvatyo bhavanty anatipādāya
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kḷptiś cānnādyaṃ ca kḷptiṃ caivaitenānnādyaṃ cābhyuttiṣṭhanti
PB  ājigaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai
PB  ājir vā eṣa pratato yat dvādaśāhas tasyaitad ujjityai
PB  ābhīkaṃ bhavaty abhikrāntyai
PB  āṅgirasas tapas tepānāḥ śucam aśocaṃs ta etat sāmāpaśyaṃs tān abhīke
'bhyavarṣat tena śucam aśamayanta yad abhīke 'bhyavarṣat tasmād ābhīkaṃ yām eva pūrvair
aharbhiḥ śucaṃ śocanti tām etenānna śamayitvottiṣṭhanti
PB  utsedho bhavati
PB  utsedhena vai devāḥ paśūn udasedhan niṣedhena paryagṛhṇan
PB  antarotsedhaniṣedhau yajñāyajñīyam
PB  paśavo 'nnādyaṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ paśūn eva tad annādyam utsedhaniṣedhābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāti
PB  mādhyandine vai pavamāne devā yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ saṃsthāpya svargaṃ
lokam ārohaṃs tad ya evaṃ veda mādhyandina evaitat pavamāne yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ
saṃsthāpya svargaṃ lokam ārohati
PB  atho parokṣam anuṣṭubhaṃ sampadyate 'har eṣā vai pratyakṣam anuṣṭup
yad yajñāyajñīyaṃ tad yat tṛtīyasavane kuryuḥ pratyakṣam anuṣṭubham ṛccheyus tasmān
mādhyandine kurvanti tena parokṣam anuṣṭubham upayanti
PB  gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
 PB  etad vai yajñasya śvastanaṃ yad gaurīvitam etad āyatano yajamāno yan madhyandino yad gaurīvitaṃ madhyandine bhavati śvastanam  
eva tad yajamāna ātman dhatte stomaḥ 
PB  ''kayā naś citra ābhuvad'' iti kavatyas tena prājāpatyāḥ ko hi prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai
PB  ''mā cid anyad viśaṃsata'' ity utthānam eva tad āśiṣo hy etarhi
PB  ''ud u tye madhumattamā'' ity udvatya udayanīye 'hany etad āśiṣo hy evaitarhi
 PB  ''tarobhir vo vidadvasum'' iti stomo vai taro yajño vidadvasuḥ stomena vai yajño yujyate yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum ity āha yajñam  
eva tad yunakti 
PB  vāmadevyasyarkṣu rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
PB  gāyatrī vai rathantarasya yoniḥ svāyām eva tad yonau rathantaraṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
 PB  tejo vai gāyatrī chandasā tejo rathantaraṃ sāmnā tejaś caturviṃśastomānāṃ teja eva tat samyak saṃdadhāty api ha putrasya putras  
tejasvī bhavati 
PB  aṣṭākṣareṇa prathamāyā ṛcaḥ prastauty aṣṭāśaphāṃs tatpaśūn avarundhe
PB  dyvakṣareṇottarayor ṛcoḥ prastauti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  gāyatraṃ vai rathantaraṃ gāyatracchando yad gāyatrīṣu rathantaram bhavati
tena svāyāṃ janatāyām ṛdhnotīme vai lokā gāyatrī yad gāyatrīṣu rathantaraṃ bhavatīmān
eva tal lokān samāpyottiṣṭhanti
PB  maidhātithaṃ bhavati
PB  etena vai medhātithiḥ kāṇvo vibhindukād vyūdhnīr gā udasṛjata paśūnām avarudhyai maidhātithaṃ kriyate
PB  abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavaty ekākṣaranidhanaḥ pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  ekākṣarā vai vāg vācy eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti
PB  kāleyam acchāvākasāma bhavati
 PB  samānaloke vai kāleyaṃ ca rathantaraṃ ceyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ paśavaḥ kāleyam asyāṃ caiva paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti stomaḥ 
PB  ''svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayā'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
PB  gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
PB  saṃhitaṃ bhavati dyvakṣaraṇidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai pratiṣṭhāyaivottiṣṭhanti
PB  saphaṃ bhavati
PB  saphena vai devā imān lokān samāpnuvant samāpnuvaṃs tat saphasya saphatvam imān evaitena lokān samāpyottiṣṭhanti
PB  rohitakūlīyaṃ bhavati yad eva rohitakūlīyasya brāhmaṇam
PB  śyāvāśvāndhīgave bhavataḥ samīcyau virājau dadhāty annādyāya
PB  pipīlikāmadhyāsu stuvanti
PB  indro vṛtraṃ hatvā nāstṛṣīti manyamānaḥ parāṃ parāvatam agacchat sa
etām anuṣṭubhaṃ vyauhat tāṃ madhye vyavāsarpad indragṛhe vā eṣo 'bhaye yajate abhaya
uttiṣṭhati ya evaṃ vidvān etāsu stuvate
PB  yajñāyajñīyanidhanaṃ sauhaviṣaṃ bhavati yajñāyajñīyād eva tat tṛtīyasavene na yanti
PB  vājajid bhavati
PB  sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvaṃ vā ete vājaṃ jayanti ye daśamam ahar āgacchanty annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  daśākṣaraṃ nidhanam upayanti daśarātrasya dhṛtyai daśākṣarā virāḍ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
PB  sūryavatīṣu stuvanty anto vai sūro 'nta etad daśamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
PB  upavatyo bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai parivatyo bhavanti sarvasya paryāptyai
PB  caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
PB  virāṭsu vāmadevyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavati śāntyai kḷptyai
 PB  sad vai vāmadevyaṃ sāmnāṃ sad virāṭ chandasāṃ sat trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ satām antān saṃdhāyottiṣṭhanty api ha putrasya sattvam 
PB  brahmavādino vadanti yatas sattrād udasthātā sthitād iti yad yata
iti brūyur apratiṣṭhānā aprajaso bhaviṣyantīty enān brūyād yat sthitād iti brūyuḥ
sthāyukaiṣāṃ śrīr bhaviṣyati na vasīyāṃso bhaviṣyantīty enān brūyāt pūrṇād eva pūrṇam
abhyudasthāmeti brūyuḥ
PB  ete vai pūrṇāt pūrṇam abhyuttiṣṭhanti ye vāmadevyena stutvottiṣṭhanti
PB  antarikṣaṃ vai vāmadevyam antarikṣeṇedaṃ sarvaṃ pūrṇam
PB  eṣa vai samṛddhaḥ stomo yat trayastriṃśas trayastriṃśadakṣarāsu samṛddhāv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  sarveṣāṃ vā etāś chandasāṃ rūpaṃ yāt tripadās tena gāyatryo yad ekādaśākṣarāṇi
padāni tena triṣṭubho yat dvādaśākṣaraṃ padaṃ tena jagatyo yat trayastriṃśadakṣarās
tena virājas tenaiva cānuṣṭubho na hy ekasmād akṣarād virādhayanti
PB  trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
PB  prajāpatir vā idam eka āsīn nāhar āsīn na rātrir āsīt so 'sminn andhe
tamasi prāsarpat sa aicchat sa etam abhyapadyata tato vai tasmai vyaucchad vyuṣṭir
vā eṣa āhriyate yad vai taj jyotir abhavat tat jyotiṣo jyotiṣṭvam
PB  eṣa vāva prathamo yajñānāṃ ya etenāniṣṭvāthānyena yajate gartapatyam eva taj jīyate pra vā mīyate
PB  yathā vā idam agner jātād agnayo vihriyanta evam etasmād adhy anye yajñā vihriyante
PB  yo hi trivṛd anyaṃ yajñakratum āpadyate sa taṃ dīpayati yaḥ pañcadaśaḥ sa taṃ yaḥ saptadaśaḥ sa taṃ ya ekaviṃśaḥ sa tam
PB  etat tad yad āhur eko yajña ity etad dhi sarve jyotiṣṭomā bhavanti
PB  asthūrir vā eṣa santato yajño dvau dvau hi stomau savanaṃ vahatas trivṛt
pañcadaśau prātaḥsavanaṃ pañcadaśasaptadaśau mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaikaviṃśau tṛtīyasavanam
PB  yā mitadakṣiṇaiva syād eṣa eva kārya iyaṃ vai jyotir iyam amitasya yantrikaiṣā vā etaṃ yantum arhati
PB  tasya navatiśataṃ stotrīyās tāsāṃ yā aśītiśataṃ tāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśinyo virājaḥ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva virājā pratitiṣṭhati
PB  atha yā daśaiṣā vā ātmanyā virāḍ etasyāṃ vā idaṃ puruṣaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
PB  gauś cāśvaś cāśvataraś ca gardabhaś cājāś cāvayaś ca vrīhayaś ca yavāś ca tilāś ca māṣāś caitasyām eva virāji pratitiṣṭhati
PB  tasya dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ
PB  vīrahā vā eṣa devānāṃ yaḥ somam abhiṣuṇoti yāḥ śataṃ vairaṃ tad devān
avadayate 'tha yā daśa daśa prāṇāḥ prāṇāṃs tābhiḥ spṛṇoti yaikādaśyātmānaṃ tayā yā
dvādaśī saiva dakṣiṇā
PB  śleṣma vā etad yajñasya yad dakṣiṇā na vā aśleṣmā ratho vahaty atha
śleṣmavatā yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam abhyaśnuta evam etena dakṣiṇāvatā yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam abhyaśnute
PB  śubho vā etā yajñasya yad dakṣiṇā yad dakṣiṇāvatā yajate śubham evāsmin dadhāti
PB  athaiṣa gauḥ
PB  gavā vai devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo 'nudantaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ nudate ya evaṃ veda
PB  yad vai tad devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo govayaṃs tad gor gotvam
PB  govayati pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ ya evaṃ veda
PB  tasya pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ vajro vai pañcadaśo vajram eva tat purastān nidadhāti tena vijayate
PB  paśustomo vā eṣa evam iva vai paśuḥ samāhitaḥ śiraḥ sthavīyo 'ṇīyas yo grīvā pārśvābhyāṃ varīyāṃ sakthibhyāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
 PB  yat pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati trivṛt tyājyāni saptadaśa mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ rūpeṇaivainaṃ tat 
PB  ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyate tasmāt paśoḥ paścād atiriktam
PB  athaiṣa gauḥ
PB  gavā vai devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo 'nudantaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ nudate ya evaṃ veda

 PB  yat pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati trivṛnty ājyāni saptadaśa mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ rūpeṇaivainaṃ tat

PB  athaiṣa āyuḥ
PB  āyuṣā vai devā asurān āyuvatāyute bhrātṛvyaṃ ya evaṃ veda
PB  svargakāmo yajeta
PB  ūrdhvāḥ stomā yanty anapabhraṃśāya
PB  etenaivāmayāvinaṃ yājayed atirātraḥ kāryaḥ
PB  sa gāyatrīṃ saṃpadyate prāṇo gāyatry āyur eṣa āyuś caivāsmin prāṇaṃ cobhe samīcī dadhāti
PB  svargyā vā ete stomā yat jyotir bhavati jyotir evāsmai sa purastād dharaty
athaiṣa gaur ekayā virājam atirikta ārambhaṇam eva tad athaiṣa āyur ekasyā virāja
ūna āsāda eva so 'tho ūnātiriktau stomau mithunau prajātyai
PB  ete vai trikadrukāḥ stomā etair vā indraḥ sarvāṃ tṛptim atṛpyat
PB  tṛpyati prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda
 PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmai śraiṣṭhyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa āsāṃ diśāṃ prajānāṃ ca rasaṃ pravṛhya srajaṃ kṛtvā pratyamuñcata tato  
'smai prajāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta 
PB  tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃ veda
 PB  so 'kāmayatendro me prajāyāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ syād iti tām asmai srajaṃ pratyamuñcat tato vā indrāya prajāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta tac chilpaṃ  
paśyantyo yat pitary apaśyan 
PB  tasmād yaḥ putrāṇāṃ dāyaṃ dhanatamam ivopaiti taṃ manyante 'yam evedaṃ bhaviṣyatīti
PB  tato vā idam indro viśvam ajayad yad viśvam ajayat tasmād viśvajit
PB  so 'kāmayata yan me 'nabhijitaṃ tad abhijayeyam iti sa etam abhijitam apaśyat tenānabhijitam abhyajayat
PB  yad abhijid bhavaty anābhijitasyābhijityai
PB  tau vā etāv indrastomau vīryavantau śilpaṃ vā etau nāma stomāv āstām
PB  paśyate gṛhe śilpaṃ ya evaṃ veda
PB  na vai yamau nāma stomau sto yo yamābhyāṃ yajetaitābhyāṃ yajeta samṛdhyai
PB  punarabhyāvartaṃ stomā bhavanti punarabhyāvartaṃ hy etābhyām indro 'jitam ajayat
 PB  trīṃs trivṛdabhijitaḥ praṇayati trīn pañcadaśaḥ trīn saptadaśaḥ trīn ekaviṃśas te dvādaśa saṃpadyante dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ  
prajāpatiḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti 
 PB  caturas trivṛdviśvajitaḥ praṇayati caturaḥ pañcadaśaś caturaḥ saptadaśas te dvādaśa saṃpadyante dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ  
prajāpatiḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti 
PB  ''upa tvā jāmayo gira'' ity upavatī pratipad bhavati stomasya rūpam
 PB  prāṇair vā eṣa vyṛdhyata ity āhur yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti sarvān stomān sarvāṇi pṛṣṭhāny upaitīti yad vāyavyā bhavati prāṇānāṃ samṛdhyai 
PB  sarasvataś ca sarasvatyāś cottare bhavataḥ
PB  mithunaṃ vā etad yat sarasvāṃś ca sarasvatī ca mithunam evāsya yajñamukhe dadhāti prajananāya
PB  sāvitrī caturthī bhavati
PB  duṣkaraṃ vā eṣa karoti yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti yat sāvitrī bhavati savitṛprasṛtaṃ me karmāsad iti savitṛprasūtam evāsya karma bhavati
PB  brāhmaṇaspatyā pañcamī bhavati
PB  brahma vai brahmaṇaspatir brahmaivāsya yajñamukhe dadhāti
PB  āgnipāvamānī ṣaṣṭhī bhavati
PB  agnir evainaṃ niṣṭapati pavamānaḥ punāti pūtam evainaṃ yajñiyaṃ pṛṣṭhāny upanayati
PB  yanti vā ete patha ity āhur ye saṃbhāryāḥ kurvate
PB  pāvamāna uttamas tṛco bhavati tena patho nayanti
PB  sa tu vai pṛṣṭhaiḥ stuvītety āhur ya etāni bahiṣpavamāne yuñjyād iti
PB  upavatī pratipad bhavaty upa vai rathantaraṃ rathantaram evāsmai tayā yunakti
PB  sarasvatī dvitīyā bhavati svargo lokaḥ sarasvān svargo loko bṛhad bṛhad evāsmai tayā yunakti
PB  sarasvatyās tṛtīyā bhavati vāg vai sarasvatī vāg vairūpaṃ vairūpam evāsmai tayā yunakti
PB  sāvitrī caturthī bhavati prajāpatir vai savitā prajāpatir vairājaṃ vairājam evāsmai tayā yunakti
PB  brāhmaṇaspatyā pañcamī bhavati brahma vai brahmaṇaspatir brahma śakvaryaḥ śakvarīr evāsmai tayā yunakti
PB  āgnipāvamānī ṣaṣṭhī bhavati gāyatrī vai revatī gāyatracchandā agnī revatīr evāsmai tayā yunakti
PB  na catvāri ṣaḍbhyo vibhavanti yad aniruktāni tena vibhavanti
PB  sarvāṇi svārāṇy ājyāni taj jāmi nānādevatyaiḥ stuvanty ajāmitāyai
PB  ''suṣamiddho na āvaha'' ity āpriya ājyāni bhavanti
PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etāny āpriya ājyāny apaśyat tair ātmānam thus BI
KSS ātmanam āprīṇād dugdha iva vā eṣa riricāno yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti yad āpriya ājyāni bhavanty ātmānam evaitair āprīṇāti
PB  etarhi tu vai pṛṣṭhāni yathāyatanaṃ kalpanta ity āhur yad rathantaraṃ prathamaṃ bṛhad uttamaṃ madhya itarāṇīti
 PB  jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yat sarvāṇi nidhanavanti saha kriyanta iti yad antarā somā yanty antarokthāni śasyante 'ntarā  
vaṣaṭkurvanti tenājāmi 
PB  vyatyāsam iḍāś ca nidhanāni cāhus tenājāmi
 PB  cyavante vā etad revatyaḥ svād āyatanād ity āhur yat trayastriṃśāt stomād yantīti yad gāyatryo bhavanti tenāyatanān na cyavante  
yā hi kā ca gāyatrī sā revatī 
PB  paraśubhir vā eṣa vyṛdhyata ity āhur yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti tac chavīṃ paridhatte paśubhir eva samṛdhyate
PB  rohiṇī chavī bhavaty etad vai paśunāṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ rūpaṃ yad rohitaṃ sākṣād evainān avarundhe
PB  araṇye tisro vasaty āraṇyaṃ tābhir annādyam avarundhe
PB  udumbare vasaty ūrg udumbara ūrjam evāvarundhe
PB  khanitreṇa jīvaty avṛttim apajayati
PB  ubhayataḥkṣṇud abhrir bhavaty ubhayata evāsmā annādyaṃ rajaty asmāc ca lokād amuṣmāc ca
PB  niṣādeṣu tisro vasaty asyāṃ vā ete parīttā yad evāsyām annādyaṃ tad avarundhe
PB  jane tisro vasati janyaṃ tābhir annādyam avarundhe
PB  samānajane tisraḥ samānajanyaṃ tābhiḥ
PB  dvādaśaitā rātrayo bhavanti dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram anv annādyaṃ prajāyate tad evāptvāvarundhe
PB  saṃvatsaraṃ na yāced āmādyam iva vā etad yaḥ sadyodattaṃ pratyatti sadyo vai devānaṃ saṃvatsaraḥ

pary enam āviśan

yūpe paśūn niyuñjanti pañcāśacchataṃ dakṣiṇā
PB  ahataṃ vasāno 'vabhṛthād udeti caturo māso na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti

 PB  upavatī pratipad vāyavyaḥ paśur āśviny anūbandhyā minvanti yūpaṃ ny uttaravediṃ vapanti yūpe paśuṃ niyuñjanti dvādaśaṃ śataṃ

ya evaṃ veda

PB  sa aikṣata yan niruktam āhariṣyāmy asurā me yajñaṃ haniṣyantīti so 'niruktam āharat

 PB  indro yatīn sālāvṛkeyebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat sa prajāpatim upādhāvat tasmā etam upahavyaṃ prāyacchat taṃ viśve  
devā upāhvayanta tasmād upahavyaḥ 
PB  abhiśasyamānaṃ yājayet

PB  grāmakāmo yajeta

PB  aśvaḥ śyavo dakṣiṇā

PB  tasya dvādaśa dīkṣopasadaḥ
PB  svargakāmo yajeta

PB  saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
PB  tasya dīkṣaṇīyāyām iṣṭau dvādaśamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ dadāti caturviṃśatimānaṃ
prāyaṇīyāyāṃ dve caturviṃśatimāne ātithyāyāṃ catvāri caturviṃśatimānāni prātaḥ prathamāyām
upasady aṣṭau caturviṃśatimānāny aparāhṇe prathamāyām upasadi ṣoḍaśacaturviṃśatimānāni
prātar madhyamāyām upasadi dvātriṃśataṃ caturviṃśatimānāny aparāhṇe madhyamāyām upasadi
catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ caturviṃśatimānāni prātar uttamāyām upasady aṣṭāviṃśatiśataṃ caturviṃśatimānāny
aparāhṇa uttamāyām upasadi dve aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamāne agnīṣomīyasya paśor vapāyāṃ catvāry
aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni prātaḥ paśor vapāyām aṣṭāv aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni prātaḥsavane
sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu ṣoḍaśāṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni mādhyandine savane 'naḍucchataṃ ca
rukmo hotuḥ srag udgātur dvātriṃśatam aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni tṛtīyasavane sanneṣu

payasā śrīṇāti

PB  somātipavitaṃ yājayet

PB  tad abhakṣayanta ṛtvijaś camasān avajighranti tīvrayanty evainaṃ tat tān acchāvākasya stotre bhakṣayanti tīvrayanty evainam
 PB  tad yat savanāni vyavabhakṣayeyur apakrāmukā yajamānāc chrīḥ syāt sakṛtsakṛt savanānām antato bhakṣayanti savanānām asaṃbhedāya 
PB  rathantaraṃ sāma bhavati
PB  iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyāṃ vā eṣa na pratitiṣṭhati yo na pratitiṣṭhaty asyām evainaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavaty etad evāsmiñ chrīṇāti
PB  vāg anuṣṭup vāco raso yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāsya rasaṃ dadhāti
PB  viśoviśīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavaty etad evāsmin sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  udvaṃśīyam ukthānām antato bhavati sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  ukthyo bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati

PB  tasya nānāvīryāṇi savanāni

citravat tṛtīyasavanaṃ svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
PB  viyonir vājapeya ity āhuḥ prājāpatyaḥ san niruktasāmeti yad aniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ tena sayoniḥ

PB  iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām evādhy abhiṣicyate

PB  yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi bhavati vāg anuṣṭup vāco raso yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāsya rasaṃ dadhāti
PB  vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavatīndriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai
PB  udvaṃśīyam ukthānām antato bhavati sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  gaurīvitaṃ ṣoḍaśisāma bhavati
PB  atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atiriktaḥ ṣoḍaśy atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti
PB  tad āhur jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyate yad udvaṃśīyād gaurīvitena stuvate svārāt svāreṇeti
PB  na jāmy asti savanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
PB  ukthaṃ śasyate vaṣaṭkāro 'ntarā tenājāmi
PB  apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yat ṣoḍaśī tenājāmi

PB  viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhad uttamaṃ bhavati
PB  eṣā vai prajāpateḥ paśuṣṭhā tanūr yac chipiviṣṭaḥ prāṇo vai bṛhat prāṇa eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
PB  bṛhatā stuvanti bṛhad amuṃ lokam āptum arhati tam evāpnoti

PB  śukravatyo jyotiṣmatyaḥ prātaḥsavane bhavanti tejo brahmavarcasaṃ tābhir avarundhe

PB  eṣa me 'muṣmin loke prakāśo 'sad iti
PB  jyotir vai hiraṇyaṃ jyotir evāsmin dadhāti

PB  nākaṃ rohati svargam eva tal lokaṃ rohati

PB  viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhaduttamaṃ bhavati svargam eva tal lokaṃ rūḍhvā bradhnasya viṣṭapam abhyatikrāmati

PB  prāṇo vai trivṛd ātmā pañcadaśaḥ
PB  mukhaṃ gāyatry annaṃ vai saptadaśo mukhata eva tad annaṃ dhatte
PB  annam atty annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  mādhyandinena vai pavamānena devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan yad eṣa caturviṃśo
mādhyandinaḥ pavamāno bhavati svargasya lokasyākrāntyai caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī
tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ
prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate
PB  ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate
PB  pakṣi vā etac chandaḥ pakṣī jyotiṣmān puṇyān lokān saṃcarati ya evaṃ veda
PB  madhyato vā agnir variṣṭhas tasmād ete stomā madhyato variṣṭhāḥ kriyante
PB  ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyata ekākinam evainam annādyasyādhyakṣaṃ karoti
PB  jyotir vā eṣo 'gniṣṭomo jyotiṣmantaṃ puṇyaṃ lokaṃ jayati ya evaṃ vidvān etena yajate
PB  athaiṣa ṛṣabhaḥ
PB  ṛṣabho vā eṣa stomānām ṛṣabhatāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
PB  rājanyaṃ yājayed ṛṣabho vai paśūnām adhipatī rājanyo manuṣyāṇām
PB  yo vā asti so 'dhipatiḥ
PB  adhipatiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  tasya sadoviśīyaṃ mādhyandine pavamāne bhavati viśam evāsmai savanābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
PB  samantaṃ bhavati samantām evāsmai viśaṃ karoty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
 PB  ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavata iyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ dyaur bṛhadevāsmāl lokād gāyatry evāmuṣmād ubhayor anayor lokayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati 
PB  anuṣṭubhi bṛhad bhavaty anto vā anuṣṭup chandasām anto bṛhat sāmnām
anto rājanyo manuṣyāṇām anta eva tad antaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmād yo rājanyānāṃ hīyate
na sa punaragraṃ paryeti
PB  yo vai vājapeyaḥ sa rājasūyo yo rājasūyaḥ sa varūṇasavo 'thaiṣa gosavaḥ svārājyo vā eṣa yajñaḥ
PB  svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
PB  prajāpatir hi svārājyaṃ parameṣṭhī svārājyam
PB  parameṣṭhitāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
PB  ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavatas tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
PB  ayutaṃ dakṣiṇās tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
PB  pratiduhābhiṣicyate tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
PB  bṛhataḥ stotra pratyabhiṣicyate tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
PB  anuddhate dakṣiṇata āhavanīyasyābhiṣicyate 'syām evānantarhite 'dhy abhiṣicyate
PB  sarvaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśastena gosavaḥ
PB  athaiṣa marutstoma etena vai maruto 'parimitāṃ puṣṭim apuṣyann aparimitāṃ puṣṭiṃ puṣyati ya evaṃ veda
PB  yad gaṇaśaḥ stomās tena marutstomo gaṇaśo hi marutaḥ
PB  etenaiva trīn yājayet
PB  yat trīṇi trivṛnti stotrāṇi bhavanti nānā brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  yat trīṇi pañcadaśāni nānā vīrye
PB  yat trīṇi saptadaśāni nānā paśuṣu
PB  yat trīṇy ekaviṃśāni nānā pratitiṣṭhanti
PB  pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
PB  athaiṣa indrāgnyoḥ kulāyaḥ prajākāmo vā paśukāmo vā yajeta prajā vai kulāyaṃ paśavaḥ kulāyaṃ gṛhāḥ kulāyaṃ kulāyam eva bhavati
PB  etenaiva dvau yājayet
PB  yat ṣaṭ trivṛnti stotrāṇi bhavanti nānā brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhato
yat dve pañcadaśe nānā vīrye yat dve saptadaśe nānā paśuṣu yat dve ekaviṃśe nānā
pratitiṣṭhataḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
PB  athaiṣa pañcadaśa indrastoma ukthyaḥ
PB  etena vā indro 'ty anyā devatā abhavad aty anyāḥ prajā bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  rājanyaṃ yājayet
PB  sarvaḥ pañcadaśo bhavaty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśa ojasaivainaṃ vīryeṇa samardhayati
PB  aindrīṣu bhavantīndriyeṇaivainaṃ vīryeṇa samardhayati
PB  ukthyo bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni viḍ ukthāni viśam evāsmai paśūn anuniyunakty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
PB  pañcadaśa stotrāṇi pañcadaśāni bhavanty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśo 'bhipūrvam evāsminn ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti
PB  athaiṣa indrāgnyoḥ stoma etena vā indrāgnī aty anyā devatā abhavatām aty anyāḥ prajā bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  trivṛt pañcadaśo bhavati
PB  brahma vai trivṛt kṣatraṃ pañcadaśo brahmaṇa iva cāsya kṣatrasyeva ca prakāśo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  rājā ca purohitaś ca yajeyātām
PB  gāyatrīṃ ca jagatīṃ ca saṃpadyate
PB  tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatryā brāhmaṇo 'varundhe viśaṃ rājā jagatyā praviśati
PB  purodhākāmo yajeta
PB  bṛhaspatir akāmayata devānāṃ purodhāṃ gaccheyam iti sa etenāyajata sa devānāṃ purodhām agacchad gacchati purodhāṃ ya evaṃ veda
PB  athaiṣa vighanaḥ
 PB  indro 'kāmayata pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vihanyām iti sa etaṃ vighanam apaśyat tena pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vyahan vi pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ  
hate ya evaṃ veda 
PB  yat trivṛd bhavati prāṇāṃs tenāvarundhe yat dvādaśaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ tena
yat pañcadaśo vīryaṃ tena yat saptadaśo 'nnādyaṃ tena yad ekaviṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhā tena
yan navadaśaḥ prajananaṃ tena yac caturviṃśo brahmavarcasaṃ tena yat triṇavo vajraṃ
bhrātṛvyāya praharati
PB  paśukāmo yajeta bṛhatīṃ saṃpadyate paśavo vai bṛhatī paśūn evāvarundhe
PB  ṣaḍ etā bṛhatyo bhavanti ṣaḍ ṛtavaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nu prajāyante tān evāptvāvarundhe
 PB  indram adevyo māyā ayacanta sa prajāpatim upādhāvavat tasmā etaṃ vighanaṃ prāyacchat tena sarvā mṛdho vyahata yad vyahata tad 
PB  sarvā mṛdho vihate ya evaṃ vidvān vighanena yajate yam evaṃ vidvān vighanena yājayati
PB  paśukāmo yajeta paśavo vai bṛhatī paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni pañcadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ
saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśa ārbhava ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ sokthyaḥ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
PB  jyotiṣṭomenātirātreṇarddhikāmo yajetābhikramo vā eṣa stomānām abhikrāntyā abhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti
 PB  eṣo 'gniṣṭoma eṣa ukthya eṣo 'tirātro 'gniṣṭomena vai devā imaṃ lokam abhyajayann ukthyair antarikṣaṃ rātryāmuṃ lokam ajayann ahorātrābhyām 
PB  parācyo vā anyā vyucchanti pratīcyo 'nyā eṣā vāva pratīcī vyucchati yāśvinena vyucchati pratīcīr evāsmā uṣaso vivāsayati
PB  dve saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyete eṣā vai stanavatī virāṭ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etāṃ dugdhe
PB  trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇo vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti
PB  trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna
ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni
triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
PB  sarvastomenātirātreṇa bubhūṣan yajeta sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
PB  yat trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati tat trivṛtaṃ stomam āpnoti gāyatrīṃ
chando yat pañcadaśāny ājyāni tat pañcadaśaṃ stomam āpnoti triṣṭubhaṃ chando yat
saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānas tat saptadaśaṃ stomam āpnoti jagatīṃ chando yad
ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭāni tad ekaviṃśaṃ stomam āpnoty anuṣṭubhaṃ chando yat triṇava ārbhavas
tat triṇavaṃ stomam āpnoti paṅktiṃ chando yat trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomas tat trayastriṃśaṃ
stomam āpnoti virājaṃ chando yad uṣṇikkakubhau kriyete tad uṣṇikkakubhāv āpnoti yad
āśvinaṃ śasyate tat sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
PB  prāñcaṃ vai trayastriṃśo yajñaṃ prabhujati tam adhvaryur ekādaśinyā purastāt
pratyudyacchaty ekādaśa raśanā ekādaśa paśava ekādaśa yūpā bhavanti tat trayastriṃśe
trayastriṃśaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
PB  tayā samudyatayā rātryā yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ tam abhyaśnute yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ tam abhyaśnute ya evaṃ veda
PB  trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna
ekaviṃśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ chandomā itarāṇi triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamam athaikaviṃśam atha saptadaśam ekaviṃśaḥ
ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhis trivṛt prathamam atiriktastotram atha pañcadaśam
atha saptadaśam athaikaviṃśam
PB  prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān agniṣṭomena nāpnot
tān ukthair nāpnot tān ṣoḍaśinā nāpnot tān rātryā nāpnot tān sandhinā nāpnot tān
āśvinena nāpnot tān agnim abravīd imān ma īpseti tān agnis trivṛtā stomena jarābodhīyena
sāmnā nāpnot tān indram abravīd imān ma īpseti tān indraḥ pañcadaśena stomena sattrāsāhīyena
sāmnā nāpnot tān viśvān devān abravīd imān ma ipsateti tān viśve devāḥ saptadaśena
stomena mārgīṃyaveṇa sāmnā nāpnuvaṃs tān viṣṇum abravīd imān ma īpseti tān viṣṇur
ekaviṃśena stomenāpnod vāravantīyenāvārayatedaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti vyakramata
PB  yasmāt pra preva paśavo bhraṃśeran sa etena yajeta
PB  etena vai devā jaitvāni jitvā yaṃ yaṃ kāmam akāmayanta taṃ tam āpnuvan yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenāpnoti
PB  tad aptoryāmno 'ptoryāmatvam
 PB  trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ navasaptadaśāni stotrāṇy ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ sokthaḥ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ 
 PB  navasaptadaśenātirātreṇa prajākāmo yajeta nava vai prāṇāḥ prajāpatiḥ saptadaśaḥ prāṇebhya eva tad adhi prajāpateḥ prajāḥ prajāyante 
PB  kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhati puruṣo vai kakup garbho vā eṣa madhyato dhīyate
PB  tasyāṃ sākamaśvam
PB  prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā na prājāyanta sa etat sāmāpaśyat tā aśvo bhūtvābhyajighrat tāḥ prājāyanta prajananaṃ vā etat sāma
PB  prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda
PB  dvipadāṃ kakubho loke karoti garbham eva taddhitaṃ madhyataḥ prajanayati
PB  atirātro bhavaty ahorātre vā anu prajāḥ prajāyante 'horātre evānu prajayā paśubhiḥ prajāyate
PB  trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni pañcadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ
saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśa ārbhava ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ saptadaśāny ukthāni pañcadaśī
rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
PB  viṣuvatātirātreṇa jyeṣṭhaṃ jyaiṣṭhineyaṃ yājayed viṣuvān vā eṣa stomānāṃ
viṣuvān eva bhavati yad eka ekaviṃśo bhavaty ekaviṃśo vā ito 'sāv āditya dvādaśa
māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā
PB  asāv āditya ekaviṃśa ādityasyaivainaṃ mātrāṃ gamayati
PB  eṣa vā udeti na vā enam anyat jyotiṣāṃ jyotiḥ pratyudeti
PB  nainam anyaḥ sveṣu pratyudeti ya evaṃ veda
PB  pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ trivṛnty ājyāni saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam
ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir goṣṭomenātirātreṇa
bhrātṛvyavān yajeta gavā vai devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo 'nudanta rātryānapajayyam
ajayann ebhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudya rātryānapajayyaṃ jayati
PB  trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam
ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir āyuṣṭomenātirātreṇa
svargakāmo yajetordhvāḥ stomā yanty anapabhraṃśāya yad atirātro bhavaty ahorātrābhyām
eva svargaṃ lokam eti
PB  trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya
pañcadaśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ saptadaśam acchāvākasyaikaviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ
saptadaśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭham ekaviṃśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya triṇavaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ekaviṃśam
acchāvakasya triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ
prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir abhijitātirātreṇa
bhrātṛvyavān yajetābhijitā vai devā asurān imān lokān abhyajayat rātryānapajayyam
ajayann abhijitaiva bhrātṛvyam imān lokān abhijitya rātryānapajayyaṃ jayati
PB  trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyaikaviṃśaṃ
brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ pañcadaśam acchāvākasya saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśaṃ
hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ triṇavaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya
PB  saptadaśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ekaviṃśam acchāvākasya triṇava ārbhavas
trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike
pañcadaśī rātriḥ trivṛt sandhir viśvajitātirātreṇa paśukāmo yajeta
PB  reto hi nābhānediṣṭhīyaṃ paśavo vālakhilyā yan nābhānediṣṭhīyaṃ pūrvaṃ
śasyata uttarā vālakhilyā retasas tat paśavaḥ prajāyante rūpāṇi vikaroti yad vārṣākapam
ṛtuṣu pratitiṣṭhati yad evayāmarut
PB  trivṛt ātirātreṇa brahmavarcasakāmo yajeta tejo vai trivṛt brahmavarcasaṃ
teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe tejasi brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhati pañcadaśenātirātreṇa
vīryakāmo yajetaujo vīryaṃ pañcadaśa oja eva vīryam avarundha ojasi vīrye pratitiṣṭhati
saptadaśenātirācreṇānnādyakāmo yajetānnaṃ vai saptadaśo 'nnādyam evāvarundha ekaviṃśenātirātreṇa
pratiṣṭhākāmo yajeta pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo yad atirātro bhavaty ahorātrayor eva pratitiṣṭhati
PB  jyotiṣṭomo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahaḥ sarvastomo 'tirātra uttaram
PB  tasya caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ
pavamāna ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy
ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamam athaikaviṃśam atha saptadaśam ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī
rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
PB  aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ haviṣmāṃś ca haviṣkṛc cāṅgirasāv
ahīyetā tāv āgacchetāṃ yato 'ṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tāv atapyetāṃ tāv ete sāmanī
apaśyatāṃ tābhyāṃ dvirātram atanvātāṃ tena svargaṃ lokam aitām
PB  yaḥ pauṇyo hīna iva syāt sa etena yajetāpnoti pūrveṣāṃ prahām āpnutāṃ hi tāv aṅgirasaḥ
PB  prajākāmo yajeta dvitīyaṃ hy etad yat prajāḥ
 PB  svargakāmo yajeta dvitīyād dhi lokāt paro loko 'bhiprakramyo durādho dvirātra ity āhur yad agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty ukthyam  
antaryanti yady ukthyo 'gniṣṭomam 
PB  yaj jyotir ukthyaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavati nāgniṣṭomam antaryanti nokthāni
PB  tad āhur eṣā vāva yajñasya mātrā yad agniṣṭomo yad agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam
ahar bhavati yajñasya mātrāṃ nātikrāmaty athottarasyāhna ukthebhyo 'dhi rātrim upayanti
tenokthāny anantaritāni
PB  caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavaty uttarasyāhnaś caturviṃśaty akṣarā gāyatrī prajananaṃ gāyatrī prajātyai
PB  ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate
PB  sarvastomo 'tirātro bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
PB  atha yasya jyotir ukthyaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty āyur atirātra uttaram
PB  tisraḥ pūrvasyāhno virājam atiricyante dvābhyām uttaram ahar virāja ūnam ūnātiriktaṃ vā anuprajāḥ prajāyante
PB  pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya evaṃ veda
PB  ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyate ekākinam evainam annādyasyādhyakṣaṃ karoti
 PB  etena vai citrarathaṃ kāpeyā ayājayaṃs tam ekākinam annādyasyādhyakṣam akurvaṃs tasmāc caitrarathīnām ekaḥ kṣatrapatir jāyate  
'nulamba iva dvitīyaḥ 
PB  atha yasya trivṛt pañcadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty āyur atirātra uttaram
PB  mithunābhyāṃ stomābhyām uttaram ahaḥ prajanayanti tat prajātaṃ śva ārabhante
cakre vā ete sākaṃvṛtī yat trivṛt pañcadaśau stomau yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenābhyaśnute
yatra yatra hi cakrīvatā kāmayate tat tad abhyaśnute
PB  atha yad āyur atirātro bhavati pratiṣṭhityai
PB  etena vai kapivano bhauvāyana iṣṭvārūkṣatām agacchat
PB  arūkṣo bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān etena yajate
PB  trivṛt prātaḥsavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ
pañcadaśaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ
soktham ekaviṃśaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ triṇavaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ trayastriṃśa ārbhavaś
catustriṃśo 'gniṣṭoma ekaviṃśāny ukthāni saṣoḍaśikāni ṣoḍaśaṃ prathamaṃ rātriṣāma
pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
PB  prajāpatir vā idam eka āsīt tasya vāg eva svam āsīd vāg dvitīyā sa aikṣatemām
eva vācaṃ visṛjā iyaṃ vā idaṃ sarvaṃ vibhavanty eṣyatīti sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sedaṃ
sarvaṃ vibhavanty ait sordhvodātanod yathāpāṃ dhārā santataivaṃ tasyā eti tṛtīyam
acchinat tad bhūmir abhavad abhūd iva vā idam iti tad bhūmer bhūmitvaṃ keti tṛtīyam
acchinat tad antarikṣam abhavad antar eva vā idam iti tad antarikṣasyāntarikṣatvaṃ
ho iti tṛtīyam ūrdhvam udāsyat tat dyaur abhavad adyutad iva vā iti tad divo divatvam
 PB  eṣā vāva pratyakṣaṃ vāg yaj jihvāgreṇaitad vāco vadati yad eti madhyenaitad vāco vadati yat keti sarvayaitad vāco raso 'dhyūrdhva  
udvad ati yaddho iti 
PB  yad etāni rūpāṇy anvahaṃ vyajyante mukhata eva tad vācaṃ visṛjante mukhato yajñiyaṃ karma
PB  prajāpatir vā idam ekākṣarāṃ vācaṃ satīṃ tredhā vyakarot ta ime lokā
abhavan rūkṣā anupajīvanāḥ sa aikṣata katham ime lokā loma gṛhṇīyuḥ katham upajīvanīyāḥ
syur iti sa etaṃ trirātram apaśyat tam āharat tenemān lokān anvātanot tato vā ime
lokā lomāgṛhṇaṃs tata upajīvanīyā abhavaṃs trirātrasya vā idaṃ puṣṭaṃ trirātrasyodaraṇaṃ
yad idam eṣu lokeṣv adhi
PB  gacchati paśūnāṃ bhūmānaṃ dvipadāṃ catuṣpadāṃ ya evaṃ veda
PB  prajāpatir yad vācaṃ vyasṛjata sākṣarad eveti prathamaṃ kṣeti dvitīyaṃ
reti tṛtīyaṃ yena yena vai rūpeṇa prajāpatir vācaṃ vyasṛjata tena tena rūpeṇājyāni
cārabhyante 'hāni cāpyante
 PB  tad āhur brahmavādino 'kṣarestho vai trirātra ity ekākṣarā vai vāk tryakṣaram akṣaraṃ tryakṣaraḥ puruṣaḥ sa vā enaṃ vedety āhur  
ya enaṃ puruṣasammitaṃ vedeti 
PB  etena vai devā eṣu lokeṣv ārdhnuvann etena svargaṃ lokamāyan
